misericordia tua in bonum converte;  
si via obscura fuerit,  
Christus lux vera nos illuminet;  
si cor trepidaverit,  
pax eius, quae exsuperat omnem sensum,  
custodiat corda nostra et intelligentias nostras.

Fiat voluntas tua;  
non praesumimus de viribus nostris,  
sed in tua providentia confidimus,  
ut sine iactura proximi, sine odio, sine maledictione,  
incolumes et grati perveniamus.

Pater noster, qui es in caelis,  
sanctificetur nomen tuum;  
adveniat regnum tuum;  
fiat voluntas tua,  
sicut in caelo et in terra.  
Panem nostrum quotidianum da nobis hodie;  
et dimitte nobis debita nostra,  
sicut et nos dimittimus debitoribus nostris;  
et ne nos inducas in tentationem;  
sed libera nos a malo. Amen.

Sub tuum praesidium confugimus,  
sancta Dei Genetrix;  
nostras deprecationes ne despicias in necessitatibus,  
sed a periculis cunctis libera nos semper,  
Virgo gloriosa et benedicta.

Exaudi, Domine, vocem meam,  
qua clamavi ad te;  
miserere mei et exaudi me.

Per Dominum nostrum Iesum Christum, Filium tuum,  
qui tecum vivit et regnat in unitate Spiritus Sancti,  
Deus, per omnia saecula saeculorum. Amen.

In manus tuas, Domine, commendo spiritum nostrum.  
Custodi nos sub umbra alarum tuarum;  
purifica intentiones nostras,  
confirma nos in humilitate et pace,  
et dirige omnem gressum nostrum ad laudem nominis tui. Amen.

Benedicamus Domino.  
Deo gratias.

---

## 实践卡巴拉（Practical Kabbalah）

רִבּוֹנוֹ שֶׁל עוֹלָם, אָנוּ עוֹמְדִים לְפָנֶיךָ בְּיִרְאָה וּבְרַחֲמִים, וְלֹא לְחִלּוּל הַשֵּׁם, וְלֹא לְהַכְרִיחַ רְצוֹן אָדָם, וְלֹא לְהַזִּיק לְשׁוּם בְּרִיָּה.

לְשֵׁם יִחוּד קוּדְשָׁא בְּרִיךְ הוּא וּשְׁכִינְתֵּיהּ, בִּדְחִילוּ וּרְחִימוּ, לְיַחֲדָא שֵׁם י״ה בו״ה בְּיִחוּדָא שְׁלִים, בְּשֵׁם כָּל יִשְׂרָאֵל.

יְהִי רָצוֹן מִלְּפָנֶיךָ, יְיָ אֱלֹהֵינוּ וֵאלֹהֵי אֲבוֹתֵינוּ, שֶׁתַּשְׁגִּיחַ בְּרַחֲמֶיךָ עַל כָּל הַיּוֹצְאִים לַדֶּרֶךְ, וְתַצִּילֵם מִכָּל פַּחַד וּמִכָּל סַכָּנָה, מִכָּל תַּקָּלָה וּמִכָּל מִכְשׁוֹל, וְתַהֲפֹךְ לָהֶם כָּל דָּבָר קָשֶׁה לְרַחֲמִים, וְתַגִּיעֵם לִמְחוֹז חֶפְצָם לְחַיִּים וּלְשִׂמְחָה וּלְשָׁלוֹם.

יְהִי רָצוֹן מִלְּפָנֶיךָ יְיָ אֱלֹהֵינוּ וֵאלֹהֵי אֲבוֹתֵינוּ, שֶׁתּוֹלִיכֵנוּ לְשָׁלוֹם, וְתַצְעִידֵנוּ לְשָׁלוֹם, וְתַדְרִיכֵנוּ לְשָׁלוֹם, וְתַסְמִיכֵנוּ לְשָׁלוֹם, וְתַגִּיעֵנוּ לִמְחוֹז חֶפְצֵנוּ לְחַיִּים וּלְשִׂמְחָה וּלְשָׁלוֹם. וְתַצִּילֵנוּ מִכַּף כָּל אוֹיֵב וְאוֹרֵב וְלִסְטִים וְחַיּוֹת רָעוֹת בַּדֶּרֶךְ, וּמִכָּל מִינֵי פֻּרְעָנוּיוֹת הַמִּתְרַגְּשׁוֹת לָבוֹא לָעוֹלָם. וְתִשְׁלַח בְּרָכָה בְּכָל מַעֲשֵׂה יָדֵינוּ, וְתִתְּנֵנוּ לְחֵן וּלְחֶסֶד וּלְרַחֲמִים בְּעֵינֶיךָ וּבְעֵינֵי כָל רוֹאֵינוּ. בָּרוּךְ אַתָּה יְיָ, שׁוֹמֵעַ תְּפִלָּה.

יֹשֵׁב בְּסֵתֶר עֶלְיוֹן, בְּצֵל שַׁדַּי יִתְלוֹנָן.  
אֹמַר לַיְיָ מַחְסִי וּמְצוּדָתִי, אֱלֹהַי אֶבְטַח־בּוֹ.  
כִּי הוּא יַצִּילְךָ מִפַּח יָקוּשׁ, מִדֶּבֶר הַוּוֹת.  
בְּאֶבְרָתוֹ יָסֶךְ לָךְ, וְתַחַת־כְּנָפָיו תֶּחְסֶה; צִנָּה וְסֹחֵרָה אֲמִתּוֹ.

אֶשָּׂא עֵינַי אֶל־הֶהָרִים, מֵאַיִן יָבֹא עֶזְרִי.  
עֶזְרִי מֵעִם יְיָ, עֹשֵׂה שָׁמַיִם וָאָרֶץ.  
אַל־יִתֵּן לַמּוֹט רַגְלֶךָ, אַל־יָנוּם שֹׁמְרֶךָ.  
הִנֵּה לֹא־יָנוּם וְלֹא יִישָׁן, שׁוֹמֵר יִשְׂרָאֵל.  
יְיָ שֹׁמְרֶךָ, יְיָ צִלְּךָ עַל־יַד יְמִינֶךָ.  
יוֹמָם הַשֶּׁמֶשׁ לֹא־יַכֶּכָּה, וְיָרֵחַ בַּלָּיְלָה.  
יְיָ יִשְׁמָרְךָ מִכָּל־רָע, יִשְׁמֹר אֶת־נַפְשֶׁךָ.  
יְיָ יִשְׁמָר־צֵאתְךָ וּבוֹאֶךָ, מֵעַתָּה וְעַד־עוֹלָם.

אָנָּא בְּכֹחַ גְּדֻלַּת יְמִינְךָ תַּתִּיר צְרוּרָה.  
קַבֵּל רִנַּת עַמְּךָ שַׂגְּבֵנוּ טַהֲרֵנוּ נוֹרָא.  
נָא גִבּוֹר דּוֹרְשֵׁי יִחוּדְךָ כְּבָבַת שָׁמְרֵם.  
בָּרְכֵם טַהֲרֵם רַחֲמֵי צִדְקָתְךָ תָּמִיד גָּמְלֵם.  
חֲסִין קָדוֹשׁ בְּרוֹב טוּבְךָ נַהֵל עֲדָתֶךָ.  
יָחִיד גֵּאֶה לְעַמְּךָ פְּנֵה זוֹכְרֵי קְדֻשָּׁתֶךָ.  
שַׁוְעָתֵנוּ קַבֵּל וּשְׁמַע צַעֲקָתֵנוּ יוֹדֵעַ תַּעֲלוּמוֹת.  
בָּרוּךְ שֵׁם כְּבוֹד מַלְכוּתוֹ לְעוֹלָם וָעֶד.

יְהִי רָצוֹן מִלְּפָנֶיךָ יְיָ אֱלֹהֵי יִשְׂרָאֵל, שֶׁיִּהְיֶה הַמַּסָּע הַזֶּה לְטוֹבָה וְלִבְרָכָה, בְּלִי עָוֹן וּבְלִי חִלּוּל הַשֵּׁם, בְּלִי הֶזֵּק לְאָדָם וּבְלִי כְּפִיָּה עַל רְצוֹן זוּלָתִי. פְּתַח שַׁעֲרֵי רַחֲמִים, וּשְׁמֹר צֵאתֵנוּ וּבוֹאֵנוּ, וְהָפֵךְ כָּל סַכָּנָה לְהַצָּלָה, וְכָל פַּחַד לְבִטָּחוֹן, וְכָל עִכּוּב לְדֶרֶךְ יְשָׁרָה וְשָׁלוֹם.

חָטָאנוּ עָוִינוּ פָּשַׁעְנוּ לְפָנֶיךָ; יְיָ, סְלַח נָא לַעֲוֹן עֲבָדֶיךָ וַאֲמָהוֹתֶיךָ, וְטַהֵר לִבֵּנוּ לְעָבְדְּךָ בֶּאֱמֶת. אַל תְּהִי תְּפִלָּתֵנוּ לְגַאֲוָה וְלֹא לְמִכְשׁוֹל, אֶלָּא לְרַחֲמִים וּלְשָׁלוֹם.

יִהְיוּ לְרָצוֹן אִמְרֵי־פִינוּ וְהֶגְיוֹן לִבֵּנוּ לְפָנֶיךָ, יְיָ צוּרֵנוּ וְגֹאֲלֵנוּ.  
בָּרוּךְ שֵׁם כְּבוֹד מַלְכוּתוֹ לְעוֹלָם וָעֶד.

---

## נוסח שאמי

לְשֵׁם יִחוּד קֻדְשָׁא בְּרִיךְ הוּא וּשְׁכִינְתֵּיהּ, בִּדְחִילוּ וּרְחִימוּ, לְיַחֵד שֵׁם י״ה בְּו״ה בְּיִחוּדָא שְׁלִים, בְּשֵׁם כָּל יִשְׂרָאֵל.

רִבּוֹנוֹ שֶׁל עוֹלָם, יְהִי רָצוֹן מִלְּפָנֶיךָ יי אֱלֹהֵינוּ וֵאלֹהֵי אֲבוֹתֵינוּ, שֶׁתְּקַבֵּל בְּרַחֲמִים וּבְרָצוֹן תְּפִלָּתֵנוּ, וְתִשְׁמְרֵנוּ בְּצֵאתֵנוּ וּבְבוֹאֵנוּ, וְתַדְרִיכֵנוּ בְּדֶרֶךְ יְשָׁרָה וּבְשָׁלוֹם.

שִׁיר לַמַּעֲלוֹת.  
אֶשָּׂא עֵינַי אֶל הֶהָרִים מֵאַיִן יָבֹא עֶזְרִי.  
עֶזְרִי מֵעִם יי עֹשֵׂה שָׁמַיִם וָאָרֶץ.  
אַל יִתֵּן לַמּוֹט רַגְלֶךָ אַל יָנוּם שֹׁמְרֶךָ.  
הִנֵּה לֹא יָנוּם וְלֹא יִישָׁן שׁוֹמֵר יִשְׂרָאֵל.  
יי שֹׁמְרֶךָ יי צִלְּךָ עַל יַד יְמִינֶךָ.  
יוֹמָם הַשֶּׁמֶשׁ לֹא יַכֶּכָּה וְיָרֵחַ בַּלָּיְלָה.  
יי יִשְׁמָרְךָ מִכָּל רָע יִשְׁמֹר אֶת נַפְשֶׁךָ.  
יי יִשְׁמָר צֵאתְךָ וּבוֹאֶךָ מֵעַתָּה וְעַד עוֹלָם.

יֹשֵׁב בְּסֵתֶר עֶלְיוֹן, בְּצֵל שַׁדַּי יִתְלוֹנָן.  
אֹמַר לַיי מַחְסִי וּמְצוּדָתִי, אֱלֹהַי אֶבְטַח בּוֹ.  
כִּי הוּא יַצִּילְךָ מִפַּח יָקוּשׁ, מִדֶּבֶר הַוּוֹת.  
בְּאֶבְרָתוֹ יָסֶךְ לָךְ, וְתַחַת כְּנָפָיו תֶּחְסֶה, צִנָּה וְסֹחֵרָה אֲמִתּוֹ.

יְהִי רָצוֹן מִלְּפָנֶיךָ יי אֱלֹהֵינוּ וֵאלֹהֵי אֲבוֹתֵינוּ, שֶׁתּוֹלִיכֵנוּ לְשָׁלוֹם וְתַצְעִידֵנוּ לְשָׁלוֹם וְתַדְרִיכֵנוּ לְשָׁלוֹם, וְתַגִּיעֵנוּ לִמְחוֹז חֶפְצֵנוּ לְחַיִּים וּלְשִׂמְחָה וּלְשָׁלוֹם. וְתַצִּילֵנוּ מִכַּף כָּל אוֹיֵב וְאוֹרֵב וְלִסְטִים וְחַיּוֹת רָעוֹת בַּדֶּרֶךְ, וּמִכָּל מִינֵי פֻּרְעָנִיּוֹת הַמִּתְרַגְּשׁוֹת לָבוֹא לָעוֹלָם. וְתִשְׁלַח בְּרָכָה בְּמַעֲשֵׂה יָדֵינוּ, וְתִתְּנֵנוּ לְחֵן וּלְחֶסֶד וּלְרַחֲמִים בְּעֵינֶיךָ וּבְעֵינֵי כָל רֹאֵינוּ, וְתִשְׁמַע קוֹל תַּחֲנוּנֵינוּ, כִּי אֵל שׁוֹמֵעַ תְּפִלָּה וְתַחֲנוּן אָתָּה.

הַשְׁכִּיבֵנוּ יי אֱלֹהֵינוּ לְשָׁלוֹם, וְהַעֲמִידֵנוּ מַלְכֵּנוּ לְחַיִּים טוֹבִים וּלְשָׁלוֹם, וּפְרוֹשׂ עָלֵינוּ סֻכַּת שְׁלוֹמֶךָ, וְתַקְּנֵנוּ בְּעֵצָה טוֹבָה מִלְּפָנֶיךָ, וְהוֹשִׁיעֵנוּ לְמַעַן שְׁמֶךָ. וְהָגֵן בַּעֲדֵנוּ, וְהָסֵר מֵעָלֵינוּ אוֹיֵב דֶּבֶר וְחֶרֶב וְרָעָב וְיָגוֹן, וְהָסֵר שָׂטָן מִלְּפָנֵינוּ וּמֵאַחֲרֵינוּ, וּבְצֵל כְּנָפֶיךָ תַּסְתִּירֵנוּ.

אָנָּא יי, שׁוֹמֵר יִשְׂרָאֵל, שְׁמֹר אֶת כָּל הַיּוֹצְאִים לַדֶּרֶךְ לְטוֹבָה; הָסֵר מִכְשׁוֹל מִלִּפְנֵיהֶם, הָפֵךְ לָהֶם סַכָּנָה לְהַצָּלָה, פַּחַד לְבִטָּחוֹן, וְצָרָה לְרַחֲמִים. יְהִי מַסָּעָם בְּנַחַת וּבְסֵדֶר, בְּלִי פֶּגַע וּבְלִי תַּקָּלָה, וְיַגִּיעוּ לִמְקוֹם חֶפְצָם בְּשָׁלוֹם, בְּטוֹבָה וּבְרַחֲמִים.

יִשָּׂא יי פָּנָיו אֵלֵינוּ וְיָשֵׂם לָנוּ שָׁלוֹם.  
יִהְיוּ לְרָצוֹן אִמְרֵי פִי וְהֶגְיוֹן לִבִּי לְפָנֶיךָ, יי צוּרִי וְגֹאֲלִי.

לְךָ יי הַגְּדֻלָּה וְהַגְּבוּרָה וְהַתִּפְאֶרֶת וְהַנֵּצַח וְהַהוֹד, כִּי כֹל בַּשָּׁמַיִם וּבָאָרֶץ; לְךָ יי הַמַּמְלָכָה וְהַמִּתְנַשֵּׂא לְכֹל לְרֹאשׁ. אֵין לָנוּ מֶלֶךְ אֶלָּא אָתָּה, וּמִלְּפָנֶיךָ לְבַדְּךָ אָנוּ מְבַקְּשִׁים רַחֲמִים. עֹשֶׂה שָׁלוֹם בִּמְרוֹמָיו, הוּא בְרַחֲמָיו יַעֲשֶׂה שָׁלוֹם עָלֵינוּ וְעַל כָּל יִשְׂרָאֵל, וְאִמְרוּ אָמֵן.

---

## נוסח רומניוטים

רִבּוֹנוֹ שֶׁל עוֹלָם, אֱלֹהֵי אַבְרָהָם אֱלֹהֵי יִצְחָק וֵאלֹהֵי יַעֲקֹב, הָאֵל הַגָּדוֹל הַגִּבּוֹר וְהַנּוֹרָא, יִהְיוּ דְבָרֵינוּ לְרָצוֹן לְפָנֶיךָ.

יִהְיוּ לְרָצוֹן אִמְרֵי פִינוּ וְהֶגְיוֹן לִבֵּנוּ לְפָנֶיךָ, יְיָ צוּרֵנוּ וְגֹאֲלֵנוּ.

שִׁיר לַמַּעֲלוֹת.  
אֶשָּׂא עֵינַי אֶל הֶהָרִים מֵאַיִן יָבֹא עֶזְרִי.  
עֶזְרִי מֵעִם יְיָ עֹשֵׂה שָׁמַיִם וָאָרֶץ.  
אַל יִתֵּן לַמּוֹט רַגְלֶךָ אַל יָנוּם שֹׁמְרֶךָ.  
הִנֵּה לֹא יָנוּם וְלֹא יִישָׁן שׁוֹמֵר יִשְׂרָאֵל.  
יְיָ שֹׁמְרֶךָ יְיָ צִלְּךָ עַל יַד יְמִינֶךָ.  
יוֹמָם הַשֶּׁמֶשׁ לֹא יַכֶּכָּה וְיָרֵחַ בַּלָּיְלָה.  
יְיָ יִשְׁמָרְךָ מִכָּל רָע יִשְׁמֹר אֶת נַפְשֶׁךָ.  
יְיָ יִשְׁמָר צֵאתְךָ וּבוֹאֶךָ מֵעַתָּה וְעַד עוֹלָם.

יֹשֵׁב בְּסֵתֶר עֶלְיוֹן בְּצֵל שַׁדַּי יִתְלוֹנָן.  
אֹמַר לַיְיָ מַחְסִי וּמְצוּדָתִי אֱלֹהַי אֶבְטַח בּוֹ.  
כִּי הוּא יַצִּילְךָ מִפַּח יָקוּשׁ מִדֶּבֶר הַוּוֹת.  
בְּאֶבְרָתוֹ יָסֶךְ לָךְ וְתַחַת כְּנָפָיו תֶּחְסֶה צִנָּה וְסֹחֵרָה אֲמִתּוֹ.  
לֹא תִירָא מִפַּחַד לָיְלָה מֵחֵץ יָעוּף יוֹמָם.  
לֹא תְאֻנֶּה אֵלֶיךָ רָעָה וְנֶגַע לֹא יִקְרַב בְּאָהֳלֶךָ.  
כִּי מַלְאָכָיו יְצַוֶּה לָּךְ לִשְׁמָרְךָ בְּכָל דְּרָכֶיךָ.  
יִקְרָאֵנִי וְאֶעֱנֵהוּ עִמּוֹ אָנֹכִי בְצָרָה אֲחַלְּצֵהוּ וַאֲכַבְּדֵהוּ.  
אֹרֶךְ יָמִים אַשְׂבִּיעֵהוּ וְאַרְאֵהוּ בִּישׁוּעָתִי.

מִי שֶׁבֵּרַךְ אֲבוֹתֵינוּ אַבְרָהָם יִצְחָק וְיַעֲקֹב, מֹשֶׁה וְאַהֲרֹן דָּוִד וּשְׁלֹמֹה, הוּא יְבָרֵךְ אֶת כָּל הַיּוֹצְאִים לַדֶּרֶךְ לְשָׁלוֹם, וְיִשְׁמְרֵם בְּצֵאתָם וּבְבוֹאָם, וְיַצִּילֵם מִכָּל צָרָה וְצוּקָה, מִכָּל מִכְשׁוֹל וּפֶגַע, מִכָּל אוֹיֵב וְאוֹרֵב וְלִסְטִים, וּמִכָּל פֻּרְעָנוּת הַבָּאָה לָעוֹלָם.  
הַקָּדוֹשׁ בָּרוּךְ הוּא יַהֲפֹךְ לָנוּ מִדַּת הַדִּין לְמִדַּת רַחֲמִים, וְיִתֵּן לָנוּ דֶּרֶךְ יְשָׁרָה וּמְיֻשֶּׁרֶת, מַעֲבָר בְּלִי פַחַד וּבְלִי מוֹרָא, וְיַגִּיעֵנוּ לִמְחוֹז חֶפְצֵנוּ לְחַיִּים וּלְשִׂמְחָה וּלְשָׁלוֹם.  
וְאֵין בַּקָּשָׁתֵנוּ לְהַזִּיק לְאָדָם, וְלֹא לִגְזֹל טוֹבָה מִבְּרִיּוֹתֶיךָ, אֶלָּא לְהָסִיר מִכְשׁוֹל מִדַּרְכֵּנוּ וּלְהוֹלִיכֵנוּ בְּרַחֲמֶיךָ.

יְהִי רָצוֹן מִלְּפָנֶיךָ יְיָ אֱלֹהֵינוּ וֵאלֹהֵי אֲבוֹתֵינוּ, שֶׁתּוֹלִיכֵנוּ לְשָׁלוֹם וְתַצְעִידֵנוּ לְשָׁלוֹם וְתַדְרִיכֵנוּ לְשָׁלוֹם, וְתַגִּיעֵנוּ לִמְחוֹז חֶפְצֵנוּ לְחַיִּים וּלְשִׂמְחָה וּלְשָׁלוֹם.  
וְתַצִּילֵנוּ מִכַּף כָּל אוֹיֵב וְאוֹרֵב וְלִסְטִים וְחַיּוֹת רָעוֹת בַּדֶּרֶךְ, וּמִכָּל מִינֵי פֻּרְעָנוּת הַמִּתְרַגְּשׁוֹת לָבוֹא לָעוֹלָם.  
וְתִשְׁלַח בְּרָכָה בְּכָל מַעֲשֵׂה יָדֵינוּ, וְתִתְּנֵנוּ לְחֵן וּלְחֶסֶד וּלְרַחֲמִים בְּעֵינֶיךָ וּבְעֵינֵי כָל רֹאֵינוּ, וְתִשְׁמַע קוֹל תַּחֲנוּנֵינוּ, כִּי אֵל שׁוֹמֵעַ תְּפִלָּה וְתַחֲנוּן אָתָּה.

הַשְׁכִּיבֵנוּ יְיָ אֱלֹהֵינוּ לְשָׁלוֹם, וְהַעֲמִידֵנוּ מַלְכֵּנוּ לְחַיִּים, וּפְרֹשׂ עָלֵינוּ סֻכַּת שְׁלוֹמֶךָ, וְתַקְּנֵנוּ בְּעֵצָה טוֹבָה מִלְּפָנֶיךָ, וְהוֹשִׁיעֵנוּ לְמַעַן שְׁמֶךָ.  
וְהָגֵן בַּעֲדֵנוּ, וְהָסֵר מֵעָלֵינוּ אוֹיֵב דֶּבֶר וְחֶרֶב וְרָעָב וְיָגוֹן, וְהָסֵר שָׂטָן מִלְּפָנֵינוּ וּמֵאַחֲרֵינוּ, וּבְצֵל כְּנָפֶיךָ תַּסְתִּירֵנוּ.

זָכְרֵנוּ לְחַיִּים, מֶלֶךְ חָפֵץ בַּחַיִּים, וְכָתְבֵנוּ בְּסֵפֶר הַחַיִּים לְמַעַנְךָ אֱלֹהִים חַיִּים.  
שָׁמְרֵנוּ כְּאִישׁוֹן בַּת עָיִן, בְּצִלְּךָ נַעֲבֹר דֶּרֶךְ, וּבְשָׁלוֹם נָבוֹא אֶל שַׁעַרֵינוּ.

עָזְרֵנוּ אֱלֹהֵי יִשְׁעֵנוּ עַל דְּבַר כְּבוֹד שְׁמֶךָ, וְהַצִּילֵנוּ וְכַפֵּר עַל חַטֹּאתֵינוּ לְמַעַן שְׁמֶךָ.  
יִהְיוּ לְרָצוֹן אִמְרֵי פִינוּ וְהֶגְיוֹן לִבֵּנוּ לְפָנֶיךָ, יְיָ צוּרֵנוּ וְגֹאֲלֵנוּ.

וּבִתְחִנָּה זוֹ אֵין אָנוּ קוֹבְעִים בְּרָכָה חֲדָשָׁה וְאֵין אָנוּ אוֹמְרִים דָּבָר שֶׁבִּקְדֻשָּׁה בְּלֹא עֲשָׂרָה; אֶלָּא רַחֲמִים אָנוּ מְבַקְּשִׁים מִלְּפָנֶיךָ כְּמִנְהַג קְהִלּוֹת רוֹמַנְיָא, בְּלֵב נִשְׁבָּר וּבְרוּחַ נְכוֹנָה.  
שׁוֹמֵר יִשְׂרָאֵל, שְׁמֹר שְׁאֵרִית יִשְׂרָאֵל, וְאַל יֹאבַד יִשְׂרָאֵל הָאוֹמְרִים: שְׁמַע יִשְׂרָאֵל, יְיָ אֱלֹהֵינוּ, יְיָ אֶחָד.  
אָמֵן.

---

## 圣公会高教派

In the Name of the Father, and of the Son, and of the Holy Ghost. Amen.

O Lord, open thou our lips.  
And our mouth shall shew forth thy praise.

O God, make speed to save us.  
O Lord, make haste to help us.

Glory be to the Father, and to the Son, and to the Holy Ghost;  
As it was in the beginning, is now, and ever shall be, world without end. Amen.

Kyrie eleison.  
Christe eleison.  
Kyrie eleison.

Almighty and most merciful Father;  
We have erred, and strayed from thy ways like lost sheep.  
We have followed too much the devices and desires of our own hearts.  
We have offended against thy holy laws.  
We have left undone those things which we ought to have done;  
And we have done those things which we ought not to have done;  
And there is no health in us.  
But thou, O Lord, have mercy upon us, miserable offenders.  
Spare thou them, O God, which confess their faults.  
Restore thou them that are penitent;  
According to thy promises declared unto mankind in Christ Jesu our Lord.  
And grant, O most merciful Father, for his sake;  
That we may hereafter live a godly, righteous, and sober life,  
To the glory of thy holy Name. Amen.

Our Father, which art in heaven,  
Hallowed be thy Name.  
Thy kingdom come.  
Thy will be done in earth, As it is in heaven.  
Give us this day our daily bread.  
And forgive us our trespasses,  
As we forgive them that trespass against us.  
And lead us not into temptation;  
But deliver us from evil. Amen.

I will lift up mine eyes unto the hills:  
from whence cometh my help.  
My help cometh even from the Lord:  
who hath made heaven and earth.  
He will not suffer thy foot to be moved:  
and he that keepeth thee will not sleep.  
Behold, he that keepeth Israel:  
shall neither slumber nor sleep.  
The Lord himself is thy keeper:  
the Lord is thy defence upon thy right hand.  
So that the sun shall not burn thee by day:  
neither the moon by night.  
The Lord shall preserve thee from all evil:  
yea, it is even he that shall keep thy soul.  
The Lord shall preserve thy going out, and thy coming in:  
from this time forth for evermore.

O Lord, shew thy mercy upon us.  
And grant us thy salvation.

O Lord, save the King.  
And mercifully hear us when we call upon thee.

Endue thy Ministers with righteousness.  
And make thy chosen people joyful.

O Lord, save thy people.  
And bless thine inheritance.

Give peace in our time, O Lord.  
Because there is none other that fighteth for us, but only thou, O God.

O God, make clean our hearts within us.  
And take not thy Holy Spirit from us.

O God, the Creator and Preserver of all mankind,  
we humbly beseech thee for all who go forth upon their way;  
that thou wouldest guide their steps, guard them from every peril,  
turn aside all occasions of harm, and bring them in safety to their journey’s end.  
In sudden danger, be thou their help; in fear, their comfort;  
in confusion, their light; and in every change of the road, their steadfast defence.  
Grant that all their going out and coming in may be ordered by thy providence,  
through Jesus Christ our Lord. Amen.

O Lord, our heavenly Father, Almighty and everlasting God,  
who hast safely brought us to the beginning of this day;  
Defend us in the same with thy mighty power;  
and grant that this day we fall into no sin,  
neither run into any kind of danger;  
but that all our doings may be ordered by thy governance,  
to do always that is righteous in thy sight;  
through Jesus Christ our Lord. Amen.

Lighten our darkness, we beseech thee, O Lord;  
and by thy great mercy defend us from all perils and dangers of this night;  
for the love of thy only Son, our Saviour, Jesus Christ. Amen.

Pater noster, qui es in caelis,  
sanctificetur nomen tuum;  
adveniat regnum tuum;  
fiat voluntas tua, sicut in caelo et in terra.  
Panem nostrum quotidianum da nobis hodie;  
et dimitte nobis debita nostra,  
sicut et nos dimittimus debitoribus nostris;  
et ne nos inducas in tentationem;  
sed libera nos a malo. Amen.

Gloria Patri, et Filio, et Spiritui Sancto:  
sicut erat in principio, et nunc, et semper,  
et in saecula saeculorum. Amen.

The grace of our Lord Jesus Christ, and the love of God,  
and the fellowship of the Holy Ghost, be with us all evermore. Amen.

---

## 黑人教会传统

Father God, in the name of Jesus, we come before You.

Leader:  
Lord, we thank You for waking us up, clothing us in our right mind, and keeping us by Your mercy.

People:  
Amen. Thank You, Lord.

Leader:  
We come not in our own strength, but leaning on Your everlasting arms.  
Search us, Lord; forgive us, cleanse us, and make our hearts right before You.

People:  
Lord, have mercy.

Leader:  
For this journey, for safe passage, for every road, station, airport, harbor, vehicle, driver, pilot, worker, and traveler, and for all who are standing in need of prayer, we lift our hearts to You.

Scripture:  
He that dwelleth in the secret place of the most High  
shall abide under the shadow of the Almighty.  
I will say of the LORD, He is my refuge and my fortress:  
my God; in him will I trust.  
Surely he shall deliver thee from the snare of the fowler,  
and from the noisome pestilence.  
He shall cover thee with his feathers,  
and under his wings shalt thou trust:  
his truth shall be thy shield and buckler.

People:  
Amen. Cover us, Lord.

Spiritual:  
There is a balm in Gilead,  
To make the wounded whole;  
There is a balm in Gilead,  
To heal the sin-sick soul.

Leader:  
Lord, where there is danger, cover with Your hand.  
Where there is confusion, give wisdom.  
Where there is delay, give patience.  
Where there is fear, speak peace.  
Where there is a hidden hazard, make a way of escape.  
Where the path is narrow, guide every step.  
Where trouble rises up, turn it aside by Your mercy.  
Bring this journey through without harm, without calamity, and without despair.  
Let every danger be met by Your protection, every difficulty be answered by Your grace, and every traveler arrive in peace.

Scripture:  
The LORD shall preserve thy going out and thy coming in  
from this time forth, and even for evermore.

People:  
Yes, Lord.

Leader:  
We put on the whole armour of God.  
We stand having our loins girt about with truth,  
and having on the breastplate of righteousness;  
our feet shod with the preparation of the gospel of peace;  
above all, taking the shield of faith,  
the helmet of salvation,  
and the sword of the Spirit, which is the word of God.  
Let the peace of Christ ride before, beside, and behind this journey.  
Let angels minister according to Your holy will.  
Let wisdom govern every decision, and let mercy meet every mile.

People:  
Lord, lead the way.

Leader:  
For the living, keep them.  
For the weary, strengthen them.  
For the anxious, quiet their hearts.  
For families waiting, give assurance.  
For strangers on the way, let kindness be near.  
For the whole community, teach us to pray, to watch, to care, and to give thanks.

Scripture:  
The LORD is my light and my salvation; whom shall I fear?  
the LORD is the strength of my life; of whom shall I be afraid?

People:  
Amen.

Leader:  
Now, Lord, teach us to pray:

All:  
Our Father which art in heaven,  
Hallowed be thy name.  
Thy kingdom come.  
Thy will be done in earth, as it is in heaven.  
Give us this day our daily bread.  
And forgive us our debts, as we forgive our debtors.  
And lead us not into temptation, but deliver us from evil:  
For thine is the kingdom, and the power, and the glory, for ever.  
Amen.

Leader:  
Father God, receive this prayer as praise, trust, and humble dependence, not as a bargain and not for show.  
Keep our hearts rooted in Scripture, mercy, and love.  
Let the Father be glorified, let the Son be honored, and let the Holy Spirit guide and comfort.  
We seal this prayer in faith, not by might, nor by power, but by Your Spirit.  
In Jesus’ name.

People:  
Amen. Amen. Amen.

---

## 东方亚述教会

Bshēm Abbā w-Brōnā w-Rūḥā d-Qudshā, ḥad Alāhā sharīrā. Āmēn.

Qadīshā Alāhā,  
Qadīshā ḥayltānā,  
Qadīshā lā māyōtā,  
etraḥam ‘layn.

Qadīshā Alāhā,  
Qadīshā ḥayltānā,  
Qadīshā lā māyōtā,  
etraḥam ‘layn.

Qadīshā Alāhā,  
Qadīshā ḥayltānā,  
Qadīshā lā māyōtā,  
etraḥam ‘layn.

Shubḥā l-Abā w-la-Brōnā w-la-Rūḥā d-Qudshā,  
min ‘ālam w-‘damā l-‘ālam. Āmēn.

Abun d-ba-shmayyā,  
nethqaddash shmakh;  
tite malkuthakh;  
nehwe sebyanakh,  
aykanna d-ba-shmayyā ap b-ar‘a.  
Haw lan laḥma d-sunqanan yawmana;  
washbuq lan ḥawbayn wa-khṭahayn,  
aykana d-af ḥnan shbaqn l-ḥayyabayn;  
wela ta‘lan l-nesyuna,  
ella paṣṣan min bisha.  
Meṭul dilakh hi malkutha w-ḥayla w-teshbuḥta  
l-‘ālam ‘ālmin. Āmēn.

Marya Alāhā,  
ḥus ‘alayn b-raḥmayk,  
daqqlen ḥawbayn wa-khṭahayn,  
w-dakkā lebbān men kul ḥushābā bīshā;  
qabbel ba‘utan b-ṣebyānā dīlakh,  
lā b-ṣebyānā dīlan.

Marya,  
‘al urḥā w-mardithā d-‘abdāyk,  
haw shaynā, ḥnānā, ḥaylā, w-nuhrā;  
dabbarn b-shlamā,  
naṭar l-raglayn men taqaltā,  
w-paṣṣan men bīshā, men nesyūnā,  
men kul qaṭrā w-men kul me’raz d-metkhazē w-lā metkhazē.  
Mā d-qāyem qaṭrā, haw purqānā;  
mā d-mettaḥzē ḥashā, haw ‘udrānā;  
w-āwbel l-‘abdāyk b-shaynā ‘damā l-dukthā d-metba‘yā.

Lakhu Mara d-kol modēnan,  
w-lakh Yeshu Mshiḥa mshabḥīnan,  
d-ant hu mnaḥmana d-pagrayn,  
w-ant hu paroqa d-nafshātan.

Marya,  
dkar l-ṭabta l-kulhon ḥayyē,  
w-‘bed raḥme ‘al aylen d-napqin b-urḥātā,  
‘al aylen d-yātbīn b-yammē, b-ar‘ā, w-ba-awwīrā,  
w-‘al aylen d-metḥashḥīn l-‘udrānā w-shaynā;  
ṭalel ‘layhon b-sitra d-raḥmayk sagī’ē.

Shubḥā l-Abā w-la-Brōnā w-la-Rūḥā d-Qudshā,  
min ‘ālam w-‘damā l-‘ālam. Āmēn.

B-raḥmayk, Marya, w-b-ṣebyānā d-qudshā dīlakh,  
la hwā b-ḥaylā dīlan, ellā b-ṭaybūthā dīlakh,  
netnaṭar w-netdabar b-shaynā.  
Shubḥā w-tawdīthā lakh, Abā w-Brōnā w-Rūḥā d-Qudshā,  
ḥad Alāhā sharīrā, l-‘ālam ‘ālmin. Āmēn.

Bshēm Abbā w-Brōnā w-Rūḥā d-Qudshā,  
ḥad Alāhā sharīrā. Āmēn.

## 天主教灵恩复兴运动

In nomine Patris, et Filii, et Spiritus Sancti. Amen.

Veni, Sancte Spiritus.  
Veni per Mariam.  
Veni, Creator Spiritus,  
mentes tuorum visita,  
imple superna gratia  
quae tu creasti pectora.

Κύριος Ἰησοῦς Χριστός.  
Ἰησοῦς Χριστός Κύριος εἰς δόξαν Θεοῦ Πατρός.

Domine Iesu Christe, Fili Dei vivi, iter hoc coram te ponimus:  
ut euntes in pace ambulent, a periculis custodiantur,  
in viis, in vehiculis, in aquis, in aere et in omni loco protegantur,  
et, te duce, salvi ac tranquilli ad locum destinatum perveniant.

Renuntio Satanae, et omnibus operibus eius, et omnibus pompis eius.  
Renuntio omni peccato, omni mendacio, omni vinculo, omni timori,  
omni odio, omni spiritui qui non confitetur Iesum Christum in carne venisse.

Pater noster, qui es in caelis,  
sanctificetur nomen tuum.  
Adveniat regnum tuum.  
Fiat voluntas tua, sicut in caelo et in terra.  
Panem nostrum quotidianum da nobis hodie,  
et dimitte nobis debita nostra,  
sicut et nos dimittimus debitoribus nostris.  
Et ne nos inducas in tentationem,  
sed libera nos a malo. Amen.

Domine Iesu Christe, per sanctam crucem tuam,  
per pretiosum sanguinem tuum, per resurrectionem tuam,  
libera famulos tuos ab omni malo, ab insidiis visibilibus et invisibilibus,  
ab infortunio, confusione, negligentia, timore et omni via periculosa.  
Mitte Spiritum Sanctum tuum super hoc iter.  
Ubi est timor, sit pax tua.  
Ubi est obscuritas, sit lux tua.  
Ubi est periculum, sit custodia tua.  
Ubi est perturbatio, sit sapientia et temperantia tua.  
Ubi est angustia, sit providentia tua.  
Converte pericula in viam salutis,  
et omnia dispone secundum misericordiam tuam,  
ut pax Christi corda custodiat.

Veni, Sancte Spiritus, reple tuorum corda fidelium,  
et tui amoris in eis ignem accende.

Sancte Michael Archangele,  
defende nos in proelio;  
contra nequitiam et insidias diaboli esto praesidium.  
Imperet illi Deus, supplices deprecamur;  
tuque, Princeps militiae caelestis,  
Satanam aliosque spiritus malignos,  
qui ad perditionem animarum pervagantur in mundo,  
divina virtute in infernum detrude. Amen.

Dominus Iesus Christus sit ante euntes ad ducendum,  
post eos ad custodiendum,  
super eos ad benedicendum,  
iuxta eos ad defendendum,  
in corde eorum ad pacificandum.  
Benedicat eos omnipotens Deus,  
Pater, et Filius, et Spiritus Sanctus. Amen.

Gloria Patri, et Filio, et Spiritui Sancto.  
Sicut erat in principio, et nunc, et semper,  
et in saecula saeculorum. Amen.

Sub tuum praesidium confugimus, sancta Dei Genitrix;  
nostras deprecationes ne despicias in necessitatibus,  
sed a periculis cunctis libera nos semper,  
Virgo gloriosa et benedicta.

In communione sanctae Ecclesiae,  
non in praesumptione sed in fide,  
non vi nostra sed gratia tua, Domine,  
omnia tibi committimus.  
Da prudentiam, sobrietatem, patientiam et obedientiam bono consilio;  
custodi corpus et animam;  
et fiat voluntas tua in pace.

In nomine Patris, et Filii, et Spiritus Sancti. Amen.

---

## 凯尔特祝福派

An ainm an Athar, agus a' Mhic, agus an Spioraid Naoimh. Amen.

A Thrianaid Naoimh,  
A Dhè nan dùl,  
A Chrìosd nan gràs,  
A Spioraid Naoimh nam beannachd,  
bi maille rinn air an turas seo.

Dia romhainn,  
Dia nar dèidh,  
Dia os ar cionn,  
Dia fodhainn,  
Dia air ar làimh dheis,  
Dia air ar làimh chlì,  
Dia mun cuairt oirnn,  
Dia nar cridhe.

Beannaich an rathad,  
beannaich an t-slighe,  
beannaich gach ceum agus gach car,  
beannaich ar dol a-mach agus ar teachd a-steach.

Sìth Chrìosd air an turas,  
gràs Chrìosd anns an t-slighe,  
neart Chrìosd fo ar casan,  
solas Chrìosd os ar cionn.

Cuir air falbh gach olc,  
gach eagal,  
gach cunnart,  
gach tubaist,  
gach droch-rùn,  
o ar slighe agus o ar cridhe.

Thoir dhuinn rathad rèidh,  
inntinn shocair,  
sùil shoilleir,  
agus làmh dhìonach;  
gun chron, gun chall, gun sgrios,  
ach gach teanntachd air a tionndadh gu tròcair,  
agus ruigsinn shàbhailte le sìth.

An Trianaid os ar cionn,  
An Trianaid fodhainn,  
An Trianaid romhainn,  
An Trianaid nar dèidh,  
An Trianaid mun cuairt oirnn,  
An Trianaid nar cridhe.

Glòir don Athair,  
agus don Mhac,  
agus don Spiorad Naomh;  
mar a bha, mar a tha,  
agus mar a bhitheas,  
gu saoghal nan saoghal. Amen.

## 基督教科学派

Our Father which art in heaven,  
Our Father-Mother God, all-harmonious,

Let every motive be purified in divine Love; let thought be meek, watchful, and obedient to Truth.  
Let no fear, haste, resentment, or personal will govern this journey; let Mind alone guide, order, and protect.

Hallowed be Thy name.  
Adorable One.

Thy kingdom come.  
Thy kingdom is come; Thou art ever-present.

Thy will be done in earth, as it is in heaven.  
Enable us to know,—as in heaven, so on earth,—God is omnipotent, supreme.

Give us this day our daily bread;  
Give us grace for to-day; feed the famished affections;

And forgive us our debts, as we forgive our debtors.  
And Love is reflected in love;

And lead us not into temptation, but deliver us from evil;  
And God leadeth us not into temptation, but delivereth us from sin, disease, and death.

For Thine is the kingdom, and the power, and the glory, forever.  
For God is infinite, all-power, all Life, Truth, Love, over all, and All.

“He shall give his angels charge over thee, to keep thee in all thy ways.”  
Under the government of divine Mind, the way is not ruled by accident, confusion, danger, or fear.  
Divine Principle maintains order; divine Love embraces each step; divine Life is present and uninterrupted.

There is no life, truth, intelligence, nor substance in matter.  
All is infinite Mind and its infinite manifestation, for God is All-in-all.  
Spirit is immortal Truth; matter is mortal error.  
Spirit is the real and eternal; matter is the unreal and temporal.  
Spirit is God, and man is His image and likeness.  
Therefore man is not material; he is spiritual.

Concerning safe and smooth travel, let thought be governed by divine Mind, not by fear, personal will, resentment, diagnosis, or material belief.  
Let motive and act be held in Truth, Life, and Love.  
Let the whole journey be spiritually known as under divine Principle, embraced by divine Love, and ordered by infinite Mind.  
Let every seeming risk be met by the understanding that God is ever-present good; let every seeming danger yield to the harmony of Truth; let arrival be peaceful, orderly, and complete.

Thy kingdom come; let the reign of divine Truth, Life, and Love be established in this journey.  
God is Spirit: and they that worship him must worship him in spirit and in truth.  
God is Love; and Love is reflected in love.

May this prayer remain wholly in divine Love: controlling no will, accusing no person, fearing no material power, and honoring Spirit as the only true reality.  
May thought be kept alert, pure, merciful, and free, under infinite Mind, divine Principle, Life, Truth, and Love.  
Amen.

---

## 天主教 Marian Apparition 派

In nomine Patris, et Filii, et Spiritus Sancti. Amen.

Domine Deus, Pater misericordiarum, in conspectu tuo et sub intercessione Beatae Mariae Virginis, intentionem hanc pono: pro itinere pacato, tuto et recte ordinato; ut euntes et redeuntes a periculis animae et corporis custodias, difficultates in bonum convertas, et ad destinatum locum in pace pervenire concedas.

Credo in Deum, Patrem omnipotentem, Creatorem caeli et terrae;  
et in Iesum Christum, Filium eius unicum, Dominum nostrum;  
qui conceptus est de Spiritu Sancto, natus ex Maria Virgine;  
passus sub Pontio Pilato, crucifixus, mortuus, et sepultus;  
descendit ad inferos; tertia die resurrexit a mortuis;  
ascendit ad caelos, sedet ad dexteram Dei Patris omnipotentis;  
inde venturus est iudicare vivos et mortuos.  
Credo in Spiritum Sanctum, sanctam Ecclesiam catholicam,  
sanctorum communionem, remissionem peccatorum,  
carnis resurrectionem, vitam aeternam. Amen.

sanctificetur nomen tuum;

fiat voluntas tua, sicut in caelo et in terra.

et ne nos inducas in tentationem;  
sed libera nos a malo. Amen.

Sancta Bernadetta, ora pro nobis.

Maria, sine labe concepta, ora pro nobis qui ad te confugimus.

Sancta Maria, Mater Dei, intercede pro hoc itinere:  
ut Dominus gressus dirigat, viam custodiat, mentes sobrias et prudentes servet,  
tempestates, errores, casus et insidias pro sua providentia avertat,  
et, si qua difficultas oriatur, eam in salutem et pacem convertat.  
Ora pro nobis peccatoribus, nunc et in hora mortis nostrae. Amen.

Domine Iesu Christe, non in signis aut praesidiis quasi magicis confidimus,  
sed in misericordia tua, in gratia tua, et in sancta voluntate Patris.  
Per intercessionem Beatae Mariae semper Virginis,  
duc hoc iter ad pacem, ad caritatem, ad prudentiam, et ad bonum finem,  
sicut tibi placuerit.

Fiat voluntas tua.  
Per Christum Dominum nostrum. Amen.

In nomine Patris, et Filii, et Spiritus Sancti. Amen.

## 灵恩派（Charismatic Movement）

天父，我奉主耶稣基督的名来到你面前，敬拜你、归向你，将这次出行交托在你手中；愿你的同在引导道路，愿你的平安护卫前后左右。

Πάτερ ἡμῶν ὁ ἐν τοῖς οὐρανοῖς·  
ἁγιασθήτω τὸ ὄνομά σου·  
ἐλθέτω ἡ βασιλεία σου·  
γενηθήτω τὸ θέλημά σου,  
ὡς ἐν οὐρανῷ καὶ ἐπὶ γῆς·  
τὸν ἄρτον ἡμῶν τὸν ἐπιούσιον  
δὸς ἡμῖν σήμερον·  
καὶ ἄφες ἡμῖν τὰ ὀφειλήματα ἡμῶν,  
ὡς καὶ ἡμεῖς ἀφήκαμεν τοῖς ὀφειλέταις ἡμῶν·  
καὶ μὴ εἰσενέγκῃς ἡμᾶς εἰς πειρασμόν,  
ἀλλὰ ῥῦσαι ἡμᾶς ἀπὸ τοῦ πονηροῦ.

主耶稣基督，我承认你是主；凡我心中有惧怕、急躁、骄傲、疏忽、埋怨或不信的地方，求你赦免我、洁净我。若我与人有亏欠，求你赐我谦卑与和好的心；我放下报复、咒诅与苦毒，把审判交在你公义怜悯的手中。

Ὑποτάγητε οὖν τῷ θεῷ· ἀντίστητε δὲ τῷ διαβόλῳ, καὶ φεύξεται ἀφ᾽ ὑμῶν· ἐγγίσατε τῷ θεῷ, καὶ ἐγγιεῖ ὑμῖν.

奉耶稣基督的名，我弃绝惧怕、混乱、鲁莽、试探与一切不合神心意的捆绑；我拒绝让焦虑控制判断，也拒绝让疏忽带来危险。愿我的心思意念、时间安排、交通工具、同行关系与每一步道路，都归在基督的主权之下。

主耶稣，你已经借着十字架和复活得胜；我披戴神所赐的全副军装：以真理束腰，以公义当作护心镜，以平安的福音当作预备走路的鞋，拿起信德的藤牌，戴上救恩的头盔，持守圣灵的宝剑，就是神的道，并靠着圣灵随时多方祷告。

σημεῖα δὲ τοῖς πιστεύσασιν ταῦτα παρακολουθήσει· ἐν τῷ ὀνόματί μου δαιμόνια ἐκβαλοῦσιν.

奉拿撒勒人耶稣基督的名，我抵挡一切黑暗、欺骗、恐惧、混乱、意外与死亡的权势；凡不属于基督的搅扰，不得侵扰这次出行。若前方有危险、拦阻或陷阱，求主亲自显明、挪开，或引导平安绕过；不求伤害任何人，只求脱离凶恶、化险为夷、平安抵达。

圣灵，求你充满我，以你的平安安定我的心，以你的智慧引导我的判断，以你的节制管理我的言语、速度、休息与选择。求你赐下警醒，使我不冒进、不分心、不轻忽安全；也赐下恩典，使途中所遇的人都蒙平安与善意相待。

 κύριε Ἰησοῦ Χριστέ, ἐλέησον.

主啊，我为这次出行祈求：愿天气、道路、交通、行程、身体、精神、通讯与一切安排都在你看顾之中；愿出行平安顺利，一路无险无难；若有突发之事，求你赐下及时的帮助、清楚的方向与合宜的保护，使我安然经过，平安抵达。

天父，求你保守这祷告在圣经真理、爱与秩序中；使我不凭恐惧夸大黑暗，也不凭情绪作冲动宣告，而是顺服你、警醒尽责、温柔谨慎。愿圣灵以平安遮盖，以真理更新，以基督的爱引导；凡事都交托在你的怜悯与圣洁旨意中。

Ἀμήν.

---

## Հայ Առաքելական Եկեղեցի

Յանուն Հօր եւ Որդւոյ եւ Հոգւոյն Սրբոյ. Ամէն.

Ամենասուրբ Երրորդութիւն, Հայր եւ Որդի եւ Հոգի Սուրբ, մէկ Աստուած, ողորմեա մեզ եւ առաջնորդեա զճանապարհս մեր խաղաղութեամբ.

Տէր Աստուած մեր, պահեա զամենայն ճանապարհորդս եւ զամենայն որք ելանեն ի ճանապարհ, զի լինիցի երթն խաղաղ եւ յաջող, անփորձանք եւ անխափան, եւ հասցո զնոսա ի տեղին իւրեանց խաղաղութեամբ.

Ողորմեա ինձ, Աստուած, ըստ մեծի ողորմութեան քում.  
եւ ըստ բազում գթութեան քում քաւեա զանօրէնութիւնս իմ.  
Առաւել եւս լուա զիս յանօրէնութենէ իմմէ,  
եւ ի մեղաց իմոց սրբեա զիս.

Պահպանիչ եւ յոյս հաւատացելոց, Քրիստոս Աստուած մեր,  
պահեա զմեզ ընդ հովանեաւ սուրբ եւ պատուական խաչի քո ի խաղաղութեան.  
Փրկեա զմեզ յերեւելի եւ յաներեւոյթ թշնամւոյն,  
արժանաւորեա գոհութեամբ փառաւորել զքեզ ընդ Հօր եւ ընդ Սրբոյ Հոգւոյն,  
այժմ եւ միշտ եւ յաւիտեանս յաւիտենից. Ամէն.

Սուրբ Աստուած, Սուրբ եւ Հզօր, Սուրբ եւ Անմահ,  
որ խաչեցար վասն մեր, ողորմեա մեզ.  
Սուրբ Աստուած, Սուրբ եւ Հզօր, Սուրբ եւ Անմահ,  
որ խաչեցար վասն մեր, ողորմեա մեզ.  
Սուրբ Աստուած, Սուրբ եւ Հզօր, Սուրբ եւ Անմահ,  
որ խաչեցար վասն մեր, ողորմեա մեզ.

Հայր մեր, որ յերկինս ես,  
սուրբ եղիցի անուն քո.  
եկեսցէ արքայութիւն քո.  
եղիցին կամք քո որպէս յերկինս եւ յերկրի.  
զհաց մեր հանապազորդ տուր մեզ այսօր.  
եւ թող մեզ զպարտիս մեր,  
որպէս եւ մեք թողումք մերոց պարտապանաց.  
եւ մի տանիր զմեզ ի փորձութիւն,  
այլ փրկեա զմեզ ի չարէն.  
զի քո է արքայութիւն եւ զօրութիւն եւ փառք յաւիտեանս. Ամէն.

Հաւատով խոստովանիմ եւ երկիր պագանեմ Քեզ,  
Հայր եւ Որդի եւ Հոգի Սուրբ,  
անեղ եւ անմահ բնութիւն.  
արարիչ հրեշտակաց եւ մարդկան եւ ամենայն եղելոց.  
ողորմեա քո արարածոց եւ ինձ բազմամեղիս.

Տէր Յիսուս Քրիստոս, Որդի Աստուծոյ կենդանւոյ,  
լուր աղաչանաց մերոց.  
Ուղղեա զքայլս ճանապարհորդաց, պահեա զմիտս ի խաղաղութեան,  
զաչս ի զգաստութեան, զսիրտս ի յոյս եւ ի հաւատս.  
Հեռացո զփորձանս, զվնասս, զխռովութիւնս եւ զամենայն չար պատահար,  
եւ եթէ վտանգ երեւի, դարձո զայն ի խաղաղութիւն քո ողորմութեամբ.  
Առաջնորդեա ընդ ճանապարհն, պահպանեա ի գնալ եւ ի դառնալ,  
եւ հասցո ի խաղաղ հանգիստ եւ ի բարի ժամանում,  
ըստ կամաց քոց սրբոց եւ փրկարարաց.

Բարեխօսութեամբ Սրբուհւոյ Աստուածածնին եւ միշտ Կուսին Մարիամու,  
սրբոց առաքելոցն, սրբոց հայրապետացն,  
սրբոյ Գրիգորի Լուսաւորչին,  
սրբոյ Ներսէսի Շնորհալւոյ,  
սրբոյ Գրիգորի Նարեկացւոյ,  
եւ ամենայն սրբոց քոց,  
Տէր, ողորմեա. Տէր, ողորմեա. Տէր, ողորմեա.

Փառք Հօր եւ Որդւոյ եւ Հոգւոյն Սրբոյ,  
այժմ եւ միշտ եւ յաւիտեանս յաւիտենից. Ամէն.

Քեզ յանձնեմք զճանապարհս եւ զկեանս մեր, Տէր մարդասէր.  
ոչ ի վստահութիւն գործոց մերոց, այլ ի մեծ ողորմութիւն քո,  
ոչ իբրեւ հատուցումն, այլ իբրեւ խոնարհ աղաչանք.  
Ամենայն օրհնութիւն, խորհուրդ եւ սրբագործութիւն եղիցի ըստ կարգի Սուրբ Եկեղեցւոյ քո,  
իսկ աղօթքս մեր ընդունեա ի խաղաղութիւն եւ ի պահպանումն.  
Քեզ փառք յաւիտեանս յաւիտենից. Ամէն.

---

## 菲律宾 El Shaddai

In the name of the Father, and of the Son, and of the Holy Spirit. Amen.

El Shaddai, El Shaddai, El Elyon na Adonai,  
we praise You, we worship You, we thank You, and we glorify Your holy name.  
Panginoon, salamat po. Hallelujah, praise the Lord.

Lord Jesus Christ, have mercy on us.  
Panginoon, maawa ka.  
Kristo, maawa ka.  
Panginoon, maawa ka.

Our Father, who art in heaven,  
hallowed be thy name;  
thy kingdom come;  
thy will be done on earth as it is in heaven.  
Give us this day our daily bread;  
and forgive us our trespasses,  
as we forgive those who trespass against us;  
and lead us not into temptation,  
but deliver us from evil. Amen.

You who dwell in the shelter of the Most High,  
who abide in the shade of the Almighty,  
say to the LORD, “My refuge and fortress,  
my God in whom I trust.”  
He will rescue you from the fowler’s snare,  
from the destroying plague,  
He will shelter you with his pinions,  
and under his wings you may take refuge;  
his faithfulness is a protecting shield.

Lord Jesus Christ,  
we bring before You this intention:  
愿出行平安顺利，一路无险无难；若遇惊险，求主施恩化险为夷，保守道路、车辆、天气、时间、同行者与一切安排，使旅程安稳有序，平安抵达。

El Shaddai, God Almighty, keep us from evil and guide our steps in truth.  
Send Your holy angels to guard the way.  
Give alertness to drivers, wisdom in decisions, patience in delays, and peace in every heart.  
Let no fear rule over us; let Your presence go before us, beside us, and behind us.  
Under Your wings may we take refuge until we arrive safely.

Therefore I tell you, all that you ask for in prayer,  
believe that you will receive it and it shall be yours.

Lord, not as a bargain and not by our power,  
but according to Your mercy and holy will,  
we ask this in the name of Jesus Christ. Amen.

Hail Mary, full of grace, the Lord is with thee;  
blessed art thou among women,  
and blessed is the fruit of thy womb, Jesus.  
Holy Mary, Mother of God,  
pray for us sinners,  
now and at the hour of our death. Amen.

Glory be to the Father, and to the Son, and to the Holy Spirit,  
as it was in the beginning, is now, and ever shall be,  
world without end. Amen.

May the Lord bless us, protect us from all evil,  
and bring us to everlasting life. Amen.  
Lord Jesus, keep this prayer within Your holy will, in faith, humility, thanksgiving, and love; may all glory belong to the Father, and to the Son, and to the Holy Spirit. Amen.

In the name of the Father, and of the Son, and of the Holy Spirit. Amen.

---

## 埃塞俄比亚 Tewahedo

Bä-səmə ʾAb wä-Wäld wä-Mänfäs Qəddus, ʾAhadu ʾAmlak. ʾAmen.

Qəddus ʾAmlak, Qəddus Ḥayl, Qəddus Ḥayw zäʾi-yəmot,  
zätäwälädä ʾəm-qəddəst Dəngəl Maryam, täsahalänä.  
Qəddus ʾAmlak, Qəddus Ḥayl, Qəddus Ḥayw zäʾi-yəmot,  
zätäṣäwwärä bəʾəntitänä, täsahalänä.  
Qəddus ʾAmlak, Qəddus Ḥayl, Qəddus Ḥayw zäʾi-yəmot,  
zätäqäbärä wä-tänśəʾa ʾəmən-mutan, täsahalänä.

ʾEgziʾo märḥänä Krəstos.  
ʾEgziʾo märḥänä Krəstos.  
ʾEgziʾo märḥänä Krəstos.

Ṣälotä haymanot:  
Näʾamən bäʾahadu ʾAmlak, ʾAb, ʾamlakä kullu,  
zägäbärä sämayat wä-mədər, zäyətarʾay wä-zäʾiyətarʾay.  
Näʾamən bäʾahadu ʾEgziʾ, Iyyäsus Krəstos, Wäldä ʾAmlak,  
Wäldä ʾAb waḥid, zätawälädä ʾəm-ʾAb qädmä kullu zämän.

Dawit:  
ʾEgziʾo, ʾəntä mänbäru lä-zäyäsəbbəḥukä,  
wä-məṣgänu lä-zäyəṭäwəq bä-məḥrätəkä.  
ʾAntä təḥəbbəlä wä-täṣəllälä,  
ʾantä täwəḥəso wä-mäʿqäbä səlam.  
ʾAy təḥaddəg lä-mənsut,  
ʾala adḥənänä wä-ʾaḍḥənänä ʾəm-kullu ʾəkuy.

ʾAntä ʾEgziʾo, ʾamlakä ʾAb wä-Wäld wä-Mänfäs Qəddus,  
bə-məḥrätəkä täsähal länä.  
Bä-mängädənä hab länä səlam,  
ʾaṣəlləlä länä bə-yəmanəkä,  
ʾazəzo lä-mälʾəktəkä yəḥəlu mängädänə,  
wä-ʾabṣaḥänə bä-səlam ḫäbä mədrä näʾati.  
ʾƏm-kullu ḫäṭär, ʾəm-kullu fətnä, ʾəm-kullu ʾəkuy,  
bə-rəḥrəhəkä adḥənänä;  
wä-zäyäqäwwəm yəstämäläs bä-səlam,  
zäyəfärሕ yətnäśśaʾ bä-təʾəmərt sälam,  
wä-mängäd zäṣəqot yəkun mängäd zä-məḥrät.

Abunä zäbä-sämayat,  
yitqäddäs səməkä;  
təmṣaʾ mängəśtəkä;  
yəkun fəqadəkä bä-kämä bä-sämay, kämä bä-mədər.  
Sisanä zä-zäntä ʿəlätä habänä yom;  
ḥədäg länä aṣəḥatänä,  
kämä nəḥna nəḥädäg lä-zä-aṣḥaḥunä;  
ʾi taʾabbanä ḫäbä mənsut,  
ʾala adḥənänä wä-ʾaḍḥənänä ʾəm-kullu ʾəkuy.  
ʾIsmä ziʾakä yəʾəti mängəśt,  
wä-ḥayl, wä-səbḥat,  
läʿaläm ʿaläm. ʾAmen.

Bäṣälotä qəddəst Dəngəl Maryam,  
wä-bäṣälotä qəddusan məlʾəkt,  
wä-bäṣälotä qəddusan wä-ṣadəqan,  
ʾEgziʾo, səmaʿ ṣälotänə,  
wä-ʾabṣaḥ länä səlamäka bä-mängäd wä-bä-məṣʾat.

Səbḥat läʾAb, səbḥat läWäld,  
səbḥat läMänfäs Qəddus,  
ʾəntä kämä bəqədmə ʾəgziʾ,  
wä-yəʾəti ʾəgziʾ,  
wä-yəkun läʿaläm ʿaläm.

Bä-Dawit wä-bä-Səʿatat, bä-Abunä zäbä-sämayat,  
bə-məḥrätəkä wä-bäfəqadəkä, ʾEgziʾo,  
ḥəlwänə bä-səlam, ʾalbo ḥəsäd, ʾalbo məḫr, ʾalbo tägbarä ʾəkuy;  
läka wäḥdəka səbḥat wä-səgədät läʿaläm ʿaläm. ʾAmen.

---

## 静修主义 Hesychasm

Εἰς τὸ ὄνομα τοῦ Πατρὸς καὶ τοῦ Υἱοῦ καὶ τοῦ Ἁγίου Πνεύματος. Ἀμήν.

Δόξα σοι, ὁ Θεὸς ἡμῶν, δόξα σοι.

Κύριε Ἰησοῦ Χριστέ, Υἱὲ τοῦ Θεοῦ, ἐλέησόν με τὸν ἁμαρτωλόν.

Κύριε Ἰησοῦ Χριστέ, Υἱὲ τοῦ Θεοῦ, ἐλέησόν με τὸν ἁμαρτωλόν.

Κύριε Ἰησοῦ Χριστέ, Υἱὲ τοῦ Θεοῦ, ἐλέησόν με τὸν ἁμαρτωλόν.

Κύριε Ἰησοῦ Χριστέ, Υἱὲ τοῦ Θεοῦ, ἐλέησόν με ἐν τῇ ὁδῷ ταύτῃ.

Κύριε Ἰησοῦ Χριστέ, Υἱὲ τοῦ Θεοῦ, φύλαξον τὴν πορείαν ἐν εἰρήνῃ, ἀπὸ παντὸς κινδύνου, θλίψεως, καὶ συμφορᾶς.

Κύριε Ἰησοῦ Χριστέ, Υἱὲ τοῦ Θεοῦ, ὁδήγησον εἰς ἀσφαλῆ ἄφιξιν κατὰ τὸ ἅγιόν σου θέλημα, καὶ τὰ δύσκολα ποίησον εἰς σωτηρίαν καὶ εἰρήνην.

Κύριε Ἰησοῦ Χριστέ, Υἱὲ τοῦ Θεοῦ, ἐλέησον ἡμᾶς.

Κύριε Ἰησοῦ Χριστέ, Υἱὲ τοῦ Θεοῦ, ἐλέησόν με τὸν ἁμαρτωλόν.

Κύριε Ἰησοῦ Χριστέ, Υἱὲ τοῦ Θεοῦ, ἐλέησόν με τὸν ἁμαρτωλόν.

Δόξα Πατρὶ καὶ Υἱῷ καὶ Ἁγίῳ Πνεύματι, καὶ νῦν καὶ ἀεὶ καὶ εἰς τοὺς αἰῶνας τῶν αἰώνων.

Κύριε, φύλαξόν με ἐν ταπεινώσει καὶ νήψει· μὴ ἐάσῃς με ζητεῖν σημεῖα ἢ φαντασίας, ἀλλὰ μόνον τὸ ἔλεός σου καὶ τὸ ἅγιόν σου θέλημα.

Ἀμήν.

---

## 菲律宾 Iglesia ni Cristo

Amang banal, Ama naming nasa langit,  
sambahin ang pangalan Mo.

Lumapit po kami sa Iyo na may pagpapakumbaba at pananampalataya.  
Kinikilala naming Ikaw ang tunay na Diyos,  
ang Maylalang, ang nagbibigay-buhay,  
at ang tanging dapat naming sambahin.

Ama, patawarin Mo po kami sa aming mga pagkukulang,  
sa aming mga kasalanan,  
at sa anumang hindi naging kalugud-lugod sa Iyong harapan.  
Linisin Mo po ang aming puso at kalooban,  
at tulungan Mo kaming makasunod sa Iyong mga salita.

Ama naming nasa langit,  
sambahin ang pangalan Mo.  
Dumating nawa ang kaharian Mo.  
Sundin nawa ang loob Mo,  
dito sa lupa para nang sa langit.  
Bigyan Mo kami ngayon ng aming kakanin sa araw-araw.  
At patawarin Mo kami sa aming mga utang,  
gaya naman namin na nagpatawad sa mga may utang sa amin.  
At huwag Mo kaming ihatid sa tukso,  
kundi iligtas Mo kami sa masama.

Ama, inilalapit po namin sa Iyo ang paglalakbay na ito.  
Hinihiling po namin ang Iyong pag-iingat, patnubay, at awa,  
upang maging payapa, maayos, at ligtas ang aming pag-alis, pagdaan, at pagdating.

Ilayo Mo po kami sa kapahamakan, aksidente, masamang panahon, karamdaman, kaguluhan, at anumang panganib.  
Kung may biglang suliranin o hadlang sa daan,  
ipagkaloob Mo po na ito ay malampasan sa paraang mabuti,  
at kung may panganib, gawin Mo pong daan ng pagkaligtas ayon sa Iyong kalooban.

Patnubayan Mo po ang mga magmamaneho, maglilingkod, at makakasalamuha sa paglalakbay.  
Bigyan Mo kami ng maingat na isip, mahinahong puso, at tamang pagpapasiya.  
Ingatan Mo po ang aming katawan, isip, at damdamin,  
at tulungan Mo kaming manatiling masunurin, mapagpasalamat, at nagtitiwala sa Iyo.

Idinadalangin din po namin ang aming sambahayan at ang mga kapatid.  
Pagkalooban Mo sila ng kapayapaan, pagkakaisa, at pag-iingat.  
Patuloy Mo pong patnubayan ang Iglesia, ang mga kapatid,  
at ang mga namumuno sa paglilingkod,  
upang manatili kaming tapat sa pagsunod sa Iyong kalooban.

Hindi po ang aming sariling kalooban ang masunod,  
kundi ang kalooban Mo.  
Turuan Mo kaming magtiwala sa Iyo sa bawat hakbang,  
mag-ingat nang may karunungan,  
at magpasalamat sa Iyong kabutihan.

Ama, sa Iyo lamang kami dumudulog at sumasamba.  
Hindi kami humihingi sa sinumang santo, anghel, larawan, espiritu, o anumang nilalang,  
kundi sa Iyo, ang nag-iisang tunay na Diyos.  
Ang lahat ng ito ay aming hinihiling at idinadalangin  
sa pamamagitan at sa pangalan ng aming Panginoong Jesucristo.

Amen.

---

## 科普特正教

Ἐν ὀνόματι τοῦ Πατρὸς καὶ τοῦ Υἱοῦ καὶ τοῦ Ἁγίου Πνεύματος, Θεοῦ ἑνός. Ἀμήν.

Εὐχαριστοῦμέν σοι, Πάτερ παντοκράτορ, ὅτι ἐσκέπασας ἡμᾶς, ἐφύλαξας ἡμᾶς, ὑπεδέξω ἡμᾶς, ἐφείσω ἡμῶν, ἐστήριξας ἡμᾶς, καὶ ἤγαγες ἡμᾶς ἕως τῆς ὥρας ταύτης. Διὰ τοῦτο δεόμεθα καὶ παρακαλοῦμέν σε, φιλάνθρωπε ἀγαθέ· φύλαξον ἡμᾶς ἐν ταύτῃ τῇ ἁγίᾳ ἡμέρᾳ καὶ πάσῃ ὥρᾳ ἐν εἰρήνῃ.

Ἐλέησον ἡμᾶς, ὁ Θεός, κατὰ τὸ μέγα ἔλεός σου.  
Κύριε ἐλέησον. Κύριε ἐλέησον. Κύριε ἐλέησον.

Ἵλεως γενοῦ, Κύριε, ταῖς ἁμαρτίαις ἡμῶν· καθάρισον τὰς καρδίας ἡμῶν, φώτισον τὸν νοῦν ἡμῶν, καὶ μὴ ἀντανέλῃς τὸ Πνεῦμά σου τὸ Ἅγιον ἀφ’ ἡμῶν· ἀλλὰ στερέωσον ἡμᾶς ἐν μετανοίᾳ, ταπεινώσει, καὶ ἐλπίδι.

Πάτερ ἡμῶν ὁ ἐν τοῖς οὐρανοῖς,  
ἁγιασθήτω τὸ ὄνομά σου·  
ἐλθέτω ἡ βασιλεία σου·  
γενηθήτω τὸ θέλημά σου,  
ὡς ἐν οὐρανῷ καὶ ἐπὶ τῆς γῆς·  
τὸν ἄρτον ἡμῶν τὸν ἐπιούσιον  
δὸς ἡμῖν σήμερον·  
καὶ ἄφες ἡμῖν τὰ ὀφειλήματα ἡμῶν,  
ὡς καὶ ἡμεῖς ἀφήκαμεν τοῖς ὀφειλέταις ἡμῶν·  
καὶ μὴ εἰσενέγκῃς ἡμᾶς εἰς πειρασμόν,  
ἀλλὰ ῥῦσαι ἡμᾶς ἀπὸ τοῦ πονηροῦ.  
Ἐν Χριστῷ Ἰησοῦ τῷ Κυρίῳ ἡμῶν·  
ὅτι σοῦ ἐστιν ἡ βασιλεία καὶ ἡ δύναμις καὶ ἡ δόξα εἰς τοὺς αἰῶνας. Ἀμήν.

Ἅγιος ὁ Θεός,  
Ἅγιος Ἰσχυρός,  
Ἅγιος Ἀθάνατος,  
ἐλέησον ἡμᾶς.

Δόξα Πατρὶ καὶ Υἱῷ καὶ Ἁγίῳ Πνεύματι,  
καὶ νῦν καὶ ἀεὶ καὶ εἰς τοὺς αἰῶνας τῶν αἰώνων. Ἀμήν.

Ἁγία Τριάς, ἐλέησον ἡμᾶς.  
Κύριε, ἱλάσθητι ταῖς ἁμαρτίαις ἡμῶν.  
Δέσποτα, συγχώρησον τὰς ἀνομίας ἡμῶν.  
Ἅγιε, ἐπίσκεψαι καὶ ἴασαι τὰς ἀσθενείας ἡμῶν, ἕνεκεν τοῦ ὀνόματός σου.

Κύριε Ἰησοῦ Χριστέ, ὁ Θεὸς ἡμῶν, ὁ ὁδηγὸς τῶν ἐλπιζόντων ἐπὶ σέ, σκέπασον τὴν πορείαν ταύτην ἐν τῷ ἐλέει σου. Φύλαξον ἀπὸ κινδύνου, ταραχῆς, βλάβης, κακῆς συναντήσεως, ἀοράτων καὶ ὁρατῶν πειρασμῶν· εὐλόγησον τὴν ὁδόν, εἰρήνευσον τὰ βήματα, καὶ ποίησον τὰ δυσχερῆ εὔοδα κατὰ τὸ ἅγιόν σου θέλημα. Ὅπου ἐστὶ φόβος, δὸς παρηγορίαν· ὅπου ἐστὶ κίνδυνος, δὸς διάσωσιν· ὅπου ἐστὶ σύγχυσις, δὸς φῶς· καὶ καταξίωσον ἐν εἰρήνῃ ἀφικέσθαι εἰς τὸν τόπον τῆς ἀναπαύσεως καὶ τῆς ἀσφαλείας.

Ταῖς πρεσβείαις τῆς Παναγίας Θεοτόκου Μαρίας, καὶ τοῦ ἀρχαγγέλου Μιχαήλ, καὶ τοῦ ἀρχαγγέλου Γαβριήλ, καὶ τοῦ ἁγίου Μάρκου τοῦ Εὐαγγελιστοῦ, καὶ πάντων τῶν ἀποστόλων, μαρτύρων, ὁμολογητῶν καὶ ἁγίων· Κύριε, χάρισαι ἡμῖν ἄφεσιν τῶν ἁμαρτιῶν, σκέπην, σωτηρίαν, καὶ εἰρήνην.

Κύριε ἐλέησον. Κύριε ἐλέησον. Κύριε ἐλέησον.

Γενηθήτω, Κύριε, οὐ τὸ θέλημα ἡμῶν, ἀλλὰ τὸ σὸν ἅγιον θέλημα· καὶ δέξαι τὴν δέησιν ταύτην ἐν μετανοίᾳ, εὐχαριστίᾳ, καὶ ὑπακοῇ τῇ ἁγίᾳ σου Ἐκκλησίᾳ, ἄνευ φόβου καὶ ἄνευ ματαιότητος, εἰς δόξαν τοῦ ἁγίου σου ὀνόματος.

Σοὶ πρέπει ἡ δόξα, ἡ τιμή, καὶ ἡ προσκύνησις, σὺν τῷ ἀγαθῷ Πατρί σου καὶ τῷ Ἁγίῳ Πνεύματι τῷ ζωοποιῷ, νῦν καὶ ἀεὶ καὶ εἰς πάντας τοὺς αἰῶνας τῶν αἰώνων. Ἀμήν.

---

## 耶和华见证人

耶和华我们的天父，יהוה，

Πάτερ ἡμῶν ὁ ἐν τοῖς οὐρανοῖς·  
ἁγιασθήτω τὸ ὄνομά σου·  
ἐλθέτω ἡ βασιλεία σου·  
γενηθήτω τὸ θέλημά σου,  
ὡς ἐν οὐρανῷ καὶ ἐπὶ γῆς·  
τὸν ἄρτον ἡμῶν τὸν ἐπιούσιον δὸς ἡμῖν σήμερον·  
καὶ ἄφες ἡμῖν τὰ ὀφειλήματα ἡμῶν,  
ὡς καὶ ἡμεῖς ἀφήκαμεν τοῖς ὀφειλέταις ἡμῶν·  
καὶ μὴ εἰσενέγκῃς ἡμᾶς εἰς πειρασμόν,  
ἀλλὰ ῥῦσαι ἡμᾶς ἀπὸ τοῦ πονηροῦ.

愿你的名被尊为圣；愿你的王国和旨意在我们心中居首位。  
我们为这次出行来到你面前祷告，求你帮助我们保持清醒、谨慎、谦卑和爱心。  
求你赐给我们智慧，使我们能作出合乎圣经原则和实际安全的决定，遵守规则，留意路况，避开不必要的危险。  
若途中遇到困难、延误或突发情况，求你帮助我们不被恐惧控制，而能冷静处理，化险为夷，平安抵达。  
求你保护我们的信心、良心和安全，使我们脱离 πονηρός，不受贪心、急躁、仇恨或不洁的事牵引。  
我们也求你帮助我们不把祷告当作护符或形式，而是以信心、感恩和顺服来依靠你。  
感谢你听我们的祷告，感谢你赐下圣经的指引，也感谢你借着耶稣基督使我们能亲近你。

奉耶稣基督的名祷告，阿们。

---

## 东正教 圣礼礼仪派

Δι’ εὐχῶν τῶν ἁγίων Πατέρων ἡμῶν, Κύριε Ἰησοῦ Χριστέ, ὁ Θεὸς ἡμῶν, ἐλέησον ἡμᾶς.  
Ἀμήν.

Βασιλεῦ οὐράνιε, Παράκλητε, τὸ Πνεῦμα τῆς ἀληθείας, ὁ πανταχοῦ παρὼν καὶ τὰ πάντα πληρῶν, ὁ θησαυρὸς τῶν ἀγαθῶν καὶ ζωῆς χορηγός, ἐλθὲ καὶ σκήνωσον ἐν ἡμῖν, καὶ καθάρισον ἡμᾶς ἀπὸ πάσης κηλῖδος, καὶ σῶσον, Ἀγαθέ, τὰς ψυχὰς ἡμῶν.

Ἅγιος ὁ Θεός, Ἅγιος Ἰσχυρός, Ἅγιος Ἀθάνατος, ἐλέησον ἡμᾶς.  
Ἅγιος ὁ Θεός, Ἅγιος Ἰσχυρός, Ἅγιος Ἀθάνατος, ἐλέησον ἡμᾶς.  
Ἅγιος ὁ Θεός, Ἅγιος Ἰσχυρός, Ἅγιος Ἀθάνατος, ἐλέησον ἡμᾶς.

Δόξα Πατρὶ καὶ Υἱῷ καὶ Ἁγίῳ Πνεύματι, καὶ νῦν καὶ ἀεὶ καὶ εἰς τοὺς αἰῶνας τῶν αἰώνων. Ἀμήν.

Παναγία Τριάς, ἐλέησον ἡμᾶς· Κύριε, ἱλάσθητι ταῖς ἁμαρτίαις ἡμῶν· Δέσποτα, συγχώρησον τὰς ἀνομίας ἡμῖν· Ἅγιε, ἐπίσκεψαι καὶ ἴασαι τὰς ἀσθενείας ἡμῶν, ἕνεκεν τοῦ ὀνόματός σου.

Κύριε, ἐλέησον. Κύριε, ἐλέησον. Κύριε, ἐλέησον.

Πάτερ ἡμῶν ὁ ἐν τοῖς οὐρανοῖς· ἁγιασθήτω τὸ ὄνομά σου· ἐλθέτω ἡ βασιλεία σου· γενηθήτω τὸ θέλημά σου, ὡς ἐν οὐρανῷ καὶ ἐπὶ τῆς γῆς· τὸν ἄρτον ἡμῶν τὸν ἐπιούσιον δὸς ἡμῖν σήμερον· καὶ ἄφες ἡμῖν τὰ ὀφειλήματα ἡμῶν, ὡς καὶ ἡμεῖς ἀφίεμεν τοῖς ὀφειλέταις ἡμῶν· καὶ μὴ εἰσενέγκῃς ἡμᾶς εἰς πειρασμόν, ἀλλὰ ῥῦσαι ἡμᾶς ἀπὸ τοῦ πονηροῦ.

Ἐλέησόν με, ὁ Θεός, κατὰ τὸ μέγα ἔλεός σου, καὶ κατὰ τὸ πλῆθος τῶν οἰκτιρμῶν σου ἐξάλειψον τὸ ἀνόμημά μου.  
Ἐπὶ πλεῖον πλῦνόν με ἀπὸ τῆς ἀνομίας μου, καὶ ἀπὸ τῆς ἁμαρτίας μου καθάρισόν με.  
Ὅτι τὴν ἀνομίαν μου ἐγὼ γινώσκω, καὶ ἡ ἁμαρτία μου ἐνώπιόν μού ἐστι διὰ παντός.

Ἐν εἰρήνῃ τοῦ Κυρίου δεηθῶμεν.  
Κύριε, ἐλέησον.

Ὑπὲρ τῆς ἄνωθεν εἰρήνης καὶ τῆς σωτηρίας τῶν ψυχῶν ἡμῶν, τοῦ Κυρίου δεηθῶμεν.  
Κύριε, ἐλέησον.

Ὑπὲρ τῶν ὁδοιπορούντων καὶ πάντων τῶν ἐν πορείᾳ ὄντων, ὑπὲρ τοῦ δοθῆναι αὐτοῖς ὁδὸν εἰρήνης, ἀσφάλειαν, σύνεσιν, ὑπομονήν, καὶ ἀγαθὴν ἄφιξιν, τοῦ Κυρίου δεηθῶμεν.  
Κύριε, ἐλέησον.

Ὑπὲρ τοῦ ῥυσθῆναι αὐτοὺς ἀπὸ πάσης θλίψεως, ὀργῆς, κινδύνου, ἀνάγκης, ἀτυχήματος, ταραχῆς, καὶ παντὸς κακοῦ συμβεβηκότος, τοῦ Κυρίου δεηθῶμεν.  
Κύριε, ἐλέησον.

Ὑπὲρ τοῦ κατευθῦναι Κύριον τὰ διαβήματα αὐτῶν ἐν εἰρήνῃ, καὶ μεταβαλεῖν τὰ δύσκολα εἰς ὁδὸν σωτηρίας κατὰ τὸ ἅγιον αὐτοῦ θέλημα, τοῦ Κυρίου δεηθῶμεν.  
Κύριε, ἐλέησον.

Ἀντιλαβοῦ, σῶσον, ἐλέησον καὶ διαφύλαξον ἡμᾶς, ὁ Θεός, τῇ σῇ χάριτι.  
Κύριε, ἐλέησον.

Τῆς Παναγίας, ἀχράντου, ὑπερευλογημένης, ἐνδόξου Δεσποίνης ἡμῶν Θεοτόκου καὶ ἀειπαρθένου Μαρίας, μετὰ πάντων τῶν ἁγίων μνημονεύσαντες, ἑαυτοὺς καὶ ἀλλήλους καὶ πᾶσαν τὴν ζωὴν ἡμῶν Χριστῷ τῷ Θεῷ παραθώμεθα.  
Σοί, Κύριε.

Ὁ κατοικῶν ἐν βοηθείᾳ τοῦ Ὑψίστου, ἐν σκέπῃ τοῦ Θεοῦ τοῦ οὐρανοῦ αὐλισθήσεται.  
Ἐρεῖ τῷ Κυρίῳ· Ἀντιλήπτωρ μου εἶ καὶ καταφυγή μου, ὁ Θεός μου, καὶ ἐλπιῶ ἐπ’ αὐτόν.  
Ὅτι αὐτὸς ῥύσεταί σε ἐκ παγίδος θηρευτῶν καὶ ἀπὸ λόγου ταραχώδους.

Κύριε Ἰησοῦ Χριστέ, ὁ Θεὸς ἡμῶν, ὁδὸν εἰρήνης καὶ σωτηρίας χάρισαι τοῖς ὁδοιποροῦσιν, καὶ φύλαξον αὐτοὺς ἀπὸ πάσης θλίψεως, ὀργῆς, κινδύνου καὶ ἀνάγκης. Ἄγγελον εἰρήνης, πιστὸν ὁδηγόν, φύλακα ψυχῶν καὶ σωμάτων, παράσχου αὐτοῖς· τὰ ἐμπόδια πραΰνον, τὰς ἀτραποὺς αὐτῶν κατεύθυνον, τὰ φοβερὰ εἰς ἔλεος μετάβαλε, καὶ ἐν εἰρήνῃ ἀγάγε αὐτοὺς εἰς τὸν προκείμενον τόπον.

Ὑπεραγία Θεοτόκε, σῶσον ἡμᾶς.  
Πάντες οἱ ἅγιοι, πρεσβεύσατε ὑπὲρ ἡμῶν.

Δόξα σοι, Χριστὲ ὁ Θεὸς ἡμῶν, ἡ ἐλπὶς ἡμῶν, δόξα σοι.

Κύριε, ἐλέησον. Κύριε, ἐλέησον. Κύριε, ἐλέησον.

Εἰς χεῖράς σου, Κύριε, παρατιθέμεθα τὴν πορείαν καὶ τὴν ἐπιστροφήν, τὴν ἀρχὴν καὶ τὸ τέλος· οὐχ ὡς ἡμεῖς θέλομεν, ἀλλ’ ὡς σύ, Κύριε, θέλεις· σὺ γὰρ εἶ ἡ εἰρήνη ἡμῶν καὶ ἡ σωτηρία τῶν ψυχῶν ἡμῶν.

Δι’ εὐχῶν τῶν ἁγίων Πατέρων ἡμῶν, Κύριε Ἰησοῦ Χριστέ, ὁ Θεὸς ἡμῶν, ἐλέησον καὶ σῶσον ἡμᾶς.  
Ἀμήν.

## Lutheran

In nomine Patris et Filii et Spiritus Sancti. Amen.

Adiutorium nostrum in nomine Domini,  
qui fecit caelum et terram.

Miserere mei, Deus, secundum misericordiam tuam;  
secundum multitudinem miserationum tuarum dele iniquitatem meam.  
Amplius lava me ab iniquitate mea,  
et a peccato meo munda me.

Kyrie eleison.  
Christe eleison.  
Kyrie eleison.

Credo in Deum Patrem omnipotentem, creatorem caeli et terrae.  
Et in Iesum Christum, Filium eius unicum, Dominum nostrum,  
qui conceptus est de Spiritu Sancto,  
natus ex Maria virgine,  
passus sub Pontio Pilato,  
crucifixus, mortuus, et sepultus,  
descendit ad inferos,  
tertia die resurrexit a mortuis,  
ascendit ad caelos,  
sedet ad dexteram Dei Patris omnipotentis,  
inde venturus est iudicare vivos et mortuos.  
Credo in Spiritum Sanctum,  
sanctam ecclesiam catholicam,  
sanctorum communionem,  
remissionem peccatorum,  
carnis resurrectionem,  
et vitam aeternam. Amen.

Pater noster, qui es in caelis,  
sanctificetur nomen tuum;  
adveniat regnum tuum;  
fiat voluntas tua,  
sicut in caelo et in terra.  
Panem nostrum quotidianum da nobis hodie;  
et dimitte nobis debita nostra,  
sicut et nos dimittimus debitoribus nostris;  
et ne nos inducas in tentationem;  
sed libera nos a malo.  
Amen.

Qui habitat in adiutorio Altissimi,  
in protectione Dei caeli commorabitur.  
Dicet Domino: Susceptor meus es tu et refugium meum,  
Deus meus; sperabo in eum.

Domine Deus, Pater caelestis,  
per Iesum Christum Filium tuum, Dominum nostrum,  
respice in misericordia super hoc iter.  
Non in meritis nostris confidimus,  
sed in sola misericordia tua et in promissione evangelii tui.

Dirige viam, Domine;  
custodi proficiscentes sub tutela tua;  
averte pericula manifesta et occulta,  
casus, terrores, violentiam, tempestates, moras nocivas,  
et omne malum quod corpori, animae, fidei et caritati nocere potest.

Da prudentiam in consiliis, sobrietatem in itinere,  
patientiam in mora, pacem in corde,  
et caritatem erga omnes in via occurrentes.  
Si periculum immineat, eripe nos misericorditer;  
si angustia oriatur, converte eam in salutem;  
si timor insurgat, confirma nos verbo tuo.  
Concede ut iter sine malo perficiatur,  
et ut in pace ad locum destinatum perveniatur,  
secundum voluntatem tuam bonam et misericordem.

In manus tuas, Domine, commendamus hoc iter;  
redemisti nos, Domine Deus veritatis.  
Custodi nos in Christo Iesu,  
qui pro nobis mortuus est et resurrexit,  
et a cuius caritate nihil nos separare potest.

Benedicamus Domino.  
Deo gratias.

Benedicat nos omnipotens et misericors Dominus,  
Pater et Filius et Spiritus Sanctus. Amen.

## 摩门教（LDS）

Our Father in Heaven,

We thank Thee for the gift of life, for the means to travel, and for the watchful care Thou hast already given.

We acknowledge Thy Son, Jesus Christ, our Savior and Redeemer, and we seek the guidance, comfort, and warning voice of the Holy Ghost.

We ask Thee to bless this journey with safety, wisdom, patience, and peace. Please help the way to be orderly and smooth; protect against danger, accident, confusion, delay, and harm; and when difficulties arise, help them be turned aside or overcome in righteousness.

May all who travel be attentive, calm, and guided to make good decisions. May the vehicle, road, weather, timing, and all needed arrangements be under Thy merciful care, that the journey may be completed safely and that arrival may be peaceful.

May Thy will be done, and may this protection come according to faith in Jesus Christ, without fear, without presumption, and with gratitude for Thy mercy.

We offer this prayer humbly, relying on no power but Thine, and seeking only what is good, lawful, and pleasing unto Thee.

We say these things in the name of Jesus Christ, amen.

---

## മലങ്കര ഓർത്തഡോക്സ് സുറിയാനി സഭ

B-shem Abo w-Bro w-Ruho d-Qudsho, Hado Aloho Shariro.  
Shubho leh, w-‘alayn raḥme w-ḥanono neshtaf‘un l-‘olam ‘olmin. Amin.

Shubho l-Abo w-la-Bro w-la-Ruho d-Qudsho,  
men ‘olam w-‘adamo l-‘olam ‘olmin. Amin.

Abun d-bashmayo,  
nethqadash shmokh,  
tithe malkuthokh,  
nehwe sebyonokh,  
aykano d-bashmayo af b-ar‘o.  
Hab lan lahmo d-sunqonan yawmono.  
Washbuq lan ḥawbayn wa-ḥṭohayn,  
aykano d-af ḥnan shbaqan l-ḥayobayn.  
W-lo ta‘lan l-nesyuno,  
ella paṣṣan men bisho.  
Metol d-dilokh hi malkutho w-ḥaylo w-teshbuḥto  
l-‘olam ‘olmin. Amin.

Qadishat Aloho,  
Qadishat Ḥayelthono,  
Qadishat Lo Moyutho,  
d-ethṣlebt ḥlopayn,  
etraḥem ‘alayn.

Qadishat Aloho,  
Qadishat Ḥayelthono,  
Qadishat Lo Moyutho,  
d-ethṣlebt ḥlopayn,  
etraḥem ‘alayn.

Qadishat Aloho,  
Qadishat Ḥayelthono,  
Qadishat Lo Moyutho,  
d-ethṣlebt ḥlopayn,  
etraḥem ‘alayn.

Moran etraḥem ‘alayn.  
Moran ḥus w-raḥem ‘alayn.  
Moran ‘ani w-raḥem ‘alayn.  
Shubho lokh Moran.  
Shubho lokh Moran.  
Shubho lokh sabran l-‘olam.

Mizmor 90/91:  
D-yotheb b-sethro d-‘Elyono,  
b-ṭelolo d-Aloho nethnaga.  
Emar l-Moryo: Beth gawsī w-beth tawklanī,  
Alohi d-‘alaw tawkleth.

കർത്താവായ ദൈവമേ, നിന്റെ കരുണയിൽ യാത്ര ചെയ്യുന്ന നിന്റെ ദാസന്മാരെ കാത്തുകൊള്ളണമേ. വഴികളിൽ അപകടവും അനർത്ഥവും വരാതെ, ഭയവും കുഴപ്പവും നീങ്ങി, കഷ്ടതകൾ നിന്റെ കരുണയാൽ നന്മയായി മാറി, സമാധാനത്തോടും ആരോഗ്യത്തോടും കൂടി സുരക്ഷിതമായി ലക്ഷ്യസ്ഥാനത്ത് എത്തുവാൻ അനുഗ്രഹിക്കണമേ. മനുഷ്യശക്തിയിലല്ല, നിന്റെ ദയയിലും സംരക്ഷണത്തിലുമത്രേ ഞങ്ങൾ ആശ്രയിക്കുന്നു. പിതാവിന്റെയും പുത്രന്റെയും പരിശുദ്ധാത്മാവിന്റെയും മഹത്വത്തിൽ ഞങ്ങളെ പ്രകാശിപ്പിച്ചു സമാധാനത്തിൽ നടത്തണമേ.

Dukhrono d-Yoldath Aloho Maryam,  
w-d-qadishe kulhon,  
nehwe ‘amman l-‘olam. Amin.

Shubho l-Abo w-la-Bro w-la-Ruho d-Qudsho,  
men ‘olam w-‘adamo l-‘olam ‘olmin. Amin.  
Haleluya, Haleluya, Haleluya, shubho lokh Aloho.

കർത്താവേ, ഈ പ്രാർത്ഥന നിന്റെ തിരുവിഷ്ടത്തിന്നും പരിശുദ്ധ സഭയുടെ ക്രമത്തിനും കീഴിൽ, മന്ത്രവാദമല്ലാതെ വിനയമുള്ള അപേക്ഷയായി സ്വീകരിക്കണമേ; നിന്റെ കരുണയാലും വിശുദ്ധ ക്രൂശിന്റെ സംരക്ഷണത്താലും ഞങ്ങളെ സമാധാനത്തിൽ ഉറപ്പിക്കണമേ. Amin.

## الكنيسة المارونية

B-shmo d-Abo w-d-Bro w-d-Ruho d-Qudsho, Had Aloho shariro. Amin.

Qadishat Aloho,  
Qadishat Hayelthono,  
Qadishat lo Moyutho,  
ethraham ‘alayn.

Shubho l-Abo w-la-Bro w-la-Ruho d-Qudsho,  
men ‘olam w-‘adamo l-‘olam ‘olmin. Amin.

Abun d-bashmayo,  
netqadash shmokh.  
Tite malkuthokh.  
Nehwe sebyonokh,  
aykano d-bashmayo oph bar‘o.  
Haw lan lahmo d-sunqonan yawmono.  
Washboq lan hawbayn wahtohayn,  
aykano doph hnan shbaqn l-hayyobayn.  
Wlo ta‘lan l-nesyuno,  
elo fasso lan men bisho.  
Metul d-dilokh hi malkutho w-haylo w-teshbuhto  
l-‘olam ‘olmin. Amin.

Shlom lekh Maryam,  
mlayat taybutho,  
Moran ‘amekh.  
Mbarakhto at b-neshe,  
w-mbarakh hu piro d-karsekh,  
Maran Yeshua.  
O qadishto Maryam,  
Yoldath Aloho,  
saloy hlofayn hnaye,  
hosho w-bsho‘at mawthan. Amin.

Moran Yeshua Mshiha,  
Bro d-Aloho hayo,  
qabel slothan mkikhto,  
w-haw shayno w-neturo l-kul d-azlin b-urho.

B-shfa‘otho d-Yoldath Aloho Maryam,  
w-d-Mor Maron,  
w-d-Mor Efram,  
w-d-Mor Ya‘qub,  
w-d-kulhon qadisho,  
Moryo etraham ‘alayn.

Moryo, nhoor urhon b-nuhrokh,  
nattar lhon b-slibokh,  
w-shadar mal’akhokh d-shayno qdamayhon.  
A‘ber menhon sakle, pahhe, hadthe,  
w-kul sakinto d-gushmo w-d-naphsho;  
w-ma d-metra‘a bisho,  
haw lhon furqono b-rahmayk,  
w-‘bad urhon shlintho ‘ad d-mato b-shayno.

Dkar, Moryo, l-‘abdayk w-l-amhotokh,  
l-msafre, l-manhage, l-‘ozre,  
w-l-kul d-mqawen ‘al rahmayk.  
Haw lhon lebbo shliho, ‘ayno nahiro,  
w-yado d-zhiro,  
d-la nethqelon w-la nashqelon,  
elo neshtewzon b-shayno.

Dkar, Moryo, l-‘anide mhaymne,  
w-ahlan ‘am kulhon qadishayk b-nuhro d-paradiso.

Moryo, nhoor lan b-nuhrokh,  
nattar lan b-slibokh,  
shadar ‘alayn rahmayk,  
w-ahlan b-shaynokh.  
La b-haylo d-milta,  
elo b-rahmayk w-b-sebyonokh qadisho,  
qabel slothan hadé mkikhto,  
w-shaw lan d-nehwe b-shayno ‘amekh.

Lakh shubho,  
l-Abokh iqoro,  
w-l-Ruho d-Qudsho segedto,  
hosho w-bkul zban  
w-l-‘olam ‘olmin. Amin.

## Ritus Hispano-Mozarabicus

V. Dominus sit semper vobiscum.  
R. Et cum spiritu tuo.

Gloria et honor Patri et Filio et Spiritui Sancto,  
in saecula saeculorum. Amen.

Psalmus:  
Qui habitat in adiutorio Altissimi,  
in protectione Dei caeli commorabitur.  
Dicet Domino: Susceptor meus es tu et refugium meum;  
Deus meus, sperabo in eum.  
Quoniam ipse liberavit me de laqueo venantium,  
et a verbo aspero.  
Scapulis suis obumbrabit tibi,  
et sub pennis eius sperabis.  
Non timebis a timore nocturno,  
a sagitta volante in die,  
a negotio perambulante in tenebris,  
ab incursu et daemonio meridiano.  
Quoniam angelis suis mandavit de te,  
ut custodiant te in omnibus viis tuis.

Oratio admonitionis:  
Oremus, fratres carissimi, Dominum Deum omnipotentem,  
pro itinere pacato et prospero,  
ut clementia eius viam dirigat,  
pericula avertat, impedimenta in salutem convertat,  
et ad locum destinatum cum pace perducat.  
Non quaerimus damnum cuiusquam,  
sed misericordiam, custodiam et pacem omnibus viatoribus.

R. Praesta, aeterne omnipotens Deus.

Alia:  
Deus, qui filios Israel per mare Rubrum sicco vestigio transire fecisti,  
et Tobiae comitem angelum dedisti,  
respice propitius super hoc iter.  
Mitte Spiritum Sanctum Paraclitum ad consolandum et regendum;  
praecedat nos Christus Dominus, via, veritas et vita;  
comitetur nos angelica custodia;  
recedat omnis metus, omnis casus, omnis insidia, omnis confusio.  
Quod asperum est, tua pietate leniatur;  
quod obscurum est, lumine tuo clarificetur;  
quod periculosum est, in tranquillitatem convertatur;  
ut sine noxa, sine scandalo, sine adversitate gravi,  
ad finem itineris incolumes perveniamus.

Post nomina:  
Memor esto, Domine, famulorum famularumque tuarum viventium,  
et omnium qui in viis, in mari, in aere, in terra,  
in labore, in peregrinatione vel in necessitate versantur.  
Memor esto etiam famulorum famularumque tuarum defunctorum,  
et dona eis locum refrigerii, lucis et pacis.

R. Amen.

Ad pacem:  
Pacem tuam, Domine Iesu Christe,  
quam dedisti discipulis tuis,  
conserva in nobis.  
Dissolve timores, comprime scandala,  
dirige gressus nostros in caritate tua,  
et fac nos pacem portare ubicumque transierimus.

R. Amen.

Sanctus:  
Sanctus, Sanctus, Sanctus Dominus Deus Sabaoth.  
Pleni sunt caeli et terra gloria tua.  
Hosanna in excelsis.  
Benedictus qui venit in nomine Domini.  
Hosanna in excelsis.

Pater noster:  
Pater noster, qui es in caelis:  
sanctificetur nomen tuum;  
adveniat regnum tuum;  
fiat voluntas tua, sicut in caelo et in terra.  
Panem nostrum quotidianum da nobis hodie;  
et dimitte nobis debita nostra,  
sicut et nos dimittimus debitoribus nostris;  
et ne nos inducas in tentationem;  
sed libera nos a malo. Amen.

Completuria:  
Libera nos, Domine, ab omni malo,  
praeterito, praesenti et futuro;  
intercedente sancta et gloriosa Dei Genitrice Maria,  
cum beatis apostolis, sancto Iacobo, sancto Isidoro,  
et omnibus sanctis,  
da propitius pacem in diebus nostris,  
ut ope misericordiae tuae adiuti  
et a peccato simus semper liberi  
et ab omni perturbatione securi.  
Iter nostrum in voluntate tua perfice,  
et ad portum quietis nos perduc in pace.

R. Amen.

V. In nomine Domini nostri Iesu Christi perficiatur oratio nostra cum pace.  
R. Amen.

Gloria et honor tibi, sancta Trinitas,  
qui regnas in Ecclesia tua;  
custodi corda nostra in fide catholica,  
in humilitate, obedientia et caritate,  
ut nihil praesumamus ex nobis,  
sed omnia tuae misericordiae committamus. Amen.

---

## 新使徒改革

Father God, I come before You in the name of Jesus Christ concerning this journey, asking for safe travel, smooth passage, deliverance from danger, and peaceful arrival.

Πάτερ ἡμῶν ὁ ἐν τοῖς οὐρανοῖς·  
ἁγιασθήτω τὸ ὄνομά σου·  
ἐλθέτω ἡ βασιλεία σου·  
γενηθήτω τὸ θέλημά σου,  
ὡς ἐν οὐρανῷ καὶ ἐπὶ γῆς·  
τὸν ἄρτον ἡμῶν τὸν ἐπιούσιον δὸς ἡμῖν σήμερον·  
καὶ ἄφες ἡμῖν τὰ ὀφειλήματα ἡμῶν,  
ὡς καὶ ἡμεῖς ἀφήκαμεν τοῖς ὀφειλέταις ἡμῶν·  
καὶ μὴ εἰσενέγκῃς ἡμᾶς εἰς πειρασμόν,  
ἀλλὰ ῥῦσαι ἡμᾶς ἀπὸ τοῦ πονηροῦ.

Father, I confess and renounce every sin, fear, presumption, carelessness, anxiety, false agreement, occult involvement, ungodly vow, spoken curse, and word of danger connected with this journey. I place this travel under the blood, lordship, and authority of Jesus Christ.

I forgive every person connected with this journey and release them from judgment. I do not curse, control, shame, or seek vengeance against any human being. I reject only the works of darkness, lies, bondage, sin, confusion, destruction, and oppression.

הַיֹּשֵׁב בְּסֵתֶר עֶלְיוֹן  
בְּצֵל שַׁדַּי יִתְלוֹנָן׃  
אֹמַר לַיהוָה מַחְסִי וּמְצוּדָתִי  
אֱלֹהַי אֶבְטַח־בּוֹ׃

Ἰδοὺ δέδωκα ὑμῖν τὴν ἐξουσίαν  
τοῦ πατεῖν ἐπάνω ὄφεων καὶ σκορπίων,  
καὶ ἐπὶ πᾶσαν τὴν δύναμιν τοῦ ἐχθροῦ,  
καὶ οὐδὲν ὑμᾶς οὐ μὴ ἀδικήσει.

ὃ ἐὰν δήσῃς ἐπὶ τῆς γῆς  
ἔσται δεδεμένον ἐν τοῖς οὐρανοῖς,  
καὶ ὃ ἐὰν λύσῃς ἐπὶ τῆς γῆς  
ἔσται λελυμένον ἐν τοῖς οὐρανοῖς.

Ὑποτάγητε οὖν τῷ θεῷ·  
ἀντίστητε δὲ τῷ διαβόλῳ,  
καὶ φεύξεται ἀφ᾽ ὑμῶν.

In the name of Jesus Christ, I bind every demonic assignment, accident scheme, spirit of fear, confusion, violence, theft, delay unto harm, destruction, infirmity, distraction, and every work of the enemy seeking to operate against this journey. I command every unclean influence connected with the route, vehicle, timing, atmosphere, or travel decisions to leave and not return, according to the authority of Jesus Christ.

In the name of Jesus Christ, I loose the peace of Christ, angelic protection, wisdom, alertness, favor, clear guidance, safe timing, sound judgment, physical strength, calm emotions, and orderly passage over this journey. Let every road, path, station, vehicle, crossing, connection, and arrival be covered by the mercy and kingdom order of God.

I cut off every ungodly soul tie, false burden, fear agreement, spoken curse, occult claim, destructive pattern, and demonic access point connected with this travel. I declare that the handwriting against this journey is canceled in Christ and that every hostile power is disarmed under the cross of Jesus Christ.

Καὶ αὐτοὶ ἐνίκησαν αὐτὸν  
διὰ τὸ αἷμα τοῦ ἀρνίου  
καὶ διὰ τὸν λόγον τῆς μαρτυρίας αὐτῶν.

Father, fill every cleansed place with the Holy Spirit, the peace of Christ, the fear of the Lord, wisdom, purity, and steadfast love. Establish Your kingdom order from departure to arrival. Turn every hidden danger away, make a way where there seems to be no way, and let what could become harm be transformed by Your mercy into safety, clarity, and peace.

Father, keep this prayer submitted to Your holy will and to the character of Jesus Christ. Let no word here become accusation against any person; let every resistance be only against sin, lies, bondage, demonic influence, and works of darkness. If fear, compulsion, conflict, or distress arises, lead into repentance, forgiveness, wise counsel, pastoral care, and proper help. I receive Your protection without presumption, and I walk in obedience, humility, and peace.

I thank You, Father, and seal this prayer in the name of Jesus Christ.

Ἀμήν.

---

## 贵格会（Quakers）

[Silence]

O God, Light within and beyond us,  
gather us into stillness.

We hold this journey in the Light.  
We bring before Thee the concern for safe travel, clear passage, watchful hearts, and peaceful arrival.  
Let truth, peace, mercy, and faithfulness be made plain along the way.

The true Light:  
“That was the true Light, which lighteth every man that cometh into the world.”

“The Lord is my shepherd; I shall not want.  
He maketh me to lie down in green pastures:  
he leadeth me beside the still waters.  
He restoreth my soul:  
he leadeth me in the paths of righteousness for his name's sake.  
Yea, though I walk through the valley of the shadow of death,  
I will fear no evil: for thou art with me;  
thy rod and thy staff they comfort me.”

[Silence]

Our Father which art in heaven,  
Hallowed be thy name.  
Thy kingdom come.  
Thy will be done in earth, as it is in heaven.  
Give us this day our daily bread.  
And forgive us our debts, as we forgive our debtors.  
And lead us not into temptation,  
but deliver us from evil:  
For thine is the kingdom, and the power, and the glory, for ever.  
Amen.

[Silence]

If words are given:

Lord, keep this journey in Thy Light.  
Order each step in peace.  
Give attention where attention is needed,  
patience where patience is needed,  
and help in every place of uncertainty.  
May danger be turned aside,  
fear be quieted,  
and the way be held in Thy mercy.  
Bring the travelers to their destination in peace,  
according to Thy will.

[Silence]

Into Thy care we commend the road, the time, the companions, and the arrival.  
Let us rest in the Light, and be faithful.

[Silence]

---

## старообрядцы

Во имя Отца и Сына и Святаго Духа. Аминь.

Господи Исусе Христе, Сыне Божии, помилуй мя грешнаго.

Царю Небесныи, Утешителю, Душе истинныи, иже везде сыи и вся исполняя, сокровище благих и жизни подателю, прииди и вселися в ны, и очисти ны от всякия скверны, и спаси, Блаже, душа наша.

Святыи Боже, Святыи Крепкии, Святыи Безсмертныи, помилуй нас.  
Святыи Боже, Святыи Крепкии, Святыи Безсмертныи, помилуй нас.  
Святыи Боже, Святыи Крепкии, Святыи Безсмертныи, помилуй нас.

Слава Отцу и Сыну и Святому Духу, и ныне и присно и во веки веком. Аминь.

Пресвятая Троице, помилуй нас. Господи, очисти грехи наша. Владыко, прости беззакония наша. Святыи, посети и исцели немощи наша, имене Твоего ради.

Господи помилуй.  
Господи помилуй.  
Господи помилуй.

Отче наш, иже еси на небесех, да святится имя Твое, да приидет Царствие Твое, да будет воля Твоя, яко на небеси и на земли. Хлеб наш насущныи даждь нам днесь, и остави нам долги наша, якоже и мы оставляем должником нашим, и не введи нас во искушение, но избави нас от лукаваго.

Господи помилуй.  
Господи помилуй.  
Господи помилуй.

Верую во единаго Бога Отца, Вседержителя, Творца небу и земли, видимым же всем и невидимым. И во единаго Господа Исуса Христа, Сына Божия, Единороднаго, иже от Отца рожденнаго прежде всех век. Света от Света, Бога истинна от Бога истинна, рожденна, а не сотворенна, единосущна Отцу, Имже вся быша. Нас ради человек и нашего ради спасения сшедшаго с небес, и воплотившагося от Духа Свята и Марии Девы, и вочеловечшася. Распятаго же за ны при Понтийстем Пилате, и страдавша, и погребенна. И воскресшаго в третии день по Писанием. И возшедшаго на небеса, и седяща одесную Отца. И паки грядущаго со славою судити живым и мертвым, Его же Царствию несть конца. И в Духа Святаго, Господа истиннаго и животворящаго, иже от Отца исходящаго, иже со Отцем и Сыном спокланяема и сславима, глаголавшаго пророки. Во едину святую соборную и апостольскую Церковь. Исповедую едино крещение во оставление грехов. Чаю воскресения мертвым, и жизни будущаго века. Аминь.

Господи Исусе Христе, Сыне Божии, призри милостивно на путь предлежащии и на вся путешествующия: настави стопы их в мире, сохрани от всякаго зла видимаго и невидимаго, от напасти, беды, смущения, клеветы, внезапныя скорби и всякаго преткновения; всякое опасение обрати во спасение, всякую тесноту разреши миром, и сподоби благополучно достигнути места потребнаго, по святей воле Твоей.

Живыи в помощи Вышняго, в крове Бога Небеснаго водворится. Речет Господеви: Заступник мой еси и Прибежище мое, Бог мой, и уповаю на Него. Яко Той избавит тя от сети ловчи и от словесе мятежна. Плещма Своима осенит тя, и под криле Его надеешися: оружием обыдет тя истина Его. Не убоишися от страха нощнаго, от стрелы летящия во дни, от вещи во тме преходящия, от сряща и беса полуденнаго. Яко Ангелом Своим заповесть о тебе, сохранити тя во всех путех твоих.

Да воскреснет Бог, и расточатся врази Его, и да бежат от лица Его ненавидящии Его. Яко исчезает дым, да исчезнут, яко тает воск от лица огня, тако да погибнут беси от лица любящих Бога и знаменующихся крестным знамением, и в веселии глаголющих: радуися, Пречестныи и Животворящии Кресте Господень, прогоняя бесы силою на тебе пропятаго Господа нашего Исуса Христа, во ад сшедшаго и поправшаго силу диаволю, и даровавшаго нам тебе Крест Свой Честныи на прогнание всякаго супостата. О Пречестныи и Животворящии Кресте Господень, помогай ми со Святою Госпожею Девою Богородицею и со всеми святыми во веки. Аминь.

Господи Исусе Христе, Сыне Божии, помилуй нас.  
Господи Исусе Христе, Сыне Божии, помилуй нас.  
Господи Исусе Христе, Сыне Божии, помилуй нас.

Пресвятая Богородице, спаси нас.

Достойно есть яко воистинну блажити Тя, Богородицу, присноблаженную и пренепорочную и Матерь Бога нашего. Честнейшую херувим и славнейшую воистинну серафим, без истления Бога Слова рождшую, сущую Богородицу Тя величаем.

Слава Отцу и Сыну и Святому Духу, и ныне и присно и во веки веком. Аминь.

Господи помилуй.  
Господи помилуй.  
Господи помилуй.

Господи Исусе Христе, Сыне Божии, молитв ради Пречистыя Твоея Матере, силою Честнаго и Животворящаго Креста, и всех святых Твоих, сохрани путь сей в мире, отведи всякое зло без вреда кому-либо, управи вся ко спасению, и помилуй и спаси нас, яко Благ и Человеколюбец. Аминь.
