أَسْتَغْفِرُ اللهَ الْعَظِيمَ الَّذِي لَا إِلٰهَ إِلَّا هُوَ الْحَيُّ الْقَيُّومُ وَأَتُوبُ إِلَيْهِ.  
أَسْتَغْفِرُ اللهَ، أَسْتَغْفِرُ اللهَ، أَسْتَغْفِرُ اللهَ.

لَا إِلٰهَ إِلَّا اللهُ.  
لَا إِلٰهَ إِلَّا اللهُ مُحَمَّدٌ رَسُولُ اللهِ.  
لَا إِلٰهَ إِلَّا أَنْتَ سُبْحَانَكَ إِنِّي كُنْتُ مِنَ الظَّالِمِينَ.

يَا اللهُ، يَا لَطِيفُ، يَا حَفِيظُ، يَا سَلَامُ، يَا مُؤْمِنُ، يَا مُهَيْمِنُ، يَا نَصِيرُ، يَا فَتَّاحُ، يَا عَلِيمُ، يَا حَكِيمُ.

هُوَ اللهُ الَّذِي لَا إِلٰهَ إِلَّا هُوَ عَالِمُ الْغَيْبِ وَالشَّهَادَةِ هُوَ الرَّحْمٰنُ الرَّحِيمُ.  
هُوَ اللهُ الَّذِي لَا إِلٰهَ إِلَّا هُوَ الْمَلِكُ الْقُدُّوسُ السَّلَامُ الْمُؤْمِنُ الْمُهَيْمِنُ الْعَزِيزُ الْجَبَّارُ الْمُتَكَبِّرُ سُبْحَانَ اللهِ عَمَّا يُشْرِكُونَ.  
هُوَ اللهُ الْخَالِقُ الْبَارِئُ الْمُصَوِّرُ لَهُ الْأَسْمَاءُ الْحُسْنَى يُسَبِّحُ لَهُ مَا فِي السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالْأَرْضِ وَهُوَ الْعَزِيزُ الْحَكِيمُ.

سُبْحَانَ الَّذِي سَخَّرَ لَنَا هٰذَا وَمَا كُنَّا لَهُ مُقْرِنِينَ، وَإِنَّا إِلَى رَبِّنَا لَمُنْقَلِبُونَ.

اللَّهُمَّ إِنَّا نَسْأَلُكَ فِي سَفَرِنَا هٰذَا الْبِرَّ وَالتَّقْوَى، وَمِنَ الْعَمَلِ مَا تَرْضَى.  
اللَّهُمَّ هَوِّنْ عَلَيْنَا سَفَرَنَا هٰذَا، وَاطْوِ عَنَّا بُعْدَهُ.  
اللَّهُمَّ أَنْتَ الصَّاحِبُ فِي السَّفَرِ، وَالْخَلِيفَةُ فِي الْأَهْلِ.  
اللَّهُمَّ إِنَّا نَعُوذُ بِكَ مِنْ وَعْثَاءِ السَّفَرِ، وَكَآبَةِ الْمَنْظَرِ، وَسُوءِ الْمُنْقَلَبِ.

اللَّهُمَّ يَا حَفِيظُ، احْفَظْنَا فِي الطَّرِيقِ مِنْ كُلِّ سُوءٍ وَفَجْأَةٍ وَضُرٍّ، وَاصْرِفْ عَنَّا مَا لَا نُطِيقُ، وَاجْعَلْ لَنَا مِنْ كُلِّ ضِيقٍ مَخْرَجًا، وَمِنْ كُلِّ خَوْفٍ أَمْنًا، وَمِنْ كُلِّ عُسْرٍ يُسْرًا.  
اللَّهُمَّ بَلِّغْنَا مَقْصِدَنَا بِسَلَامٍ وَعَافِيَةٍ، وَرُدَّنَا إِنْ رَدَدْتَنَا بِسَلَامٍ وَعَافِيَةٍ، غَيْرَ ضَالِّينَ وَلَا مُضِلِّينَ، غَيْرَ ضَارِّينَ وَلَا مَضْرُورِينَ.

اللَّهُمَّ لَا نَطْلُبُ بِهٰذَا الدُّعَاءِ ضَرَرًا لِأَحَدٍ مِنْ خَلْقِكَ، وَلَا عُدْوَانًا، وَلَكِنْ نَسْأَلُكَ أَنْ تَرْفَعَ الْمَانِعَ، وَتَصْرِفَ الْبَلَاءَ، وَتَجْعَلَ السَّبِيلَ سَبِيلَ رَحْمَةٍ وَسَلَامٍ.

اللَّهُمَّ صَلِّ وَسَلِّمْ وَبَارِكْ عَلَى سَيِّدِنَا مُحَمَّدٍ، عَبْدِكَ وَنَبِيِّكَ وَرَسُولِكَ، وَعَلَى آلِهِ وَصَحْبِهِ.

بِسْمِ اللهِ الرَّحْمٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ.  
الْحَمْدُ لِلّٰهِ رَبِّ الْعَالَمِينَ.  
الرَّحْمٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ.  
مَالِكِ يَوْمِ الدِّينِ.  
إِيَّاكَ نَعْبُدُ وَإِيَّاكَ نَسْتَعِينُ.  
اهْدِنَا الصِّرَاطَ الْمُسْتَقِيمَ.  
صِرَاطَ الَّذِينَ أَنْعَمْتَ عَلَيْهِمْ، غَيْرِ الْمَغْضُوبِ عَلَيْهِمْ وَلَا الضَّالِّينَ.  
آمِينَ.

أَسْتَغْفِرُ اللهَ وَأَتُوبُ إِلَيْهِ.  
لَا إِلٰهَ إِلَّا اللهُ، وَحْدَهُ لَا شَرِيكَ لَهُ، لَهُ الْمُلْكُ وَلَهُ الْحَمْدُ، وَهُوَ عَلَى كُلِّ شَيْءٍ قَدِيرٌ.  
اللَّهُمَّ صَلِّ عَلَى سَيِّدِنَا مُحَمَّدٍ وَعَلَى آلِهِ وَصَحْبِهِ وَسَلِّمْ.  
وَحَسْبُنَا اللهُ وَنِعْمَ الْوَكِيلُ، نِعْمَ الْمَوْلَى وَنِعْمَ النَّصِيرُ.  
وَالْحَمْدُ لِلّٰهِ رَبِّ الْعَالَمِينَ.

---

## 巴哈伊（Bahá'í）

Yā Ilāhī, Yā Rabbī, Yā Maqṣūdī.

Ashhadu yā Ilāhī bi-annaka khalaqtanī li-‘irfānika wa ‘ibādatika.  
Ashhadu fī hādhā al-ḥīn bi-‘ajzī wa qudratika, wa ḍa‘fī wa iqtidārika, wa faqrī wa ghinā’ika.  
Lā ilāha illā anta al-Muhayminu al-Qayyūm.

Yā Ibn ar-Rūḥ!  
Fī awwal al-qawl imlik qalban jayyidan ḥasanan munīran,  
li-tamlika mulkan dā’iman bāqiyan azalīyan qadīman.

Yā Ibn ar-Rūḥ!  
Aḥabba al-ashyā’i ‘indī al-inṣāf;  
lā targhab ‘anhu in takun ilayya rāghiban,  
wa-lā taghful minhu li-takūna lī amīnan.

Yā Ilāhī,  
aj‘al hādhā as-safar fī ḥifẓika wa ri‘āyatika,  
wa-sahhil ṭarīqahu, wa-iṣrif ‘anhu al-khaṭar wa al-balā’,  
wa-ij‘al kulla ‘usrin yantahī ilā yusrin bi-faḍlika,  
ḥattā yakūna al-wuṣūl salāman wa ṭuma’nīnatan.  
Wa-lā naqṣidu illā al-khayra, wa-lā naṭlub ḍararan li-aḥad;  
bal nufawwiḍu al-amra kullahu ilā mashī’atika wa raḥmatika.

Alláh-u-Abhá.  
Alláh-u-Abhá.  
Alláh-u-Abhá.

Anta al-Muhayminu al-Qayyūm.  
Lā ilāha illā anta.

---

## 曼达派

B-šumaihun ḏ-Hiia Rbia.  
Bišum Manda ḏ-Hiia.  
Bišum Kušṭa rba.

Bišum Hiia Rbia u-bišum Manda ḏ-Hiia,  
b-kušṭa rba ḏ-lā šuqra,  
nishmata u-pagra ḏ-kul man ḏ-azil b-urha,  
nidkian b-nhura,  
niqaiman b-kušṭa,  
u-šlama nihui b-urhaihun.

Hiia Rbia, Manda ḏ-Hiia,  
nhura rba, ziwa rba,  
naṭar l-azlia b-urha,  
min ḥišuka, min šiqra,  
min sakinta, min pašquta,  
min urha ḏ-lā kušṭa.

Manda ḏ-Hiia,  
dakir lan b-kušṭa,  
hab šlama b-mahlaḵta,  
hab asuta b-pagra,  
hab zakuta b-nishimta,  
u-habilun maṭia b-šlama,  
b-lā ḥišuka, b-lā niqra, b-lā dardara.

Kušṭa asgir l-kun.  
Kušṭa asgir l-Hiia.  
Kušṭa asgir l-Manda ḏ-Hiia.

Asuta u-zakuta  
nihuilun l-kul azlia b-urha;  
laufa ḏ-Hiia,  
laufa ḏ-kušṭa,  
laufa ḏ-nhura.

B-kušṭa, lā šuqra.  
B-nhura, lā ḥišuka.  
B-šlama, lā hizqa.  
Lā masbuta, lā masiqta, lā qabin;  
ella brakha dakia b-kušṭa,  
b-rahma ḏ-Hiia Rbia.

B-šumaihun ḏ-Hiia Rbia.  
Asuta u-zakuta.

---

## 德鲁兹派

بِسْمِ اللهِ الرَّحْمٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

الْحَمْدُ لِلَّهِ رَبِّ الْعَالَمِينَ.

أَشْهَدُ أَنْ لَا إِلٰهَ إِلَّا اللهُ وَحْدَهُ لَا شَرِيكَ لَهُ.  
التَّوْحِيدُ حَقٌّ، وَالصِّدْقُ حَقٌّ، وَالتَّسْلِيمُ لِأَمْرِ الْمَوْلَى حَقٌّ.

نَوَيْنَا نِيَّةَ صِدْقٍ وَتَوْحِيدٍ فِي السَّفَرِ،  
أَنْ يَكُونَ الطَّرِيقُ بِسَلَامٍ وَسَدَادٍ،  
وَأَنْ يُصْرَفَ عَنِ السَّائِرِ كُلُّ خَوْفٍ وَضَرَرٍ،  
وَأَنْ يَبْلُغَ مَقْصِدَهُ آمِنًا مُطْمَئِنًّا.

قُلْ هُوَ اللَّهُ أَحَدٌ.  
اللَّهُ الصَّمَدُ.  
لَمْ يَلِدْ وَلَمْ يُولَدْ.  
وَلَمْ يَكُنْ لَهُ كُفُوًا أَحَدٌ.

قُلْ أَعُوذُ بِرَبِّ الْفَلَقِ.  
مِنْ شَرِّ مَا خَلَقَ.  
وَمِنْ شَرِّ غَاسِقٍ إِذَا وَقَبَ.  
وَمِنْ شَرِّ النَّفَّاثَاتِ فِي الْعُقَدِ.  
وَمِنْ شَرِّ حَاسِدٍ إِذَا حَسَدَ.

قُلْ أَعُوذُ بِرَبِّ النَّاسِ.  
مَلِكِ النَّاسِ.  
إِلَٰهِ النَّاسِ.  
مِنْ شَرِّ الْوَسْوَاسِ الْخَنَّاسِ.  
الَّذِي يُوَسْوِسُ فِي صُدُورِ النَّاسِ.  
مِنَ الْجِنَّةِ وَالنَّاسِ.

اللَّهُمَّ يَا وَاحِدُ يَا أَحَدُ، يَا مَوْلَانَا جَلَّ ذِكْرُهُ،  
احْفَظِ السَّائِرَ فِي خُرُوجِهِ وَدُخُولِهِ،  
وَسَهِّلْ طَرِيقَهُ، وَأَمِّنْ مَسِيرَهُ،  
وَاصْرِفْ عَنْهُ الْخَطَرَ وَالْحَادِثَ وَالضِّيقَ وَالْفَزَعَ،  
وَاجْعَلْ مَا عَسُرَ عَلَيْهِ يَسِيرًا،  
وَمَا خِيفَ مِنْهُ سَبَبًا لِلْعَافِيَةِ وَحُسْنِ الْعَاقِبَةِ،  
وَبَلِّغْهُ مَقْصِدَهُ بِسَلَامٍ وَسَكِينَةٍ.

اللَّهُمَّ ثَبِّتْهُ عَلَى الصِّدْقِ وَالْأَمَانَةِ وَحُسْنِ التَّدْبِيرِ،  
وَاجْعَلْهُ لَا يَظْلِمُ أَحَدًا وَلَا يُؤْذِي أَحَدًا،  
وَاكْفِهِ شَرَّ مَا يَعْلَمُ وَمَا لَا يَعْلَمُ،  
وَاهْدِهِ إِلَى مَا فِيهِ الْحَقُّ وَالْحِكْمَةُ وَالسَّلَامَةُ.

رَضِينَا بِفِعْلِكَ، وَسَلَّمْنَا لِأَمْرِكَ،  
وَلَا حَوْلَ وَلَا قُوَّةَ إِلَّا بِاللهِ.

اللَّهُمَّ طَهِّرْ نِيَّتَنَا مِنَ الشِّرْكِ وَالرِّيَاءِ وَالْبَغْيِ،  
وَاجْعَلْ ذِكْرَنَا لَكَ تَوْحِيدًا وَصِدْقًا وَتَسْلِيمًا،  
وَاحْفَظْنَا مِنْ قَوْلِ الزُّورِ وَالْأَذَى وَالْعُدْوَانِ.

وَالسَّلَامُ عَلَى مَنِ اتَّبَعَ الْهُدَى.

---

## 苏菲 Tijaniyya

بِسْمِ اللهِ الرَّحْمٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ.

اللَّهُمَّ إِنَّا نَوَيْنَا ذِكْرَكَ، وَطَلَبَ رِضَاكَ، وَالتَّوْبَةَ إِلَيْكَ، وَنَسْأَلُكَ سَفَرًا سَالِمًا مُيَسَّرًا، وَطَرِيقًا مَحْفُوظًا، وَوُصُولًا بِخَيْرٍ وَعَافِيَةٍ.

أَسْتَغْفِرُ اللهَ.  
أَسْتَغْفِرُ اللهَ.  
أَسْتَغْفِرُ اللهَ.

أَسْتَغْفِرُ اللهَ الْعَظِيمَ الَّذِي لَا إِلٰهَ إِلَّا هُوَ الْحَيُّ الْقَيُّومُ، وَأَتُوبُ إِلَيْهِ.

اللَّهُمَّ صَلِّ عَلَى سَيِّدِنَا مُحَمَّدٍ، الْفَاتِحِ لِمَا أُغْلِقَ، وَالْخَاتِمِ لِمَا سَبَقَ، نَاصِرِ الْحَقِّ بِالْحَقِّ، وَالْهَادِي إِلَى صِرَاطِكَ الْمُسْتَقِيمِ، وَعَلَى آلِهِ حَقَّ قَدْرِهِ وَمِقْدَارِهِ الْعَظِيمِ.

لَا إِلٰهَ إِلَّا اللهُ.  
لَا إِلٰهَ إِلَّا اللهُ.  
لَا إِلٰهَ إِلَّا اللهُ.

قُلْ هُوَ اللهُ أَحَدٌ ۝ اللهُ الصَّمَدُ ۝ لَمْ يَلِدْ وَلَمْ يُولَدْ ۝ وَلَمْ يَكُنْ لَهُ كُفُوًا أَحَدٌ.

قُلْ أَعُوذُ بِرَبِّ الْفَلَقِ ۝ مِنْ شَرِّ مَا خَلَقَ ۝ وَمِنْ شَرِّ غَاسِقٍ إِذَا وَقَبَ ۝ وَمِنْ شَرِّ النَّفَّاثَاتِ فِي الْعُقَدِ ۝ وَمِنْ شَرِّ حَاسِدٍ إِذَا حَسَدَ.

قُلْ أَعُوذُ بِرَبِّ النَّاسِ ۝ مَلِكِ النَّاسِ ۝ إِلٰهِ النَّاسِ ۝ مِنْ شَرِّ الْوَسْوَاسِ الْخَنَّاسِ ۝ الَّذِي يُوَسْوِسُ فِي صُدُورِ النَّاسِ ۝ مِنَ الْجِنَّةِ وَالنَّاسِ.

اللَّهُمَّ صَلِّ وَسَلِّمْ عَلَى سَيِّدِنَا مُحَمَّدٍ، وَأَذِنْ لَنَا فِي الْأَدَبِ مَعَكَ، وَاجْعَلْ لَنَا مِنْ أَسْرَارِ الصَّلَاةِ عَلَى نَبِيِّكَ نُورًا وَحِفْظًا وَلُطْفًا، بِغَيْرِ دَعْوَى وَلَا عُدْوَانٍ.

سُبْحَانَ الَّذِي سَخَّرَ لَنَا هٰذَا وَمَا كُنَّا لَهُ مُقْرِنِينَ، وَإِنَّا إِلَى رَبِّنَا لَمُنْقَلِبُونَ.

اللَّهُمَّ إِنَّا نَسْأَلُكَ فِي سَفَرِنَا هٰذَا الْبِرَّ وَالتَّقْوَى، وَمِنَ الْعَمَلِ مَا تَرْضَى.  
اللَّهُمَّ هَوِّنْ عَلَيْنَا سَفَرَنَا هٰذَا، وَاطْوِ عَنَّا بُعْدَهُ.  
اللَّهُمَّ أَنْتَ الصَّاحِبُ فِي السَّفَرِ، وَالْخَلِيفَةُ فِي الْأَهْلِ.  
اللَّهُمَّ إِنَّا نَعُوذُ بِكَ مِنْ وَعْثَاءِ السَّفَرِ، وَكَآبَةِ الْمَنْظَرِ، وَسُوءِ الْمُنْقَلَبِ.

يَا اللهُ، يَا رَحْمٰنُ، يَا رَحِيمُ، يَا حَفِيظُ، يَا لَطِيفُ،  
اِحْفَظْنَا فِي الذَّهَابِ وَالإِيَابِ، وَفِي كُلِّ طَرِيقٍ وَمَعْبَرٍ،  
وَاصْرِفْ عَنَّا الْبَلَاءَ وَالْخَوْفَ وَالْحَادِثَ وَالشَّرَّ،  
وَاجْعَلْ كُلَّ عُسْرٍ يُسْرًا، وَكُلَّ خَوْفٍ أَمْنًا، وَكُلَّ ضِيقٍ فَرَجًا،  
وَلَا تَجْعَلْ دُعَاءَنَا سَبَبًا لِضَرَرِ أَحَدٍ مِنْ خَلْقِكَ، بَلِ اصْرِفِ الْأَذَى وَاهْدِ الْقُلُوبَ، إِنَّكَ عَلَى كُلِّ شَيْءٍ قَدِيرٌ.

رَبَّنَا آتِنَا فِي الدُّنْيَا حَسَنَةً، وَفِي الْآخِرَةِ حَسَنَةً، وَقِنَا عَذَابَ النَّارِ.

الْحَمْدُ لِلَّهِ رَبِّ الْعَالَمِينَ ۝ الرَّحْمٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ ۝ مَالِكِ يَوْمِ الدِّينِ ۝ إِيَّاكَ نَعْبُدُ وَإِيَّاكَ نَسْتَعِينُ ۝ اهْدِنَا الصِّرَاطَ الْمُسْتَقِيمَ ۝ صِرَاطَ الَّذِينَ أَنْعَمْتَ عَلَيْهِمْ، غَيْرِ الْمَغْضُوبِ عَلَيْهِمْ وَلَا الضَّالِّينَ. آمِينَ.

اللَّهُمَّ ثَبِّتْنَا عَلَى الْإِذْنِ وَالْأَدَبِ، وَنَقِّ نِيَّاتِنَا مِنَ الرِّيَاءِ وَالدَّعْوَى، وَلَا تَجْعَلْنَا نَخْلِطُ عَهْدًا بِعَهْدٍ وَلَا وِرْدًا بِوِرْدٍ، وَلَا نَسْتَعْمِلُ صَلَاتَنَا وَذِكْرَنَا فِي لَعْنٍ وَلَا قَهْرٍ وَلَا بَيْعٍ وَلَا ضَمَانٍ، وَاجْعَلْ هٰذَا الدُّعَاءَ خَالِصًا لِوَجْهِكَ الْكَرِيمِ، مَقْبُولًا بِرَحْمَتِكَ، مَخْتُومًا بِالسَّلَامِ.  
وَصَلَّى اللهُ عَلَى سَيِّدِنَا مُحَمَّدٍ وَعَلَى آلِهِ وَصَحْبِهِ، وَسَلَّمَ تَسْلِيمًا، وَالْحَمْدُ لِلَّهِ رَبِّ الْعَالَمِينَ.

---

## 十二伊玛目什叶 · 阿舒拉哀仪

نَوَيْنَا قِرَاءَةَ زِيَارَةِ عَاشُورَاءَ، وَإِهْدَاءَ ثَوَابِهَا إِلَى النَّبِيِّ مُحَمَّدٍ وَآلِهِ الطَّاهِرِينَ، وَإِلَى أَرْوَاحِ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ وَالْمُؤْمِنَاتِ، وَسَأَلْنَا اللهَ تَعَالَى قَضَاءَ حَاجَتِنَا فِي حِفْظِ السَّفَرِ وَسَلَامَةِ الطَّرِيقِ وَدَفْعِ الْبَلَاءِ وَحُسْنِ الْوُصُولِ، قُرْبَةً إِلَى اللهِ تَعَالَى.

بِسْمِ اللهِ الرَّحْمٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

الْحَمْدُ لِلّٰهِ رَبِّ الْعَالَمِينَ  
الرَّحْمٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ  
مَالِكِ يَوْمِ الدِّينِ  
إِيَّاكَ نَعْبُدُ وَإِيَّاكَ نَسْتَعِينُ  
اهْدِنَا الصِّرَاطَ الْمُسْتَقِيمَ  
صِرَاطَ الَّذِينَ أَنْعَمْتَ عَلَيْهِمْ  
غَيْرِ الْمَغْضُوبِ عَلَيْهِمْ وَلَا الضَّالِّينَ

قُلْ هُوَ اللهُ أَحَدٌ  
اللهُ الصَّمَدُ  
لَمْ يَلِدْ وَلَمْ يُولَدْ  
وَلَمْ يَكُنْ لَهُ كُفُوًا أَحَدٌ

اللَّهُمَّ صَلِّ عَلَى مُحَمَّدٍ وَآلِ مُحَمَّدٍ.

السَّلَامُ عَلَيْكَ يَا أَبَا عَبْدِ اللهِ.  
السَّلَامُ عَلَيْكَ يَا ابْنَ رَسُولِ اللهِ.  
السَّلَامُ عَلَيْكَ يَا ابْنَ أَمِيرِ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ وَابْنَ سَيِّدِ الْوَصِيِّينَ.  
السَّلَامُ عَلَيْكَ يَا ابْنَ فَاطِمَةَ سَيِّدَةِ نِسَاءِ الْعَالَمِينَ.  
السَّلَامُ عَلَيْكَ يَا ثَارَ اللهِ وَابْنَ ثَارِهِ وَالْوِتْرَ الْمَوْتُورَ.  
السَّلَامُ عَلَيْكَ وَعَلَى الْأَرْوَاحِ الَّتِي حَلَّتْ بِفِنَائِكَ.  
عَلَيْكُمْ مِنِّي جَمِيعًا سَلَامُ اللهِ أَبَدًا مَا بَقِيتُ وَبَقِيَ اللَّيْلُ وَالنَّهَارُ،  
وَلَا جَعَلَهُ اللهُ آخِرَ الْعَهْدِ مِنِّي لِزِيَارَتِكُمْ.

السَّلَامُ عَلَى الْحُسَيْنِ،  
وَعَلَى عَلِيِّ بْنِ الْحُسَيْنِ،  
وَعَلَى أَوْلَادِ الْحُسَيْنِ،  
وَعَلَى أَصْحَابِ الْحُسَيْنِ.

يَا أَبَا عَبْدِ اللهِ، لَقَدْ عَظُمَتِ الرَّزِيَّةُ وَجَلَّتْ وَعَظُمَتِ الْمُصِيبَةُ بِكَ عَلَيْنَا وَعَلَى جَمِيعِ أَهْلِ الْإِسْلَامِ،  
وَجَلَّتْ وَعَظُمَتْ مُصِيبَتُكَ فِي السَّمَاوَاتِ عَلَى جَمِيعِ أَهْلِ السَّمَاوَاتِ.

فَلَعَنَ اللهُ أُمَّةً أَسَّسَتْ أَسَاسَ الظُّلْمِ وَالْجَوْرِ عَلَيْكُمْ أَهْلَ الْبَيْتِ،  
وَلَعَنَ اللهُ أُمَّةً دَفَعَتْكُمْ عَنْ مَقَامِكُمْ وَأَزَالَتْكُمْ عَنْ مَرَاتِبِكُمُ الَّتِي رَتَّبَكُمُ اللهُ فِيهَا،  
وَلَعَنَ اللهُ أُمَّةً قَتَلَتْكُمْ،  
وَلَعَنَ اللهُ الْمُمَهِّدِينَ لَهُمْ بِالتَّمْكِينِ مِنْ قِتَالِكُمْ.  
بَرِئْنَا إِلَى اللهِ وَإِلَيْكُمْ مِنْهُمْ وَمِنْ أَشْيَاعِهِمْ وَأَتْبَاعِهِمْ وَأَوْلِيَائِهِمْ.

يَا أَبَا عَبْدِ اللهِ، إِنَّا سِلْمٌ لِمَنْ سَالَمَكُمْ، وَحَرْبٌ لِمَنْ حَارَبَكُمْ إِلَى يَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ.

اللَّهُمَّ اجْعَلْنَا عِنْدَكَ وُجَهَاءَ بِالْحُسَيْنِ عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ فِي الدُّنْيَا وَالْآخِرَةِ.  
اللَّهُمَّ اجْعَلْ مَحْيَانَا مَحْيَا مُحَمَّدٍ وَآلِ مُحَمَّدٍ،  
وَمَمَاتَنَا مَمَاتَ مُحَمَّدٍ وَآلِ مُحَمَّدٍ.

اللَّهُمَّ لَكَ الْحَمْدُ حَمْدَ الشَّاكِرِينَ لَكَ عَلَى مُصَابِهِمْ،  
الْحَمْدُ لِلَّهِ عَلَى عَظِيمِ رَزِيَّتِنَا.  
اللَّهُمَّ ارْزُقْنَا شَفَاعَةَ الْحُسَيْنِ يَوْمَ الْوُرُودِ،  
وَثَبِّتْ لَنَا قَدَمَ صِدْقٍ عِنْدَكَ مَعَ الْحُسَيْنِ وَأَصْحَابِ الْحُسَيْنِ الَّذِينَ بَذَلُوا مُهَجَهُمْ دُونَ الْحُسَيْنِ عَلَيْهِ السَّلَامُ.

وَا حُسَيْنَاه.  
وَا شَهِيدَاه.  
يَا لَيْتَنَا كُنَّا مَعَكُمْ فَنَفُوزَ فَوْزًا عَظِيمًا.  
لَبَّيْكَ يَا حُسَيْن.  
لَبَّيْكَ يَا ثَارَ الله.

اللَّهُمَّ إِنَّا نَسْأَلُكَ بِحَقِّ مُحَمَّدٍ وَآلِ مُحَمَّدٍ، وَبِحَقِّ الْحُسَيْنِ الشَّهِيدِ، وَبِحَقِّ أَهْلِ بَيْتِهِ وَأَصْحَابِهِ،  
أَنْ تَحْفَظَنَا فِي سَفَرِنَا وَطَرِيقِنَا وَمَرْكَبِنَا وَمَمْشَانَا وَمَنْزِلِنَا،  
وَأَنْ تَصْرِفَ عَنَّا كُلَّ خَوْفٍ وَخَطَرٍ وَحَادِثٍ وَفِتْنَةٍ وَشَرٍّ،  
وَأَنْ تَجْعَلَ لَنَا مِنْ كُلِّ ضِيقٍ فَرَجًا، وَمِنْ كُلِّ عُسْرٍ يُسْرًا، وَمِنْ كُلِّ بَلَاءٍ عَافِيَةً،  
وَأَنْ تُبَدِّلَ الْخَوْفَ أَمْنًا، وَالْعَثْرَةَ سَلَامَةً، وَالْمَشَقَّةَ رَحْمَةً،  
وَأَنْ تُوصِلَنَا إِلَى مَقْصِدِنَا سَالِمِينَ غَانِمِينَ، بِخَيْرٍ وَسِتْرٍ وَعَافِيَةٍ.

يَا اللهُ يَا اللهُ يَا اللهُ،  
يَا حَافِظُ يَا كَرِيمُ،  
يَا لَطِيفُ يَا رَحِيمُ،  
احْفَظْنَا بِحِفْظِكَ، وَاكْلَأْنَا بِكَلَاءَتِكَ، وَاجْعَلْنَا فِي أَمَانِكَ،  
فَإِنَّهُ لَا حِفْظَ إِلَّا حِفْظُكَ، وَلَا أَمَانَ إِلَّا أَمَانُكَ.

اللَّهُمَّ صَلِّ عَلَى مُحَمَّدٍ وَآلِ مُحَمَّدٍ.  
اللَّهُمَّ تَقَبَّلْ هَذَا الْقَلِيلَ مِنَّا، وَاجْعَلْ ثَوَابَهُ هَدِيَّةً إِلَى رَسُولِكَ مُحَمَّدٍ وَآلِهِ الطَّاهِرِينَ، وَإِلَى أَرْوَاحِ شُهَدَاءِ كَرْبَلَاءَ، وَإِلَى أَرْوَاحِ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ وَالْمُؤْمِنَاتِ.

اللَّهُمَّ طَهِّرْ نِيَّاتِنَا مِنَ الرِّيَاءِ وَالْغِلِّ وَالْعُدْوَانِ،  
وَاجْعَلْ وَلَاءَنَا لِمُحَمَّدٍ وَآلِ مُحَمَّدٍ وَلَاءَ رَحْمَةٍ وَثَبَاتٍ وَتُقًى،  
وَاجْعَلْ بَرَاءَتَنَا مِنَ الظُّلْمِ بَرَاءَةً إِلَيْكَ، لَا ظُلْمَ فِيهَا وَلَا فَسَادَ وَلَا أَذًى لِعَبِيدِكَ،  
وَاحْفَظِ الطُّرُقَ وَالْمَسَالِكَ وَالْمَرَاكِبَ وَالْمَارَّةَ مِنَ الضَّرَرِ وَالْفَزَعِ،  
وَارْحَمْنَا بِرَحْمَتِكَ يَا أَرْحَمَ الرَّاحِمِينَ.

اللَّهُمَّ صَلِّ عَلَى مُحَمَّدٍ وَآلِ مُحَمَّدٍ.

---

## 拉斯塔法里 Nyahbinghi

Jah Rastafari.  
His Imperial Majesty Emperor Haile Selassie I,  
King of Kings, Lord of Lords,  
Conquering Lion of the Tribe of Judah,  
Elect of God, Light of this world.

I and I come before Jah in truth and livity.  
I and I lift up this journey before Jah Rastafari.  
I and I speak for safe going out and safe coming in,  
for a road kept from danger, distress, confusion, and harm,  
for every peril to be turned aside,  
and for peaceful arrival under Jah guidance.  
Let righteousness stand upon the way.  
Let clean heart, clean word, and clean works be found in I and I.

The LORD is my shepherd; I shall not want.  
He maketh me to lie down in green pastures:  
he leadeth me beside the still waters.  
He restoreth my soul:  
he leadeth me in the paths of righteousness for his name's sake.  
Yea, though I walk through the valley of the shadow of death,  
I will fear no evil:  
for thou art with me;  
thy rod and thy staff they comfort me.  
Thou preparest a table before me in the presence of mine enemies:  
thou anointest my head with oil;  
my cup runneth over.  
Surely goodness and mercy shall follow me all the days of my life:  
and I will dwell in the house of the LORD for ever.

Jah Rastafari.  
Jah Rastafari.  
Jah Rastafari.

Let God arise, let his enemies be scattered:  
let them also that hate him flee before him.  
As smoke is driven away, so drive them away:  
as wax melteth before the fire,  
so let the wicked perish at the presence of God.  
But let the righteous be glad;  
let them rejoice before God:  
yea, let them exceedingly rejoice.  
Sing unto God, sing praises to his name:  
extol him that rideth upon the heavens by his name JAH,  
and rejoice before him.

Jah is I shepherd, I shall not want.  
Jah is I light and I salvation.  
Jah Rastafari, ever living, ever faithful, ever sure.  
Jah guide I and I upon the road.  
Jah keep I and I from accident, fear, and confusion.  
Jah carry I and I through the valley and over the mountain.  
Babylon trouble gone down, gone down, gone down.  
Jah kingdom rise in Zion.

I and I ask Jah to guide this travel in peace.  
Keep I and I from reckless counsel, vain haste, anger, and disorder.  
Turn aside the snare, the danger, the delay, and the hidden trouble.  
Let no harm be wished upon any soul;  
only remove the obstacle and make the way righteous.  
Set I and I feet upon Zion way.  
Let truth, justice, mercy, and livity remain.

I will lift up mine eyes unto the hills,  
from whence cometh my help.  
My help cometh from the LORD,  
which made heaven and earth.  
He will not suffer thy foot to be moved:  
he that keepeth thee will not slumber.  
Behold, he that keepeth Israel  
shall neither slumber nor sleep.  
The LORD is thy keeper:  
the LORD is thy shade upon thy right hand.  
The sun shall not smite thee by day,  
nor the moon by night.  
The LORD shall preserve thee from all evil:  
he shall preserve thy soul.  
The LORD shall preserve thy going out and thy coming in  
from this time forth, and even for evermore.

Give thanks and praises unto the Most High Jah Rastafari.  
Let this prayer remain in righteousness, clean heart, and humble livity.  
Let all chant rise in peace, unity, and reverence before Jah,  
with no confusion, no vanity, no harm, and no Babylon disorder.  
Qədamawi Ḫaylä Śəllase.  
Jah Rastafari.  
Amen.  
Selah.

---

## שומרונים

בשם יהוה אלהינו, אל עולם.

שמע ישראל: יהוה אלהינו יהוה אחד.  
ואהבת את יהוה אלהיך בכל לבבך ובכל נפשך ובכל מאדך.

יהוה ימלך לעלם ועד.  
בהר גריזים בחר יהוה לשכן שמו שם.

יהוה אלהי אברהם אלהי יצחק ואלהי יעקב,  
שמר נא את היוצאים לדרך הזאת בשלום.  
הוליכם בדרך ישרה ובטוחה,  
הסר פחד ומכשול מעל נתיבם,  
והפוך סכנה לשלום, צרה לרוחה, וחשכה לאור.  
אל תתן רגלם למוט, ויהי בואם בשלום אל מקום חפצם.  
לא רעת אדם נבקש, כי אם שמירה, רחמים, וחיים בשלום.

יברכך יהוה וישמרך.  
יאר יהוה פניו אליך ויחנך.  
ישא יהוה פניו אליך וישם לך שלום.

יהוה הוא האלהים; תורת משה אמת; וברכת הר גריזים לפניך.  
לך לבדך התפלה והשבח, ואין לנו אלהים אחרים.

אמן.

---

## 雅兹迪信仰

Bi navê Xwedêyê mezin û dilovan.

Şehda dînê min:  
Ez şehdê dînê xwe dikim.  
Xwedê yek e.  
Tawisê Melek heq e.  
Şêx Adî şîrê Xwedê ye.  
Siltan Êzîd padşahê min e.

Sebeha:  
Subhanê Xwedê.  
Subhanê Tawisê Melek.  
Subhanê Şêx Adî.  
Subhanê Êzîdê Sor.

Ya Xwedê,  
xêr û silametî li ser vê rêwîtîyê binivîse.  
Rê rast be, dil aram be, gav bi ronahî be.  
Ji xeter, şer, nexweşî, tarî û bêçaretiyê biparêze.  
Eger asteng derkeve, bi rehmeta te bibe hêsanî;  
eger tengasî nêzîk bibe, bi destê xêrê bibe rizgarî.  
Bi bereketa Tawisê Melek,  
rê bê tirs be, derî vekirî be,  
û gihîştin bi silametî û aramî be.

Em xwe dispêrin Xwedêyê mezin,  
bi dilê pak, bi rêya rast,  
bê ziyan ji av, agir, ax û bayê,  
bê ziyan ji kesekî û bê daxwaza şer.

Qebûl be li ber dergehê Xwedê.  
Amîn.

---

## یارسان / اهل حق

Yā Ḥaqq.  
یا حق.

Niyyat-e īn duʿā va yād kardān:  
barā-ye safar-e bī-khatar, rāh-e hamvār, dūrī az āfat va sakhtī,  
rasīdan be maqṣad dar salāmat va ārāmī,  
dar rāh-e Yārī,  
bā pākī, rāstī, nīstī, riḍā.

Pākī, rāstī, nīstī, riḍā.  
پاکی، راستی، نیستی، رضا.

Yā Ḥaqq, Yā Ḥaqq, Yā Ḥaqq.  
یا حق، یا حق، یا حق.

Dar īn yād-e jam,  
niyāz-e del barā-ye negahbānī dar safar ast;  
har gām rā be nūr-e Ḥaqq mī-sepārīm,  
har bīm rā be rāstī va riḍā farū mī-nehīm,  
har band va sakhtī rā bī-āzār az rāh bardār,  
tā khatar be āsānī gardad  
va rāh be salāmat anjām pazīrad.

Yā Ḥaqq.  
یا حق.

Be yād-e kalām-e ʿalānī va āvāz-e tanbūr-e pāk,  
del-hā rā ham-sadā mī-konīm:  
Ḥaqq negah dārad, Yārī hamrāh ast,  
rāh dar pākī roshan,  
qadam dar rāstī ustuvār,  
del dar nīstī farūtan,  
jān dar riḍā ārām.

Yā Ḥaqq.  
Yā Sultān Sahāk.  
یا حق.  
یا سلطان سهاک.

Har che hast az Ḥaqq ast,  
har che mī-khāhīm be Ḥaqq mī-sepārīm:  
safar rā bī-khatar gardān,  
rāh rā az āfat va ranj dūr dār,  
dargozar az girih-hā va tangī-hā,  
va be mehr-e Ḥaqq, salāmat va āsāyish dar maqṣad bakhsh.

Aval o ākhar Yār.  
اول و آخر یار.

Be nām-hā-ye āshkār qāneʿīm,  
rāz-e jam va kalām-e poshīdeh rā be ahl-e rāh mī-sepārīm;  
bī-daʿvā, bī-bāzār, bī-āzār,  
dar pākī, rāstī, nīstī, riḍā mī-mānīm.

Yā Ḥaqq, Yā Ḥaqq, Yā Ḥaqq.  
یا حق، یا حق، یا حق.

---

## الدعاء والزيارة الإمامية

بِسْمِ اللهِ الرَّحْمٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ

اَلْحَمْدُ لِلّٰهِ رَبِّ الْعَالَمِينَ، الرَّحْمٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ، مَالِكِ يَوْمِ الدِّينِ.  
إِيَّاكَ نَعْبُدُ وَإِيَّاكَ نَسْتَعِينُ.  
اِهْدِنَا الصِّرَاطَ الْمُسْتَقِيمَ، صِرَاطَ الَّذِينَ أَنْعَمْتَ عَلَيْهِمْ، غَيْرِ الْمَغْضُوبِ عَلَيْهِمْ وَلَا الضَّالِّينَ.

اَللّٰهُمَّ صَلِّ عَلَى مُحَمَّدٍ وَآلِ مُحَمَّدٍ، كَمَا صَلَّيْتَ عَلَى إِبْرَاهِيمَ وَآلِ إِبْرَاهِيمَ، إِنَّكَ حَمِيدٌ مَجِيدٌ.

اَللّٰهُمَّ إِنِّي أُقِرُّ لَكَ بِالتَّوْحِيدِ، وَأَشْهَدُ أَنْ لا إِلٰهَ إِلَّا اللهُ وَحْدَهُ لا شَرِيكَ لَهُ، وَأَشْهَدُ أَنَّ مُحَمَّدًا عَبْدُهُ وَرَسُولُهُ، وَأَنَّ عَلِيًّا وَلِيُّ اللهِ، وَأَنَّ الْأَئِمَّةَ مِنْ وُلْدِهِ حُجَجُ اللهِ.

رَبَّنَا ظَلَمْنَا أَنْفُسَنَا، وَإِنْ لَمْ تَغْفِرْ لَنَا وَتَرْحَمْنَا لَنَكُونَنَّ مِنَ الْخَاسِرِينَ.  
اَللّٰهُمَّ اغْفِرْ لِيَ الذُّنُوبَ الَّتِي تَهْتِكُ الْعِصَمَ، اَللّٰهُمَّ اغْفِرْ لِيَ الذُّنُوبَ الَّتِي تُنْزِلُ النِّقَمَ، اَللّٰهُمَّ اغْفِرْ لِيَ الذُّنُوبَ الَّتِي تُغَيِّرُ النِّعَمَ، اَللّٰهُمَّ اغْفِرْ لِيَ الذُّنُوبَ الَّتِي تَحْبِسُ الدُّعَاءَ، اَللّٰهُمَّ اغْفِرْ لِيَ الذُّنُوبَ الَّتِي تُنْزِلُ الْبَلَاءَ.

اَللّٰهُمَّ إِنِّي أَتَوَجَّهُ إِلَيْكَ بِنَبِيِّكَ نَبِيِّ الرَّحْمَةِ مُحَمَّدٍ صَلَّى اللهُ عَلَيْهِ وَآلِهِ، وَبِأَهْلِ بَيْتِهِ الطَّيِّبِينَ الطَّاهِرِينَ.  
يَا وَجِيهًا عِنْدَ اللهِ، اِشْفَعْ لَنَا عِنْدَ اللهِ.  
اَللّٰهُمَّ بِحَقِّ مُحَمَّدٍ وَآلِ مُحَمَّدٍ، اقْبَلْ دُعَاءَنَا، وَاسْمَعْ نِدَاءَنَا، وَاقْضِ حَاجَتَنَا بِرَحْمَتِكَ.

السَّلَامُ عَلَيْكَ يَا رَسُولَ اللهِ، السَّلَامُ عَلَيْكَ يَا أَمِيرَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ، السَّلَامُ عَلَيْكِ يَا فَاطِمَةُ الزَّهْرَاءُ، السَّلَامُ عَلَى الْحَسَنِ وَالْحُسَيْنِ، السَّلَامُ عَلَى عَلِيِّ بْنِ الْحُسَيْنِ، السَّلَامُ عَلَى مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ عَلِيٍّ، السَّلَامُ عَلَى جَعْفَرِ بْنِ مُحَمَّدٍ، السَّلَامُ عَلَى مُوسَى بْنِ جَعْفَرٍ، السَّلَامُ عَلَى عَلِيِّ بْنِ مُوسَى، السَّلَامُ عَلَى مُحَمَّدِ بْنِ عَلِيٍّ، السَّلَامُ عَلَى عَلِيِّ بْنِ مُحَمَّدٍ، السَّلَامُ عَلَى الْحَسَنِ بْنِ عَلِيٍّ، السَّلَامُ عَلَى الْحُجَّةِ بْنِ الْحَسَنِ.

اَللّٰهُ لَا إِلٰهَ إِلَّا هُوَ الْحَيُّ الْقَيُّومُ، لَا تَأْخُذُهُ سِنَةٌ وَلَا نَوْمٌ، لَهُ مَا فِي السَّمَاوَاتِ وَمَا فِي الْأَرْضِ، مَنْ ذَا الَّذِي يَشْفَعُ عِنْدَهُ إِلَّا بِإِذْنِهِ، يَعْلَمُ مَا بَيْنَ أَيْدِيهِمْ وَمَا خَلْفَهُمْ، وَلَا يُحِيطُونَ بِشَيْءٍ مِنْ عِلْمِهِ إِلَّا بِمَا شَاءَ، وَسِعَ كُرْسِيُّهُ السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالْأَرْضَ، وَلَا يَئُودُهُ حِفْظُهُمَا، وَهُوَ الْعَلِيُّ الْعَظِيمُ.

سُبْحَانَ الَّذِي سَخَّرَ لَنَا هٰذَا وَمَا كُنَّا لَهُ مُقْرِنِينَ، وَإِنَّا إِلَىٰ رَبِّنَا لَمُنْقَلِبُونَ.

اَللّٰهُمَّ إِنَّا نَسْأَلُكَ فِي هٰذَا السَّفَرِ حِفْظًا مِنْ عِنْدِكَ، وَسَتْرًا مِنْ لَدُنْكَ، وَتَيْسِيرًا لِلطَّرِيقِ، وَسَلَامَةً فِي الذَّهَابِ وَالإِيَابِ.  
اَللّٰهُمَّ اصْرِفْ عَنِ الطَّرِيقِ كُلَّ بَلَاءٍ وَخَطَرٍ وَحَادِثٍ وَفَزَعٍ، وَاجْعَلْ كُلَّ عُسْرٍ يُسْرًا، وَكُلَّ ضِيقٍ فَرَجًا، وَكُلَّ خَوْفٍ أَمْنًا، وَأَوْصِلْنَا إِلَى الْمَقْصِدِ سَالِمِينَ غَانِمِينَ بِفَضْلِكَ يَا أَرْحَمَ الرَّاحِمِينَ.  
اَللّٰهُمَّ لا نَسْأَلُكَ ضَرَرًا لِأَحَدٍ مِنْ خَلْقِكَ، وَلٰكِنْ نَسْأَلُكَ أَنْ تَرْفَعَ الْمَانِعَ، وَتَكْفِيَ الْأَذَى، وَتَجْعَلَ الْعَاقِبَةَ خَيْرًا.

لَا إِلٰهَ إِلَّا أَنْتَ سُبْحَانَكَ إِنِّي كُنْتُ مِنَ الظَّالِمِينَ.  
حَسْبُنَا اللهُ وَنِعْمَ الْوَكِيلُ.

قُلْ هُوَ اللهُ أَحَدٌ، اللهُ الصَّمَدُ، لَمْ يَلِدْ وَلَمْ يُولَدْ، وَلَمْ يَكُنْ لَهُ كُفُوًا أَحَدٌ.  
قُلْ أَعُوذُ بِرَبِّ الْفَلَقِ، مِنْ شَرِّ مَا خَلَقَ، وَمِنْ شَرِّ غَاسِقٍ إِذَا وَقَبَ، وَمِنْ شَرِّ النَّفَّاثَاتِ فِي الْعُقَدِ، وَمِنْ شَرِّ حَاسِدٍ إِذَا حَسَدَ.  
قُلْ أَعُوذُ بِرَبِّ النَّاسِ، مَلِكِ النَّاسِ، إِلٰهِ النَّاسِ، مِنْ شَرِّ الْوَسْوَاسِ الْخَنَّاسِ، الَّذِي يُوَسْوِسُ فِي صُدُورِ النَّاسِ، مِنَ الْجِنَّةِ وَالنَّاسِ.

اَللّٰهُمَّ كُنْ لِوَلِيِّكَ الْحُجَّةِ بْنِ الْحَسَنِ، صَلَوَاتُكَ عَلَيْهِ وَعَلَى آبَائِهِ، فِي هٰذِهِ السَّاعَةِ وَفِي كُلِّ سَاعَةٍ، وَلِيًّا وَحَافِظًا وَقَائِدًا وَنَاصِرًا وَدَلِيلًا وَعَيْنًا، حَتَّى تُسْكِنَهُ أَرْضَكَ طَوْعًا، وَتُمَتِّعَهُ فِيهَا طَوِيلًا.

اَللّٰهُمَّ اغْفِرْ لِلْمُؤْمِنِينَ وَالْمُؤْمِنَاتِ، وَالْمُسْلِمِينَ وَالْمُسْلِمَاتِ، الْأَحْيَاءِ مِنْهُمْ وَالْأَمْوَاتِ، وَاجْعَلْ ثَوَابَ مَا قُرِئَ وَدُعِيَ نُورًا وَرَحْمَةً وَأَمْنًا لِعِبَادِكَ الصَّالِحِينَ.

رَبَّنَا تَقَبَّلْ مِنَّا إِنَّكَ أَنْتَ السَّمِيعُ الْعَلِيمُ، وَتُبْ عَلَيْنَا إِنَّكَ أَنْتَ التَّوَّابُ الرَّحِيمُ.  
اَللّٰهُمَّ صَلِّ عَلَى مُحَمَّدٍ وَآلِ مُحَمَّدٍ، وَاجْعَلْ تَوَسُّلَنَا بِهِمْ إِلَيْكَ، وَحِفْظَنَا مِنْكَ، وَرَجَاءَنَا فِيكَ، وَاعْتِمَادَنَا عَلَيْكَ وَحْدَكَ، لا إِلٰهَ إِلَّا أَنْتَ.  
سُبْحَانَ رَبِّكَ رَبِّ الْعِزَّةِ عَمَّا يَصِفُونَ، وَسَلَامٌ عَلَى الْمُرْسَلِينَ، وَالْحَمْدُ لِلّٰهِ رَبِّ الْعَالَمِينَ.

---

## AMORC 玫瑰十字会

Pax Profunda.

God of my Heart, God of my Realization,  
I enter the silence in humility, sincerity, and service.

May the Cosmic attune the Inner Self  
to Light, Life, and Love.

Lux. Vita. Amor.

For protection in travel,  
may every journey be peaceful, orderly, and free from harm.  
May all roads, crossings, vehicles, and moments of passage  
be guided by lawful protection, clear judgment, harmony, and the highest good.

Let danger be averted without injury to any being.  
Let difficulty be transformed into safety.  
Let confusion give way to wisdom,  
and let the journey reach its rightful destination in peace.

AUM.  
AUM.  
AUM.

May peace profound abide upon the way.  
May wisdom guide every action and decision.  
May harmony be restored where harmony is rightful.  
May all selfishness, coercion, fear, and harmful intention be dissolved.

Pax Profunda.

Lux, Vita, Amor.

AUM.

---

## Aurum Solis

In stillness and in purity I stand within the Light of the Ogdoadic Star.

Agios ho Theos,  
Agios Ischyros,  
Agios Athanatos,  
eleēson hēmas.

Deo Duce, Comite Ferro.

Let the work be established in the matter of protection upon the road: that the journey may be peaceful and rightly ordered, without peril or hardship, that danger be turned aside and transformed, and that arrival be safe.

IAO.  
AGATHOS DAIMŌN.  
IAO.

Holy and deathless Light, source and crown of the work, receive this vow:  
I seek safe passage, clear way, calm movement, and harmonious arrival without falsehood, without malice, and without violation of the rightful will of another.

Agios ho Theos,  
Agios Ischyros,  
Agios Athanatos,  
eleēson hēmas.

Let the wards stand about this journey: before and behind, at the right hand and the left, above and beneath, within and without.

Deo Duce, Comite Ferro.  
Agios ho Theos, Agios Ischyros, Agios Athanatos, eleēson hēmas.

Let confusion be clarified, obstruction be passed in peace, harm be turned from its course, and every hazard be brought to harmlessness under the governance of the Divine Mind.

IAO. IAO. IAO.

The word is spoken, the measure is sealed, and the force is returned to its proper sphere.

Agios ho Theos,  
Agios Ischyros,  
Agios Athanatos,  
eleēson hēmas.

I withdraw all unruly intention; I release all force not rightly ordered; I return every power invoked to its proper sphere in peace and harmony.

Deo Duce, Comite Ferro.  
IAO.

Let the wards be closed in purity, the heart restored to stillness, and the Light remain without compulsion or excess.

Agios ho Theos,  
Agios Ischyros,  
Agios Athanatos,  
eleēson hēmas.

Fiat. Amen.

## 人智学 · 基督社区

Im Namen des Vaters und des Sohnes und des Heiligen Geistes. Amen.

In stiller Sammlung stehen wir vor Gott, dem Vater,  
durch Christus Jesus,  
im Licht des Heiligen Geistes.

Christus spricht:  
„Ich bin der Weg und die Wahrheit und das Leben.“

Für die bevorstehende Reise legen wir dieses Anliegen nicht als Zwang,  
sondern als Opfer des Herzens vor den Christus:  
Möge der Weg in Wachheit, Frieden und rechter Ordnung geschehen;  
mögen Gefahr und Verwirrung abgewendet werden;  
möge, was schwer oder unheilvoll werden könnte,  
durch Wahrheit, Besonnenheit und schützende Gnade gewandelt werden;  
möge die Ankunft in Frieden geschehen.

Vater unser im Himmel,  
geheiligt werde dein Name.  
Dein Reich komme.  
Dein Wille geschehe,  
wie im Himmel, so auf Erden.  
Unser tägliches Brot gib uns heute.  
Und vergib uns unsere Schuld,  
wie auch wir vergeben unsern Schuldigern.  
Und führe uns nicht in Versuchung,  
sondern erlöse uns von dem Bösen.  
Denn dein ist das Reich  
und die Kraft  
und die Herrlichkeit  
in Ewigkeit.  
Amen.

Πάτερ ἡμῶν ὁ ἐν τοῖς οὐρανοῖς·  
ἁγιασθήτω τὸ ὄνομά σου·  
ἐλθέτω ἡ βασιλεία σου·  
γενηθήτω τὸ θέλημά σου,  
ὡς ἐν οὐρανῷ καὶ ἐπὶ γῆς·  
τὸν ἄρτον ἡμῶν τὸν ἐπιούσιον  
δὸς ἡμῖν σήμερον·  
καὶ ἄφες ἡμῖν τὰ ὀφειλήματα ἡμῶν,  
ὡς καὶ ἡμεῖς ἀφήκαμεν τοῖς ὀφειλέταις ἡμῶν·  
καὶ μὴ εἰσενέγκῃς ἡμᾶς εἰς πειρασμόν,  
ἀλλὰ ῥῦσαι ἡμᾶς ἀπὸ τοῦ πονηροῦ.  
Amen.

Nicht unser Wille,  
sondern dein Wille geschehe.

Was mit diesem Weg verbunden ist,  
sei dem Christus übergeben.  
Was ungeordnet, gefährlich oder dunkel ist,  
werde nicht durch unseren Zwang,  
sondern durch Wahrheit, Freiheit und Liebe vor Gott geordnet.

Im Frieden Christi.  
Amen.

---

## BOTA

In the One Life, centered in silence, I stand in reverence before the Light.

Holy art Thou, Lord of the Universe.  
Holy art Thou, Whom Nature hath not formed.  
Holy art Thou, the Vast and the Mighty One.  
Lord of the Light and of the Darkness.

אהיה  
Ehyeh.

יהוה אלהים  
YHVH Elohim.

יהוה אלוה ודעת  
YHVH Eloah ve-Daath.

אל  
El.

אלהים גבור  
Elohim Gibor.

יהוה צבאות  
YHVH Tzabaoth.

אלהים צבאות  
Elohim Tzabaoth.

שדי אל חי  
Shaddai El Chai.

אדני מלך  
Adonai Melekh.

אדני הארץ  
Adonai ha-Aretz.

Before the One Life, I set forth this petition:  
愿出行平安顺利，一路无险无难；若有危难，愿化险为夷；愿行程秩序分明、道路清明、身心安稳，平安抵达。

Let every word concerning this journey be ordered by Wisdom, measured by Understanding, balanced by Beauty, and grounded in righteous manifestation.  
Let no clause of this prayer bind, coerce, diminish, or violate any soul.  
Let the hidden pattern behind this journey be aligned with the Holy Names and with the true good of all concerned.

אהיה יהוה צבאות אלהים גבור  
Ehyeh. YHVH Tzabaoth. Elohim Gibor.

Ateh.  
Malkuth.  
ve-Geburah.  
ve-Gedulah.  
le-Olam.  
Amen.

Holy art Thou, Lord of the Universe.  
Holy art Thou, Whom Nature hath not formed.  
Holy art Thou, the Vast and the Mighty One.  
Lord of the Light and of the Darkness.

Amen.

In the One Life, let every desire be purified in the Light.  
Let no force be turned toward coercion, vengeance, display, or harm.  
Let the Holy Names return all wandering thought to reverence, clarity, and peace.  
Let the way be guarded in righteousness, and let the traveler abide in the true order of the One Life.

Amen.

## 祆教 / 琐罗亚斯德教

### —— 1. Padyab 洁净立界 / Khshnaothra ——

Khshnaothra Ahurahe Mazdāo.

Ashem Vohū vahishtem astī,  
ushtā astī ushtā ahmāi,  
hyat ashāi vahishtāi ashem.

### —— 2. Niyyat / Dibache ——

Pa nām i yazdān, Ohrmazd Khodāe awazūnī.  
愿此行平安顺利，一路无险无难；若遇障碍，愿在 Asha 中化险为夷，身心守护，安然抵达。  
Humata, hukhta, hvarshta andar Asha.

### —— 3. Kem Na Mazda / Kusti 守护 ——

Kêm-nâ mazdâ mavaitê pâyûm dadå,  
hyat mâ dregvå dîdareshatâ aênanghê,  
anyêm thwahmât âthrascâ mananghascâ,  
ýayå shyaothanâish ashem thraoshtâ ahurâ,  
tãm môi dãstvãm daênayâi frâvaocâ.

Kê verethrem-jâ thwâ pôi sêñghâ ýôi heñtî,  
cithrâ môi dãm ahûmbish ratûm cizhdî,  
at hôi vohû seraoshô jañtû mananghâ,  
mazdâ ahmâi ýahmâi vashî kahmâicît.

Pâta-nô tbishyañtat pairi mazdåsca ârmaitishca speñtasca,  
nase daêvî druxsh, nase daêvô-cithre, nase daêvô-frakarshte, nase daêvô-fradâiti,  
apa druxsh nase, apa druxsh dvâra, apa druxsh vînase, apâxedhre apa-nasyehe,  
mâ mereñcainîsh gaêthå astvaitîsh ashahe,  
nemascâ ýâ ârmaitish îzhâcâ.

Ashem Vohū vahishtem astī,  
ushtā astī ushtā ahmāi,  
hyat ashāi vahishtāi ashem.

### —— 4. Ahura Mazda Khodāe / Patet 悔净 ——

Ahura-Mazda khodāe, Ahereman awā-dashãn, dur avāz dāshtār, zad shekasteh bād.

Ahura-Mazda khodāe, az hamā gunāh patet pashemānum,  
az harvastīn dushmata duzhukhta duzhvarshta,  
mem pa getī manīd, oem goft, oem kard, oem jast, oem būn būd ested.

Az ān gunāh, manashnī gavashnī kunashnī, tanī ravānī getī minōānī,  
okhe awākhsh pashemān, pa se gavashnī pa patet hom.

### —— 5. Jasa me Avanghe Mazda / Fravarane ——

Jasa me avanghe Mazda. Jasa me avanghe Mazda. Jasa me avanghe Mazda.

Mazdayasnō ahmī, Mazdayasnō Zarathushtrish fravarānē āstūtascā fravaretascā.  
Āstuyē humatem manō, āstuyē hūkhtem vachō, āstuyē hvarshtem shyaothanem.  
Āstuyē daēnām vanguhīm Māzdayasnīm,  
fraspāyaokhedhrām, nidhāsnaithishem, khvaētvadathām ashaonīm,  
yā hāitināmchā būshyeintināmchā mazishtāchā vahishtāchā sraēshtāchā,  
yā āhūirish Zarathushtrish.

Ahurāi Mazdāi vīspā vohū chinahmī.  
Aēshā astī daēnayāo Māzdayasnōish āstūitish.

Ashem Vohū vahishtem astī,  
ushtā astī ushtā ahmāi,  
hyat ashāi vahishtāi ashem.

### —— 6. 核心 Manthra ——

Yathā ahū vairyō, athā ratush ashāt-chit hachā,  
vanghēush dazdā mananghō, shyaothananām anghēush Mazdāi,  
xshathremchā Ahurāi ā, yim drigubyō dadat vāstārem.

Ashem Vohū vahishtem astī,  
ushtā astī ushtā ahmāi,  
hyat ashāi vahishtāi ashem.

Yenghē hātām āat yesnē paiti vanghō,  
Mazdāo Ahurō vaēthā ashāt hachā,  
yāonghāmchā tāschā tāschā yazamaidē.

### —— 7. 正行：Sraosha / Warharan 守护出行 ——

Sraoshahe ashyehe, takhmahe, tanu-manthrahe, darshi-draosh ahuiryehe,  
khshnaothra yasnaicha vahmaicha khshnaothraicha frasastayaecha.

Yasnemcha vahmemcha aojascha zavarecha āfrīnāmi,  
Verethraghnahe Ahuradhātahe vanaintyāoscha uparatātō.

Yathā ahū vairyō, athā ratush ashāt-chit hachā,  
vanghēush dazdā mananghō, shyaothananām anghēush Mazdāi,  
xshathremchā Ahurāi ā, yim drigubyō dadat vāstārem.

Ashem Vohū vahishtem astī,  
ushtā astī ushtā ahmāi,  
hyat ashāi vahishtāi ashem.

### —— 8. Ahmai Raeshcha / Doa Tan-Dorosti 祝祷 ——

Ahmāi raēshcha khvarenanghacha,  
Ahmāi tanvō drvatātem,  
Ahmāi tanvō vazdvārē,  
Ahmāi tanvō verethrem,  
Ahmāi ishtim pourush-khathrem,  
Ahmāi asnāmchit frazantim,  
Ahmāi darekham darekho-jītim,  
Ahmāi vahishtem ahum ashaonām,  
raochanghem vispō-khathrem.

Tandarosti, dorosti, zor, niru, khoreh, awazuni,  
ravāni shād, tan dorost, geti minōānī andar Asha.

Ahmāi raēshcha; Hazanghrem; Jasa me Avanghe Mazda; Kerfeh Mozd.

### —— 9. 回结 / Asha 守护净结 ——

Ahura-Mazda khodāe, az hamā gunāh patet pashemānum.  
Āstuyē humatem manō, āstuyē hūkhtem vachō, āstuyē hvarshtem shyaothanem.  
Humata, hukhta, hvarshta andar Asha.

Yathā ahū vairyō, athā ratush ashāt-chit hachā,  
vanghēush dazdā mananghō, shyaothananām anghēush Mazdāi,  
xshathremchā Ahurāi ā, yim drigubyō dadat vāstārem.

Ashem Vohū vahishtem astī,  
ushtā astī ushtā ahmāi,  
hyat ashāi vahishtāi ashem.

---

## 混沌魔法（Chaos Magick）

I banish from this working all obsession, confusion, and reflected desire.  
I banish every needless snare, accident, delay, danger, and fear from the road.

Neither-neither.  
I am not this.  
I am not that.  
No belief is true.  
Everything is permitted.

KIA.  
ZOS.  
KIA.  
ZOS.

This is my will:  
The journey proceeds safely and smoothly; all danger is turned aside, all difficulty becomes a way through, and arrival is peaceful and unharmed.

The sign is made:  
SAFE-ROAD-SIGIL.

The desire is bound into the sign.  
The sign is empty of words.  
The sign is full of will.

IAŌ.  
SABAŌ.  
ABRASAX.  
ZAZAS ZAZAS NASATANADA ZAZAS.  
IAŌ SABAŌ ABRASAX.

By gnosis, by silence, by the death of thought:  
SAFE-ROAD-SIGIL is launched.

It is done.  
It is forgotten.  
It is no longer mine.

HA.  
HA.  
HA.

The working is closed.  
The mask is removed.  
The road is only road.  
The body is only body.  
The breath returns to ordinary breath.  
The feet return to the earth.

The sign is released, dissolved, or destroyed.  
The desire is not watched.  
The result is not chased.  
The record remains:  
Safe passage working sealed and ended.

HA.  
HA.  
HA.

---

## 现代术士派（Cochranian、Sabbatic Craft）

In the name of the Old One,  
Master of the Crooked Path,  
Keeper of the hidden fire,  
we hallow this compass.

By stang, by stone, by thorn, by flame,  
by bone, by blood, by breath, by name,  
let this ring be whole;  
let no false word enter,  
let no oath be broken,  
let no secret be profaned.

Old One, hear the word set upon the road.  
The work is for protection in travel:  
may the going be safe and orderly,  
may the path be clear of needless peril,  
may danger be turned aside,  
may hardship be changed into safe passage,  
and may the journey come to its rightful arrival in peace.

No stolen oath is spoken here.  
No hidden word is claimed here.  
Only the open charm is set,  
only the rightful prayer is made.

Thorn before, thorn behind,  
thorn at the left, thorn at the right;  
by blackthorn, whitethorn, and the crooked bough,  
let the ward stand fast around the road.

Road before, road behind,  
gate before, gate behind;  
let the way be opened where it is rightful,  
let the way be closed where harm would enter,  
let wheel, foot, wing, and vessel keep true course,  
let confusion be stilled,  
let accident pass by,  
let delay become guidance,  
let fear become clear sight,  
let the traveler be brought safely through.

By stang, by stone, by thorn, by flame,  
by bone, by blood, by breath, by name,  
the word is spoken,  
the work is sealed,  
the compass is whole.

Old One, receive thanks.  
If any word has gone beyond its rightful bound,  
let it be withdrawn into silence.  
If any force has been stirred without need,  
let it be settled and sent in peace.  
Let the road be shut where it must be shut.  
Let the road be open where it must be open.  
Peace to the ring,  
peace to the dead,  
peace to the living.

So mote it be.

---

## 金色黎明

In the matter of safe and peaceable travel: may the way be clear, the passage guarded, all peril averted or transformed, and arrival be in safety and order.

Ateh.  
Malkuth.  
Ve-Geburah.  
Ve-Gedulah.  
Le-Olahm.

And in the Column shines the Six-rayed Star.

Ve-Gedulah.  
Le-Olahm.

## A∴A∴

Do what thou wilt shall be the whole of the Law.

I stand within the current of A∴A∴, setting this will toward safe and orderly travel: that the road be clear, the passage protected, all peril averted or transformed, and the arrival accomplished in peace; not for vanity, coercion, harm, or the disturbance of another will, but according to the True Will.

A ka dua  
Tuf ur biu  
Bi a'a chefu  
Dudu ner af an nuteru.

In the name of the Great Work, I banish from this place, this body, this vehicle, this road, and this course all confusion, obsession, falsehood, wandering force, negligence, and accident that is not in accord with the Work.

Ateh.  
Malkuth.  
Ve-Geburah.  
Ve-Gedulah.  
Le-Olahm, Amen.

YHVH.  
ADNI.  
AHIH.  
AGLA.

Before me Raphael;  
Behind me Gabriel;  
On my right hand Michael;  
On my left hand Auriel;  
For about me flames the Pentagram,  
And in the Column stands the Six-rayed Star.

Thee I invoke, the Bornless One.  
Thee, that didst create the Earth and the Heavens.  
Thee, that didst create the Night and the Day.  
Thee, that didst create the Darkness and the Light.  
Thou art Osorronophris: Whom no man hath seen at any time.

Hear me, not for domination, nor for the bending of another will, but that every force opposed to this lawful passage be dissolved, redirected, or rendered harmless under the True Will.

Holy Guardian Angel,  
not as an image of desire,  
not as a voice of confusion,  
not as a mask of fear,  
but as the Knowledge and Conversation appointed to the True Will:  
be present in the silence of the heart.

Guide the going forth.  
Guard the threshold, the road, the crossing, the air, the water, the wheel, the step, and the hour.  
Let haste be steadied, danger be foreseen, confusion be banished, and obstacle be passed without injury.  
Let no harm be wished upon any being; let the obstacle be removed, the danger turned aside, and the way made clear.  
Let the journey proceed without peril, without misfortune, without terror, and without loss.  
Let all hazards be transformed into safety, and let the arrival be peaceful.

Abrahadabra.  
Aumgn.

Love is the law, love under will.

Let the record of this working be true:  
work: protection of travel  
intention: safe, smooth, unharmed passage and peaceful arrival  
limit: no coercion, no injury, no violation of True Will  
witnessed sign or silence: to be recorded faithfully

Ateh.  
Malkuth.  
Ve-Geburah.  
Ve-Gedulah.  
Le-Olahm, Amen.

YHVH.  
ADNI.  
AHIH.  
AGLA.

Before me Raphael;  
Behind me Gabriel;  
On my right hand Michael;  
On my left hand Auriel;  
For about me flames the Pentagram,  
And in the Column stands the Six-rayed Star.

Ateh.  
Malkuth.  
Ve-Geburah.  
Ve-Gedulah.  
Le-Olahm, Amen.

Hail unto Thee who art Ra in Thy rising, even unto Thee who art Ra in Thy strength, who travellest over the Heavens in Thy bark at the Uprising of the Sun.  
Tahuti standeth in His splendour at the prow, and Ra-Hoor abideth at the helm.  
Hail unto Thee from the Abodes of Night.

Hail unto Thee who art Ahathoor in Thy triumphing, even unto Thee who art Ahathoor in Thy beauty, who travellest over the Heavens in Thy bark at the Mid-course of the Sun.  
Tahuti standeth in His splendour at the prow, and Ra-Hoor abideth at the helm.  
Hail unto Thee from the Abodes of Morning.

Hail unto Thee who art Tum in Thy setting, even unto Thee who art Tum in Thy joy, who travellest over the Heavens in Thy bark at the Down-going of the Sun.  
Tahuti standeth in His splendour at the prow, and Ra-Hoor abideth at the helm.  
Hail unto Thee from the Abodes of Day.

Hail unto Thee who art Khephra in Thy hiding, even unto Thee who art Khephra in Thy silence, who travellest over the Heavens in Thy bark at the Midnight Hour of the Sun.  
Tahuti standeth in His splendour at the prow, and Ra-Hoor abideth at the helm.  
Hail unto Thee from the Abodes of Evening.

Do what thou wilt shall be the whole of the Law.  
Love is the law, love under will.

## 共济会

Most holy and glorious Lord God,  
the Great Architect of the Universe,  
the Giver of all good gifts and graces:

Thou hast promised that where two or three are gathered together in Thy Name,  
Thou wilt be in the midst of them and bless them.

In Thy Name, and in reverence before Thy presence,  
we place this petition for safe and orderly travel:  
that the road may be made peaceable,  
the way kept clear of needless peril,  
and every danger, seen or unseen,  
be turned aside or brought to harmless issue,  
until the journey is completed in safety.

Grant that every thought, word, and act  
may be ordered by Wisdom,  
supported by Strength,  
and adorned with Beauty.

הִנֵּה מַה־טּוֹב וּמַה־נָּעִים  
שֶׁבֶת אַחִים גַּם־יָחַד׃

Let Brotherly Love, Relief, and Truth  
govern our hearts toward all whom we meet upon the way.  
Let no anger, vanity, unlawful gain, false witness,  
or betrayal of trust enter this work.

Direct this journey  
so that it may proceed in order, concord, and uprightness.  
Set the plumb-line of prudence before every step,  
the square of right conduct upon every decision,  
and the compass of temperance around every desire.  
May confusion be reduced to order,  
fear be steadied by trust,  
and obstruction give way to peace.

Keep us faithful to every lawful obligation,  
silent where silence is due,  
truthful where speech is required,  
and charitable toward all mankind.  
Preserve us from wrongful use of sacred forms,  
from pride, deceit, coercion, and vain display;  
let this supplication remain humble, public, peaceable,  
and directed only toward protection, virtue, and safe arrival.

May the Supreme Grand Master  
preside over this intention,  
until all travel is ended in peace  
and all work is closed in harmony.

So mote it be.

---

## 赫密士主义当代社团

[净化与定向]  
En sigē, eusebeia kai katharotēti histamai;  
ou kakōsai, ou biasasthai, ou apatēsai, ou harpasai boulomai.  
Genesthō hē euchē pros τὸ ἕν, νοῦς, λόγος, kai tēn hieran taxin.

[向一者与Nous发愿]  
Pros ton theion Noun trepomai;  
pausatō hē planē, orthōthētō hē gnōmē,  
mē hyperbētō ho logos tēn eusebeian.

[神圣呼语：Corpus Hermeticum XIII, Secret Hymn]  
Hagios ho Theos, ho Patēr tōn holōn.  
Hagios ho Theos, hou hē boulē teleitai tais idiais dynameisin.  
Hagios ho Theos, hos gnōsthēnai bouletai kai ginōsketai tois idiois.

Hagios ei, ho logō systēsas ta onta.  
Hagios ei, hou pasa physis eikōn ephu.  
Hagios ei, hon hē physis ouk emorphōsen.  
Hagios ei, ho pasēs dynameōs ischyroteros.  
Hagios ei, ho pantos hyperechōn.  
Hagios ei, ho kreittōn epainou.

[陈明所愿]  
愿出行平安顺利，一路无险无难；若遇险阻，愿化险为夷；愿道路清明、身心安定、判断明智，平安抵达。愿此护持不侵害他人自由、尊严与正当边界。

[感恩]  
Ouk epitassō tō theiō; en eusebeia legō, akouō, kai epanorthoumai.  
Charis tō Heni, charis tō Nōi, charis tō Logō,  
hoti phōs, taxis, sōphrosynē kai phylakē phaneroutai.

[回向与静默]  
Hosa agatha, hosa kathara, hosa sōtēria ek tēs euchēs tautēs genētai,  
anakeisthō tē hierā taxei, tō agathō, kai tē sigē.  
En katharotēti teleiousthō; en eusebeia menētō; en eucharistiā pausasthō.  
Ei phobos ē tarachē anistētai, hē klēsis pauesthō,  
kai monē charis en sigē legesthō.

Sigē. Nous. Logos. Hen.

---

## 玫瑰十字 Lectorium Rosicrucianum

**[静默归心]**

Silentium.

In lumine interiore cor se colligat;  
in quiete mens desistat a timore, a vi, a dominatione.

**[承认真实意向]**

愿出行平安顺利，一路无险无难；若遇险阻，愿化险为夷，平安抵达。

Non ad cogendum, non ad possidendum, non ad nocendum hoc petitur.  
Quod in me est confusum, cupidum, anxium aut violentum, in silentio cesset.  
Fiat iter rectum, sobrius animus, vigilans corpus, pax in via.

**[光明呼求]**

Lux vera, quae in tenebris lucet,  
dirige gressus, compone horas, averte imprudentiam,  
et in omni transitu custodi cor in veritate.

**[经文正行：Johannine Prologue / Oratio Dominica / Rosicrucian motto]**

In principio erat Verbum,  
et Verbum erat apud Deum,  
et Deus erat Verbum.  
Hoc erat in principio apud Deum.  
Omnia per ipsum facta sunt,  
et sine ipso factum est nihil, quod factum est.  
In ipso vita erat,  
et vita erat lux hominum;  
et lux in tenebris lucet,  
et tenebrae eam non comprehenderunt.

Pater noster, qui es in caelis,  
sanctificetur nomen tuum.  
Adveniat regnum tuum.  
Fiat voluntas tua, sicut in caelo et in terra.  
Panem nostrum quotidianum da nobis hodie.  
Et dimitte nobis debita nostra, sicut et nos dimittimus debitoribus nostris.  
Et ne nos inducas in tentationem,  
sed libera nos a malo.  
Amen.

Ad Rosam per Crucem;  
ad Crucem per Rosam.  
Deo gloria intacta.

**[放下自我意志]**

Non mea voluntas anxia, sed lumen veritatis praevaleat.  
Non peto signa, non voco spiritus, non impero alteri voluntati.  
Quod rectum est, aperiatur; quod periculosum est, pacifice avertatur;  
quod necesse est transire, cum prudentia et pace transeatur.

**[非强制性回向与封印]**

Sit hoc iter in pace, sine laesione cuiusquam, sine odio, sine iniuria.  
Pax ante me, pax post me, pax circa me;  
lux Verbi in corde, sobrietas in sensibus, rectitudo in opere.

Si qua intentio in me declinavit ad vim, ad avaritiam, ad invocationem obscuram,  
nunc revocetur, solvatur, et taceat.  
Redeo ad orationem puram:

Pater noster, qui es in caelis,  
sanctificetur nomen tuum.  
Adveniat regnum tuum.  
Fiat voluntas tua, sicut in caelo et in terra.  
Et ne nos inducas in tentationem,  
sed libera nos a malo.  
Amen.

Et lux in tenebris lucet,  
et tenebrae eam non comprehenderunt.

In silentio signetur.  
Amen.

---

## Reclaiming（Starhawk）

Ground of being, Earth below and within,  
I center in breath, body, and presence.  
I return to my body, to this moment, to the living Earth.

By my will, by my breath, by my truth,  
this circle is cast:  
a boundary of clarity, consent, and love.

East, powers of Air:  
breath, song, thought, and dawn,  
be present in this circle.

South, powers of Fire:  
will, courage, heat, and transformation,  
be present in this circle.

West, powers of Water:  
feeling, dream, grief, and healing,  
be present in this circle.

North, powers of Earth:  
body, root, stone, and bread,  
be present in this circle.

Goddess, immanent one,  
She who is within and around all beings,  
be present in this circle.

Air I am,  
Fire I am,  
Water, Earth, and Spirit I am.

For safe travel, for clear roads and steady passage,  
for a journey without danger or hardship,  
for every risk to be turned aside or transformed,  
for peaceful arrival in wholeness and ease,  
I raise this prayer.

She changes everything She touches,  
and everything She touches changes.

Let the way be opened in wisdom.  
Let confusion fall away.  
Let danger be seen before it ripens.  
Let harm be turned aside without harm to another.  
Let helpers appear, timing align, and the path be made clear.

This circle is whole.  
This boundary is clear.  
What serves love, justice, safety, and right passage may enter.  
What feeds harm, coercion, deceit, panic, or mischance is turned away.

Let coercion fall away.  
Let fear be named and released.  
Let power-over be undone.  
Let power-with arise.

---

## 东方圣殿骑士团（OTO）

Do what thou wilt shall be the whole of the Law.

I set forth my will in this prayer:  
for safe passage, clear roads, protection from peril, the turning aside of danger, and peaceful arrival.

I believe in one secret and ineffable LORD; and in one Star in the Company of Stars of whose fire we are created, and to which we shall return; and in one Father of Life, Mystery of Mystery, in His name CHAOS, the sole viceregent of the Sun upon the Earth; and in one Air the nourisher of all that breathes.

A ka dua  
Tuf ur biu  
Bi a'a chefu  
Dudu ner af an nuteru.

Unity uttermost showed!  
I adore the might of Thy breath,  
Supreme and terrible God,  
Who makest the gods and death  
To tremble before Thee:  
I, I adore thee!

Let this journey be ordered under Will.  
Let the path be opened in Light.  
Let all harm be driven far from the way.  
Let every danger be changed into passage, every obstruction into right turning, every uncertainty into clear arrival.

APO PANTOS KAKODAIMONOS.  
IO PAN, IO PAN PAN.  
IO ISCHUROS, IO ATHANATOS, IO ABROTOS, IO IAO.  
CHAIRE PHALLE, CHAIRE PAMPHAGE, CHAIRE PANGENETOR.  
HAGIOS, HAGIOS, HAGIOS IAO.

There is no part of me that is not of the gods.

Love is the law, love under will.

APO PANTOS KAKODAIMONOS.  
HAGIOS, HAGIOS, HAGIOS IAO.

---

## 玛丁主义（Martinism）

In nomine Patris, et Filii, et Spiritus Sancti. Amen.

Domine Deus aeterne, fons lucis, iustitiae et misericordiae,  
in silentio interioris templi cor nostrum ad Te convertimus.  
Domine Iesu Christe, Réparateur, lux vera quae in tenebris lucet,  
dirige cogitationem, verbum et actum nostrum,  
ut hoc iter sub providentia tua, sine superbia et sine violentia,  
ad pacem, ordinem et reditum in Te disponatur.

Miserere mei, Deus, secundum magnam misericordiam tuam.  
Et secundum multitudinem miserationum tuarum, dele iniquitatem meam.  
Amplius lava me ab iniquitate mea,  
et a peccato meo munda me.  
Cor mundum crea in me, Deus,  
et spiritum rectum innova in visceribus meis.  
Ne proicias me a facie tua,  
et Spiritum sanctum tuum ne auferas a me.  
Redde mihi laetitiam salutaris tui,  
et spiritu principali confirma me.

Asperges me, Domine, hyssopo, et mundabor;  
lavabis me, et super nivem dealbabor.

Pater noster, qui es in caelis,  
sanctificetur nomen tuum.  
Adveniat regnum tuum.  
Fiat voluntas tua, sicut in caelo et in terra.  
Panem nostrum quotidianum da nobis hodie.  
Et dimitte nobis debita nostra,  
sicut et nos dimittimus debitoribus nostris.  
Et ne nos inducas in tentationem,  
sed libera nos a malo. Amen.

In principio erat Verbum,  
et Verbum erat apud Deum,  
et Deus erat Verbum.  
Hoc erat in principio apud Deum.  
Omnia per ipsum facta sunt:  
et sine ipso factum est nihil, quod factum est.  
In ipso vita erat,  
et vita erat lux hominum:  
et lux in tenebris lucet,  
et tenebrae eam non comprehenderunt.

Qui habitat in adiutorio Altissimi,  
in protectione Dei caeli commorabitur.  
Dicet Domino: Susceptor meus es tu, et refugium meum;  
Deus meus, sperabo in eum.  
Quoniam ipse liberavit me de laqueo venantium,  
et a verbo aspero.  
Scapulis suis obumbrabit tibi,  
et sub pennis eius sperabis.  
Scuto circumdabit te veritas eius:  
non timebis a timore nocturno,  
a sagitta volante in die,  
a negotio perambulante in tenebris,  
ab incursu et daemonio meridiano.  
Angelis suis mandavit de te,  
ut custodiant te in omnibus viis tuis.  
In manibus portabunt te,  
ne forte offendas ad lapidem pedem tuum.

Domine, custodi exitum et introitum huius itineris.  
Averte pericula visibilia et invisibilia;  
quod asperum est, mitiga; quod confusum est, ordina;  
quod impedit pacem, dissolve in misericordia tua.  
Non petimus malum ulli creaturae,  
sed remotionem impedimentorum, illuminationem viae,  
prudentiam cordis, tutelam corporis,  
et adventum pacificum ad locum destinatum.  
Fiat voluntas tua.

Pax Christi, Réparateur, descendat super viam.  
Lux Verbi praecedat, misericordia comitetur,  
ordo divinus sequatur,  
et anima nostra in humilitate reintegretur ad Fontem.

Gloria Patri, et Filio, et Spiritui Sancto;  
sicut erat in principio, et nunc, et semper,  
et in saecula saeculorum. Amen.

Miserere mei, Deus, secundum magnam misericordiam tuam.  
Cor mundum crea in me, Deus,  
et spiritum rectum innova in visceribus meis.  

Pater noster, qui es in caelis,  
sanctificetur nomen tuum.  
Adveniat regnum tuum.  
Fiat voluntas tua, sicut in caelo et in terra.  
Panem nostrum quotidianum da nobis hodie.  
Et dimitte nobis debita nostra,  
sicut et nos dimittimus debitoribus nostris.  
Et ne nos inducas in tentationem,  
sed libera nos a malo. Amen.

---

## 神智学协会

In the name of the One Life, and for the good of the whole human family, this prayer is held for safe and harmonious travel: that the journey may be peaceful, free from danger and hardship, that peril may be turned aside, and that arrival may be secure; all within right human relations and the Plan of Love and Light.

From the point of Light within the Mind of God  
Let light stream forth into the minds of men.  
Let Light descend on Earth.

From the point of Love within the Heart of God  
Let love stream forth into the hearts of men.  
May Christ return to Earth.

From the centre where the Will of God is known  
Let purpose guide the little wills of men—  
The purpose which the Masters know and serve.

From the centre which we call the race of men  
Let the Plan of Love and Light work out  
And may it seal the door where evil dwells.

Let every path be illumined by Light, every decision held in Love, and every movement guided by Power rightly used.  
May fear, confusion, accident, obstruction, and all harmful influence be closed away without hatred, retaliation, or coercion.  
May the traveller pass in peace, meet timely help, avoid needless danger, and arrive safely.

Let Light and Love and Power restore the Plan on Earth.

May this need be held within Light, Love and Power; may no will be coerced; may no harm be returned; may no private gain stand above the good of the whole human family.  
May goodwill, freedom of thought, right human relations, and the service of all beings prevail.

---

## Spiritism · Kardecism（凯德克派）

Dieu tout-puissant, souverainement juste et bon,  
que ta volonté soit faite et non la nôtre.  
Si la demande que nous formons est utile à notre âme  
et conforme à ta loi, daigne l’accueillir.

Notre Père qui êtes aux cieux,  
que votre nom soit sanctifié;  
que votre règne arrive;  
que votre volonté soit faite sur la terre comme au ciel.  
Donnez-nous aujourd’hui notre pain de chaque jour;  
pardonnez-nous nos offenses,  
comme nous pardonnons à ceux qui nous ont offensés;  
ne nous laissez pas succomber à la tentation,  
mais délivrez-nous du mal.  
Ainsi soit-il.

Bons Esprits qui êtes les ministres de Dieu,  
assistez-nous dans l’épreuve présente.  
Anges gardiens, Esprits protecteurs,  
éclairez notre pensée, soutenez notre courage,  
écartez de nous les pensées mauvaises,  
et inspirez-nous ce qui est juste, prudent, charitable  
et conforme à la loi de Dieu.

Seigneur,  
nous te prions pour ce voyage.  
Que les bons Esprits accompagnent le chemin;  
qu’ils inspirent vigilance, patience et discernement;  
qu’ils écartent les imprudences, les troubles et les dangers,  
sans nuire à aucune créature visible ou invisible.  
S’il survient une difficulté,  
que ta lumière nous aide à la traverser avec calme,  
et que ce qui pourrait devenir péril soit changé en occasion de prudence,  
de secours mutuel et de confiance en ta bonté.

Au nom de Dieu tout-puissant,  
que les mauvais Esprits s’éloignent de ce chemin,  
et que les bons servent de rempart contre leurs suggestions.  
Bons Esprits, inspirez la force de résister à la peur,  
à l’impatience, à l’orgueil et à toute pensée mauvaise;  
faites naître en nous le désir sincère de nous corriger  
et d’agir avec justice envers tous.

Mon Dieu,  
nous prions aussi pour tous les voyageurs,  
pour ceux qui veillent sur les routes, les mers, les airs et les passages,  
pour les vivants exposés à l’inquiétude,  
et pour les Esprits souffrants qui peuvent recevoir quelque soulagement  
par une pensée fraternelle.  
Que la paix, la lumière et le progrès leur soient accordés  
selon ta sagesse et ta miséricorde.

Seigneur,  
ne permets pas que cette prière serve l’orgueil,  
l’intérêt égoïste, la curiosité frivole,  
ni la domination d’aucune créature visible ou invisible.  
Qu’elle soit seulement un acte de foi,  
de charité, de repentir, de prudence  
et de soumission à ta volonté.

Que le départ, le chemin et l’arrivée soient placés sous ta garde;  
que nous arrivions en paix, si cela est conforme à tes desseins,  
et que, quoi qu’il advienne, notre âme demeure tournée vers le bien.

Ainsi soit-il.

---

## Spiritualism / NSAC

Infinite Intelligence, God of love, law, and life,  
I come in reverence, in sincerity, and in personal responsibility,  
holding this journey and the prayer for safe, smooth travel before Thee.

Our Father which art in heaven,  
Hallowed be thy name.  
Thy kingdom come.  
Thy will be done in earth, as it is in heaven.  
Give us this day our daily bread.  
And forgive us our debts, as we forgive our debtors.  
And lead us not into temptation,  
but deliver us from evil:  
For thine is the kingdom, and the power, and the glory, for ever.  
Amen.

I affirm:  
We believe in Infinite Intelligence.  
We believe that the phenomena of Nature, both physical and spiritual,  
are the expression of Infinite Intelligence.  
We affirm that true religion is living in obedience to Nature's Laws.  
We affirm that the existence and personal identity of the individual  
continue after the change called death.  
We affirm that communication with the so-called dead is a fact,  
scientifically proven by the phenomena of Spiritualism.  
We affirm the highest morality contained in the Golden Rule:  
Therefore all things whatsoever ye would that men should do to you,  
do ye even so to them.  
We affirm moral responsibility, and that each soul makes its own happiness  
or unhappiness as it obeys or disobeys Nature's physical and spiritual laws.  
We affirm that the doorway to reformation is never closed  
against any soul here or hereafter.  
We affirm that the precepts of Prophecy and Healing are Divine attributes  
proven through Mediumship.

Infinite Intelligence,  
within Divine Law, truth, compassion, and the welfare of all concerned,  
let this journey be held in light.  
May the way be orderly, the timing be right, the mind be calm,  
and every step, road, vehicle, crossing, and arrival be guided by wisdom and care.  
Deliver us from evil, fear, deception, accident, confusion, and harm.  
Where there is danger, let it be avoided;  
where there is difficulty, let courage and clear judgment arise;  
where there is sudden change, let protection, patience, and right action be present.  
May all obstacles be removed without harm to any soul,  
and may this traveler arrive safely, peacefully, and in due order.

Let the words of my mouth, and the meditation of my heart,  
be acceptable in thy sight, O LORD, my strength, and my redeemer.

May no word spoken here replace conscience, responsibility, or truth.  
May no spirit, person, or influence be compelled.  
May all be governed by Infinite Intelligence, Divine Love, and Natural Law.

We now close every seeking of signs or messages,  
and return to the Lord’s Prayer, to quietness, to personal responsibility,  
and to obedience to Nature’s physical and spiritual laws.  
In silence, may peace settle over the mind, the road, and the destination.  
May right help be sought from wise and proper hands whenever it is needed.  
May Divine Love bless, guard, and uplift all concerned.

Amen.

---

## 瑟勒玛（Thelema）

Do what thou wilt shall be the whole of the Law.

Under the Law of Thelema, in the matter of safe passage and fortunate arrival, let this word be set in harmony with True Will.

ΑΠΟ ΠΑΝΤΟΣ ΚΑΚΟΔΑΙΜΟΝΟΣ.

ΣΟΙ, Ὦ ΦΑΛΛΕ, ἸΣΧΥΡΟΣ, ΕΥΧΑΡΙΣΤΟΣ, ΙΑΩ.

ΘΗΡΙΟΝ.

ΝΥΙΤ.

ΒΑΒΑΛΟΝ.

ΑΔΙΤ.

ΙΩ ΠΑΝ.

ΠΡΟ ΜΟΥ ΙΥΓΓΕΣ,  
ΟΠΙΣΩ ΜΟΥ ΤΕΛΕΤΑΡΧΑΙ,  
ΕΠΙ ΔΕΞΙΑ ΣΥΝΟΧΕΣ,  
ΕΠΑΡΙΣΤΕΡΑ ΔΑΙΜΟΝΕΣ,  
ΦΛΕΓΕΙ ΓΑΡ ΠΕΡΙ ΜΟΥ Ὁ ΑΣΤΗΡ ΤΩΝ ΠΕΝΤΕ,  
ΚΑΙ ΕΝ ΤΗΙ ΣΤΗΛΗΙ Ὁ ΑΣΤΗΡ ΤΩΝ ἙΞ ἙΣΤΗΚΕ.

Hail unto Thee who art Ra in Thy rising, even unto Thee who art Ra in Thy strength, who travellest over the Heavens in Thy bark at the Uprising of the Sun. Tahuti standeth in His splendour at the prow, and Ra-Hoor abideth at the helm. Hail unto Thee from the Abodes of Night!

Unity uttermost showed!  
I adore the might of Thy breath,  
Supreme and terrible God,  
Who makest the gods and death  
To tremble before Thee:—  
I, I adore thee!

Appear on the throne of Ra!  
Open the ways of the Khu!  
Lighten the ways of the Ka!  
The ways of the Khabs run through  
To stir me or still me!  
Aum! let it fill me!

Let the journey be ordered according to True Will: may the road be clear, the passage guarded, danger averted, peril transformed, hindrance dissolved, and arrival accomplished in peace, without restriction of another star.

ΑΠΟ ΠΑΝΤΟΣ ΚΑΚΟΔΑΙΜΟΝΟΣ.  
ΦΛΕΓΕΙ ΓΑΡ ΠΕΡΙ ΜΟΥ Ὁ ΑΣΤΗΡ ΤΩΝ ΠΕΝΤΕ,  
ΚΑΙ ΕΝ ΤΗΙ ΣΤΗΛΗΙ Ὁ ΑΣΤΗΡ ΤΩΝ ἙΞ ἙΣΤΗΚΕ.

Love is the law, love under will.

---

## 威卡 Alexandrian

I stand within the Circle, in perfect love and perfect trust.  
Let all within this rite be bounded by the Rede:  
An it harm none, do what ye will.

By Air, by Fire, by Water, by Earth,  
this Circle is cast and sealed.  
Between the worlds, and in the presence of the Mighty Ones,  
let this rite be held for safe passage, clear roads, protection from peril, and peaceful arrival.

Ye Lords of the Watchtowers of the East,  
powers of Air,  
I do summon, stir, and call you up,  
to witness and guard this rite.

Ye Lords of the Watchtowers of the South,  
powers of Fire,  
I do summon, stir, and call you up,  
to witness and guard this rite.

Ye Lords of the Watchtowers of the West,  
powers of Water,  
I do summon, stir, and call you up,  
to witness and guard this rite.

Ye Lords of the Watchtowers of the North,  
powers of Earth,  
I do summon, stir, and call you up,  
to witness and guard this rite.

O Great Mother,  
Lady of the Moon,  
Listen to the words of the Great Mother.  
Receive this prayer for a journey made in safety,  
with dangers turned aside, obstacles softened,  
and every crossing brought into peace.

O Horned One,  
Lord of the Greenwood,  
guardian of life, death, and return,  
Receive this prayer for strength upon the road,  
steady steps, wise timing, and safe arrival.

Eko Eko Azarak,  
Eko Eko Zomelak,  
Eko Eko Azarak,  
Eko Eko Zomelak.

For the road ahead,  
for every path, vehicle, station, crossing, and threshold,  
for protection from accident, confusion, delay, violence, mischance, and fear,  
within right will, right boundary, and harm to none,  
let the prayer be shaped in truth.

May all peril be averted without harm to any being.  
May what is difficult become passable.  
May what is dangerous be seen in time and wisely avoided.  
May help arise where help is needed.  
May the journey be smooth, guarded, and complete.  
May peace be at the departure, peace upon the way, and peace at the arrival.

So mote it be.

Ye Lords of the Watchtowers of the North,  
powers of Earth,  
I thank you for witnessing and guarding this rite.  
Hail and farewell.

Ye Lords of the Watchtowers of the West,  
powers of Water,  
I thank you for witnessing and guarding this rite.  
Hail and farewell.

Ye Lords of the Watchtowers of the South,  
powers of Fire,  
I thank you for witnessing and guarding this rite.  
Hail and farewell.

Ye Lords of the Watchtowers of the East,  
powers of Air,  
I thank you for witnessing and guarding this rite.  
Hail and farewell.

The Circle is open, but unbroken.  
Merry meet, merry part, and merry meet again.

Blessed be.

If any word, will, or working has strayed beyond right boundary,  
let it be stilled, cleansed, and returned to the Earth.  
Let no force here bind, compel, injure, or trouble any being.  
By the Rede, by perfect love and perfect trust:  
An it harm none.

So mote it be.

---

## 威卡 Dianic

By earth and moon, by breath and flame,  
this place is made sacred.

I cast this circle as a boundary of truth,  
a circle of protection,  
a circle of blessing,  
a circle of the Goddess.

Guarded be the path before me,  
guarded be the path behind me,  
guarded be the road beneath my feet,  
guarded be the sky above my head.

O Diana,  
Bright Lady of the Moon,  
Mother of the wild places,  
Keeper of women’s mysteries,  
be present in this circle.

I name the matter of this rite:  
may travel be safe and smooth;  
may the journey be free from danger and hardship;  
may peril be turned aside;  
may all difficulty be transformed into safety;  
may the destination be reached in peace.

Let this prayer touch only what may be touched in freedom.  
Let it bind no unwilling heart.  
Let it cross no oath-bound door.  
Let it harm none.

O Diana,  
shine your moonlight upon the road.

Where there is fear, let there be clear boundary.  
Where there is confusion, let there be inner knowing.  
Where there is danger, let there be warning and protection.  
Where there is delay, let there be patience and right timing.  
Where there is accident, let there be turning away.  
Where there is uncertainty, let there be calm passage.

All acts of love and pleasure are my rituals.

I place within this circle my breath, my attention, and my honest goodwill.  
I dedicate this prayer to safe passage, clear sight, steady steps, and peaceful arrival.

By the waxing, full, and waning Moon,  
by the dark and returning Moon,  
may what is true be strengthened,  
may what is harmful be dissolved,  
may what belongs to the journey arrive in peace,  
may what does not belong depart in peace.

For safe travel, protection on the way, and peaceful arrival,  
I ask blessing, clarity, and right unfolding.

An it harm none, do what ye will.

O Diana,  
I thank you for your presence.  
Remain if you will,  
depart if you must,  
with blessing between us.

The circle is open,  
but unbroken.  
Merry meet,  
merry part,  
and merry meet again.

In freedom, not force;  
in blessing, not binding;  
in protection, not harm;  
within the clear boundary of the Goddess,  
may this rite be sealed in peace.

---

## 巴斯克 Sorginak 复兴

Ni naiz bidean doan ahotsa.  
Hitz hau nire ahoan, arnasa nire bularrean, lurra nire oinen azpian.

Agur, Mari Anbotoko Dama.  
Agur, Lurraren bihotzeko andrea.  
Entzun nire hitza, entzun nire arnasa.

Sasi guztien gainetik eta laino guztien azpitik.  
Gezurra behera, egia gora.  
Iluna behera, argia gora.

Nire eskaria hau da:  
Bidea bakez ireki dadila.  
Urrats bakoitza argiz zaindua izan dadila.  
Arriskua urrundu dadila, kaltea desegin dadila, nahasmendua bare dadila.  
Zailtasuna etortzen bada, on bihur dadila;  
beldurra haizeak eraman dezala;  
bidaiaren amaiera seguru eta oso irits dadila.

Bidearen inguruan,  
ibilaldiaren inguruan,  
irteeraren eta iritsieraren inguruan,  
lotura gaiztoa askatu dadila,  
bidea garbi ager dadila,  
hitza zuzen gera dadila.

Eguzki amandrea, argitu bidea.  
Ilargi amandrea, gorde isila.  
Lurra, hartu mina.  
Haizea, eraman beldurra.  
Ura, garbitu aztarna.  
Sua, piztu indarra.

Ez dut kalterik nahi.  
Ez dut inor behartu nahi.  
Ez dut gezurrik zin egiten.  
Ez dut sorgin izena gaizki erabiltzen.  
Ez dut inoren bidea itxi nahi; nire bidea bakez zabal dadila.

Mari Anbotoko Dama,  
nire hitza entzuna izan dadila,  
nire muga gordea izan dadila,  
nire bidea argitua izan dadila.

Kalterik gabe, gezurrik gabe, behartzerik gabe.  
Arnasa garbi, oinak sendo, bihotza bare.  
Lurrak eutsi, urak garbitu, haizeak arindu, suak indartu.  
Sasi guztien gainetik eta laino guztien azpitik.  
Gezurra behera, egia gora.  
Hala bedi.

---

## 威卡 Gardnerian

In this place, in this hour, we stand between the worlds,  
with clean hands, clear speech, and a will held in Perfect Love and Perfect Trust.

I conjure thee, O Circle of Power,  
that thou beest a boundary between the world of men and the realms of the Mighty Ones,  
a guardian and a meeting-place for this working of protection upon the road.

Lady of the Moon,  
Great Mother, Bright One, Queen of the secret place,  
hear the words spoken within this circle.

Whenever ye have need of anything,  
once in the month, and better it be when the moon is full,  
then shall ye assemble in some desert place,  
or in a forest all together join  
to adore the potent spirit of your queen.

Horned One,  
Lord of the wildwood, keeper of life and death,  
stand apart in thy own power and witness this working.

Before the Lady we speak the need:  
may this journey be safe and smooth;  
may the road be clear, the way be fortunate,  
danger turned aside, hardship softened,  
and every peril changed into a path of deliverance.

Before the Lord we speak the boundary:  
let this protection harm none, bind none, compel none,  
and take nothing from the freedom, blessing, or rightful way of any living being.

Let this prayer be for safe departure, safe passage, and safe arrival,  
harming none, binding none against the true will,  
and turning aside all falsehood, fear, and ill-wrought force.

Eko, Eko, Azarak,  
Eko, Eko, Zomelak.

By earth, let the feet be steady and the road be firm.  
By air, let the mind be clear and the signs be rightly known.  
By fire, let courage be kindled without rashness or harm.  
By water, let the way flow in peace until safe arrival.

Lady of the Moon, receive this prayer.  
Horned One, witness this prayer.  
Mighty Ones of the circle, keep it within right measure.

As the cup and the bread are blessed in fellowship,  
so may the work be whole:  
for protection in travel,  
for a road without calamity,  
for danger transformed and peace at the journey’s end.

What is raised in love, let it be grounded in peace.  
What is not needed, let it fall away without harm.  
May this working remain within right measure, free of coercion, free of pride, and clean of ill intent.

The Lady be thanked.  
The Horned One be thanked.  
The Mighty Ones be thanked.  
The circle is open, yet unbroken.  
Merry meet, and merry part, and merry meet again.

---

## Dievturība（拉脱维亚）

Dievs, Dieviņ, labais devēj,  
stāv pie mana ceļa,  
stāv pie mana soļa,  
stāv pie drošas aiziešanas un mierīgas pārnākšanas.

Dievs, dod man kalnā kāpt,  
Ne no kalna lejiņā;  
Dievs, dod man otram dot,  
Ne no otra mīļi lūgt.

Par šo ceļu es saku taisnu vārdu:  
lai mana doma ir skaidra,  
lai mans darbs ir godīgs,  
lai mans ceļš ir taisns,  
lai mana roka nedara pāri nevienam.  
Lai ceļā nav briesmu un nelaimes,  
lai grūtums top viegls,  
lai šķērslis paiet sāņus,  
lai aiziešana ir mierīga,  
lai nonākšana ir droša.

Dod, Dieviņi, otram dot,  
Ne no otra mīļi lūgt;  
Otram devu, sev palika,  
Savu mūžu dzīvojot.

Dievs, Dieviņ, labais devēj,  
pieņem šo vārdu par manu ceļu,  
pieņem šo dainu par drošu nonākšanu.

Lai šis vārds paliek dainā un tikumā,  
bez ļauna vēlējuma, bez spaida, bez asins, bez sveša vārda.  
Lai top.

---

## 威卡 Eclectic

I stand within the circle between the worlds,  
in perfect love and perfect trust,  
for protection in travel: safe passage, freedom from peril and hardship, the turning aside of danger, and peaceful arrival.

By earth and sea and sky,  
let this circle be cast and sealed.  
What enters here shall enter in truth;  
what leaves here shall leave in peace.

Guardians of the Watchtowers of the East, powers of Air,  
I do summon, stir, and call you up,  
to witness this rite of protection for the road ahead.

Guardians of the Watchtowers of the South, powers of Fire,  
I do summon, stir, and call you up,  
to witness this rite of protection for the road ahead.

Guardians of the Watchtowers of the West, powers of Water,  
I do summon, stir, and call you up,  
to witness this rite of protection for the road ahead.

Guardians of the Watchtowers of the North, powers of Earth,  
I do summon, stir, and call you up,  
to witness this rite of protection for the road ahead.

Great Mother,  
Listen to the words of the Great Mother,  
who of old was called Artemis, Astarte, Dione, Melusine,  
Aphrodite, Cerridwen, Diana, Arionrhod, Brigid, and by many other names.  
All acts of love and pleasure are my rituals.  
Be present to this prayer of protection and safe arrival.

Horned One,  
Lord of the wildwood, keeper of life, death, and return,  
be present to this prayer of protection and safe arrival.

An it harm none, do what ye will.

Therefore I speak only within willing, rightful, and harmless bounds:  
May the journey be peaceful and well-guided.  
May the path be clear, the timing be fortunate, and the way be free from danger.  
May accidents, confusion, delay, malice, and mischance be turned aside without harm to any being.  
May every crossing, road, station, vehicle, threshold, and resting place be guarded in right measure.  
May danger be transformed into safety, difficulty into passage, and uncertainty into clear guidance.  
May the traveler arrive safely, smoothly, and in peace.

Let no will be bound.  
Let no heart be compelled.  
Let no life be diminished.  
Let what is not mine return to its own place.  
Let what is mine stand clear in truth.

Eko Eko Azarak,  
Eko Eko Zomelak,  
Eko Eko Azarak,  
Eko Eko Zomelak.

For this journey,  
may the crooked be made clear,  
may the harmful be made harmless,  
may the hidden be known in right measure,  
may the needed path open without coercion.

If any word of this rite has exceeded rightful boundary,  
I withdraw it now.  
If any force has been called beyond consent,  
I release it now.  
If any bond has been made against true will,  
I unmake it now.  
Peace to all beings touched by this prayer.

Great Mother, I thank you and release you.  
Go if you must, stay if you will.  
Hail and farewell.

Horned One, I thank you and release you.  
Go if you must, stay if you will.  
Hail and farewell.

Guardians of the Watchtowers of the North, powers of Earth,  
I thank you and release you.  
Hail and farewell.

Guardians of the Watchtowers of the West, powers of Water,  
I thank you and release you.  
Hail and farewell.

Guardians of the Watchtowers of the South, powers of Fire,  
I thank you and release you.  
Hail and farewell.

Guardians of the Watchtowers of the East, powers of Air,  
I thank you and release you.  
Hail and farewell.

The circle is open, but unbroken.  
Merry meet, merry part, and merry meet again.  
So mote it be.

---

## 匈牙利 Ősmagyar Vallás

Istenem, Magyarok Istene,  
hallgasd meg e tiszta szót.

Őseim, apáim és anyáim,  
kik előttem jártatok,  
álljatok mögém tiszta emlékezettel,  
ne ártással, ne haraggal,  
hanem áldással.

Áldjon meg az Isten,  
őrizzen meg az Isten,  
fordítsa jóra az útnak dolgát.  
Adjon Isten jó utat,  
nyitott kaput előre,  
békességet hátra,  
jó társat mellé,  
tiszta eget fölé.

Isten oltalma legyen az úton,  
ősök emlékezete legyen a hát mögött,  
rossz szó, rossz szem, rossz szándék  
ne találjon fogást.  
A kerék forduljon rendben,  
a lépés essék biztosan,  
az ösvény legyen világos,  
a veszedelem térjen el,  
a baj változzék jóra,  
és az érkezés legyen békés.

Ami ártó szó,  
ami rossz kötés,  
ami nem igaz rend szerint tapad az út köré,  
az oldódjék el,  
menjen vissza a semmibe,  
ne bántson senkit,  
ne térjen ártással.

Nem kérek ártást,  
nem kívánok bajt senkire,  
nem mondok hamis esküt,  
nem gyalázom az ősöket,  
nem töröm meg a kenyeret haraggal,  
nem szennyezem a tüzet rossz szóval,  
nem keverek idegen szent nevet e magyar áldás rendjébe.

Hála legyen az Istennek,  
hála az ősök tiszta emlékezetének,  
hála a földnek, mely hordoz,  
a víznek, mely tisztít,  
a tűznek, mely világít,  
és a kenyérnek, mely életet tart.

Áldás legyen az induláson,  
áldás legyen az úton,  
áldás legyen a hazatérésen vagy megérkezésen,  
áldás legyen azon, ami igaz és tiszta.

Úgy legyen.  
Áldás, békesség.

---

## Heathenry / Ásatrú

Friðr sé hér.  
Helga ek þenna stað til fríðar ok sannra orða.

Ek kalla á Þórr,  
Véurr, vinr manna,  
heyr orð mín.

Heill dagr, heilir dags synir,  
heil nótt ok nipt!  
Óreiðum augum lítið okkr þinig,  
ok gefið sitjendum sigr.

Heilir æsir, heilar ásynjur,  
heil sjá in fjölnýta fold!  
Mál ok manvit gefið okkr mærum tveim  
ok læknishendr, meðan lifum.

Ek ber fram lof, minning ok góð orð.  
Ek bið um heila ferð, greiðan veg,  
engan vá, engan háska, enga nauð,  
ok at hverr háski snúisk frá meini til heilla.  
Lát ferðamenn koma heilum fæti,  
með heilum hug, heilum orðum, heilum verkum,  
ok ná áfangastað í friði.

Sigrúnar skaltu kunna,  
ef þú vilt sigr hafa,  
ok rísta á hjalti hjörs.

Brimrúnar skaltu kunna,  
ef þú vilt borgit hafa  
á sundi seglmörum.

Þórr, halt hamri þínum yfir vegi,  
ver frá slysum, villu, ofviðri ok ófriði.  
Lát hjól, fót, skip eða vagn ganga rétt,  
lát augu vaka, hendur stýra,  
ok hjarta standa stöðugt innan frithar.

Ek geri eigi níð.  
Ek bind eigi vilja annars.  
Ek sver eigi ósannan eið.  
Orð mín standi innan frithar.

Þórr, tak við loforðum þessum.  
Gef heila ferð ok friðsæla komu,  
ef það er rétt, heilt ok innan frithar.

Svá sé.  
Friðr með oss.

---

## 凯尔特德鲁伊（OBOD / ADF / AODA）

[净化与定界]  
Â dŵr glân, ag anadl da, gosodir cylch heddwch.  
Awen, Awen, Awen.

[向土地与三界致敬]  
Anrhydedd i bridd y lle hwn, i ddŵr y lle hwn, i wynt y lle hwn, ac i dân y lle hwn.  
Anrhydedd i’r byd uchaf, i’r byd canol, ac i’r byd isaf.  
Anrhydedd i ysbrydion y lle, yn heddychlon ac yn gyfiawn.

[陈明目的]  
Amcan y weddi hon yw taith ddiogel, esmwyth, a bendigaid:  
boed y ffordd heb niwed, heb ddamwain, heb rwystrau dinistriol;  
boed pob perygl yn troi’n ffordd glir, a boed cyrraedd mewn heddwch.  
Ni cheisir niwed i neb, na gorfodi ewyllys neb,  
na thorri cydbwysedd y tir, y bodau byw, na’r gymuned.

[分别致敬土地灵、祖灵、Awen]  
Ysbrydion y lle, derbyniwch y parch hwn.  
Hynafiaid anrhydeddus, rhai a fu o’n blaenau, tystiwch y weddi hon.  
Awen, Awen, Awen.  
Awen, Awen, Awen.  
Awen, Awen, Awen.

[正行：Gweddi’r Derwydd]  
Dyro, Dduw, dy nawdd;  
Ac yn nawdd, nerth;  
Ac yn nerth, deall;  
Ac yn neall, gwybod;  
Ac yngwybod, gwybod y cyfiawn;  
Ac yngwybod y cyfiawn, ei garu;  
Ac o garu, caru pob hanfod;  
Ac ymhob hanfod, caru Duw;  
Duw a phob daioni.

[供献与请求]  
Boed nawdd ar y daith hon.
